CHAPTER I. GENERAL PROVISIONS 

§1. Purpose 

The  purpose  of  these  Enforcement  Rules  is  to  stipulate  the  matters  necessary  for  the 
enforcement of the KOSPI Market Business Regulation (hereinafter referred to as "the 
Regulation")  of  the  Korea  Exchange  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  Exchange”). 
(Amended on July 16, 2009) 

§2. Definitions 

The meanings of terms used in these Enforcement Rules shall be as follows: (Amended 
on April 12, 2023) 

1.  “KOSPI 200” refers to a market capitalization weighted stock price index based 
on 200 issues listed on the KOSPI Market, which is calculated by the Exchange 
using base index of one hundred (100) points on the base date of January 3, 1990. 

2.  “Sector index” refers to an index calculated by each industry or type for the stocks 

listed on the KOSPI Market. 

3.  “Issue using the first trading price as the base price” refers to an issue whose the 
first  trading  price  determined  in  accordance  with  [§37(1)]  of  the  Regulation 
becomes  the  base  price  of  the  day  within  the  range  of  quotations  within  the 
minimum  and  the  maximum  quotation  price  noted  in  [Annex  1],  and  it  is 
classified as follows: 

(a) Relisted issue and issue with listing change;   

(b)  Issue  whose  amount  of  distribution  or  dividend  per  share  reported  to  the 
Exchange exceeds the price limit range on the day before two (2) trading days of 
the  record  date  noted  in  [§132(1)],  as  stocks  issued  by  investment  companies 
(hereinafter referred to as “investment company stocks”) under Article 9(18)2 of 
the Financial Investment Services and Capital Markets Act (hereinafter referred 
to as the “Act”), stocks of real estate investment companies under the Real Estate 
Investment  Company  Act,  and  stocks  of  ship  investment  companies  under  the 
Ship Investment Company Act; 

(c) Issue whose paid-in capital is reduced [refers to the case where paid-in capital 
amount is reduced according to reverse stock split or stock retirement of stocks 
held by minority shareholders (refers to minority shareholders noted in [§2(19)] 
of the KOSPI Market Disclosure Regulation; the same hereinafter)]; 

(d) ETN security that is underwent the reverse stock split or stock split; and 

(e) Issue that resumes trading after trading has been halted or suspended for thirty 
(30) trading days or more. 

12 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
4.  “Relisted  issue”  refers  to  stocks  (including  class  stocks)  that  are  re-listed  in 
accordance with [§42] of the KOSPI Market Listing Regulation, as stocks issued 

by  corporations  incorporated  according  to  merger  between  corporations  and 

stock-listed  corporations  established  by  merger  or  merger  after  split-off  of 

delisted corporations or stock-listed corporations. 

5.  “Issue  with  listing  change”  refers  to  stocks  that  are  issued  by  a  corporation 
(excluding corporations surviving after carving out noted in Article 530-12 of the 

Commercial Act) surviving after split-off or merger after split-off of a stock-listed 

corporations. 

6.  “Issue  listed  after  merger”  refers  to  stocks  that  are  issued  by  a  corporation 
incorporated  according  to  the  merger  between  a  special  purpose  acquisition 

company  noted  in  [§2(1)25]  of  the  KOSPI  Market  Listing  Regulation  and  a 

corporation that has not listed its stocks on the stock market, and that are listed in 

accordance with [§76-2] of the KOSPI Market Listing Regulation.   

[Wholly amended on March 12, 2021] 

§3. Prices of Immediately Executable Limit Quotations 

“A price set by the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(4)4] of the Regulation shall refer to each 
of the following prices: (February 27, 2025) 

1. In the case of immediately executable offer limit quotation   

The highest bid price (excluding a bid quotation submitted as a mid-price quotation; 
the same hereinafter in this Article) at the time of receipt of the relevant offer quotation. 
Provided that, in cases where there are no bid quotations, it shall be the price (the lower 
limit  price  shall  be  the  minimum)  which  is  one  quotation  price  unit  lower  than  the 
lowest offer (excluding an offer quotation submitted as a mid-price quotation; the same 
hereinafter in this Article), and in cases where there is no bid or offer quotation, it shall 
be the most recent price (if the price does not match the quotation price unit, it shall be 
the price closest to that price among the prices that are lower than that price and match 
the quotation price unit). (February 27, 2025) 

2. In the case of immediately executable bid limit quotation   

The lowest offer price at the time of receipt of the relevant bid quotation. Provided that, 
in cases where there are no offer quotations, it shall be the price which is one quotation 
price unit higher than the highest bid price (the upper limit price shall be the maximum), 

13 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
and in cases where there is no bid or offer, it shall be the most recent price (if this price 
does not match the quotation price unit, it shall be the price closest to that price among 
the prices that are higher than that price and match the quotation price unit). (February 
27, 2025) 

§4. Prices of Best Limit Quotations 

“A price set by the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(4)5] of the Regulation shall refer to each 
of the following prices: (February 27, 2025) 

1. In the case of best limit offer quotations 

The lowest offer price (excluding an offer quotation submitted as a mid-price quotation; 
the same hereinafter in this Article) at the time when the relevant offer quotation is 
received.  Provided that,  in  cases where there  are no offer quotations, it shall be the 
most recent price (if this price does not match the quotation price unit, it shall be the 
price closest to that price among the prices that are higher than that price and match the 
quotation price unit). (February 27, 2025) 

2. In the case of best limit bid quotations 

The highest bid price (excluding a bid quotation submitted as a mid-price quotation; 
the  same  hereinafter  in  this  Article)  at  the  time  when  the  relevant  bid  quotation  is 
received. Provided that, in cases where there are no bid quotations, it shall be the most 
recent price (if this price does not match the quotation price unit, it shall be the price 
closest  to  that  price  among  the  prices  that  are  lower  than  that  price  and  match  the 
quotation price unit). (February 27, 2025) 

§4-2. Prices of Mid-price Quotations 

The “price set by the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(4)7] of the Regulation shall refer to the 
simple arithmetic average of the best offer quotation price and the best bid quotation price 
at the time of continuous auction (anything less than KRW 1 is rounded down; hereinafter 
referred to as “mid-price”). 

[February 27, 2025] 

§4-3. Conditions for Stop-limit Quotation to Trigger into Limit Quotation 

The “conditions set by the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(4)8] of the Regulation shall refer 
to conditions in each of the followings: 

1. In the case of stop-limit sell quotations 

    The previous transaction price (if there is no previous transaction price, the base price 
is used; the same hereinafter in this Article) shall be equal to or lower than the stop 
price noted in [§2(4)8] of the Regulation (hereinafter referred to as the “stop price”). 

14 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2. In the case of stop-limit buy quotations 

    The previous transaction price shall be equal to or higher than the stop price. 

[February 27, 2025] 

§5. [Deleted on July 11, 2019] 

§6. [Deleted on July 11, 2019] 

§6-2. [Deleted on July 29, 2010] 

§6-3. Issue for Which Special Quotation Price is Not Recognized 

The “criteria specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(9)] of the Regulation shall refer 
to the case where the base price of different classes of stocks (referring to the stocks that 
are not common stocks) on the day is one point five (1.5) times or more of the base price 
of the relevant common share. (Amended on April 20, 2012; September 22, 2020) 

[December 30, 2009] 

§6-4. Index Arbitrage Trades 

(1) “An index specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(21)1] of the Regulation shall 
refer to an index falling under any of the following subparagraphs (hereinafter referred to 
as “index for index arbitrage trading”): (Amended on July 11, 2019) 

1. KOSPI 200; and 

2. KRX 300(referring to a market capitalization weighted stock price index based on 
300 issues, from among the stocks listed on the KOSPI Market and the stocks listed 
on the KOSDAQ Market, which is calculated by the Exchange using the base index of 
1,000 on the base date of January 4, 2010; the same hereinafter). 

(2) “A form set by the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(21)1] of the Regulation shall refer to 
any of the following subparagraphs: 

1. A trade in  which the  sale  (including the final  settlement  of a buying  contract) of 
futures contracts on an index for index arbitrage trading (including synthetic stock price 
index futures) is conducted at the same time or immediately after/before the purchase 
of a basket of stocks linked to the same index (hereinafter referred to as “a basket of 
stocks” in this Article); and   

2. A trade in which the purchase (including the final settlement of a selling contract) 
of futures contracts on the same index (including synthetic stock price index futures) 

15 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
is conducted at the same time or immediately after/before the sale of a basket of stocks.   

(3) The "sale of synthetic stock price index futures" in paragraph (2) shall refer to buying 
of  put  options  while  selling  call  options  in  trading  of  options  on  an  index  for  index 
arbitrage trading of the index options markets noted in [§3(2)1] of the Derivatives Market 
Business Regulation (hereinafter referred to as the “trading of index options”), and the 
"purchase of synthetic stock price index futures" shall refer to selling of put options while 
buying call options in the trading of index options.   

(4) The  “purchase” or “sale” in  paragraph (2) shall include the cases of purchasing  or 
selling after splitting an order into two (2) or more smaller ones. 

[December 6, 2018] 

§6-5. Non-arbitrage Trades 

(1)  The  “identical  person  who  is  within  the  scope  set  by  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in 
[§2(21)2] of the Regulation shall be classified based on the trust assets of each fund and 
the proprietary assets. 

(2) “A specific number set forth in the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(21)2] of the Regulation 
shall  refer  to  fifteen  (15)  [calculated  including  cases  of  transactions  at  a  multilateral 
trading  company  pursuant  to  Article  8-2  (5)  of  the  Act  (hereinafter  referred  to  as 
“multilateral trading company”)]. In such cases, the number of stocks shall be calculated 
for each of buy and sell. (Amended on January 24, 2019; February 27, 2025) 

(3)  Notwithstanding  paragraphs  (1)  and  (2),  none  of  the  quotations  noted  in  each  the 
following subparagraphs shall be deemed to be the quotations for non-arbitrage trading. 
[January 24, 2019] 

1. Liquidity providing quotations under [§12(1)23]; 

2. Quotations placed through the market-making accounts under [§12(1)16d]; and 

3. Quotations under item (j) through (m) of [§12(1)19]. Provided that, in the case of 
item (m), this shall not apply to the case where it is otherwise specified in the market-
making agreement. 

[December 6, 2018] 

§6-6. Exceptions of Algorithmic Trades 

The “securities stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(22)] of the Regulation shall 
refer to debt securities.   

16 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§7. Fiction in Application 

(1) [Deleted on September 10, 2019] 

(2)  In applying  these Enforcement  Rules, the provisions on debt  securities shall apply 
mutatis  mutandis to  the beneficiary  certificates  that  are  applied  with  the  provisions  of 
[§111]  of  the  KOSPI  Market  Listing  Regulation.  (Amended  on  February  3,  2009; 
September 20, 2012; May 13, 2013) 

(3) [Deleted on September 2, 2014] 

CHAPTER II. MARKET OPERATION 

Section 1. Division of the Market and Opening and Closing Thereof 

§8. Change of Trading Hours 

(1) The Exchange may, pursuant to the proviso to [§4(3)] of the Regulation, temporarily 
change the trading hours in any of the following cases: (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

1. In the cases of failures of the Exchange’s computer systems, member’s computer 
systems and other computer systems that are known to perform similar tasks thereof 
(refers  to  the  situation  where  the  computer  systems  fail  to  operate  normally  for  a 
specific period of time or longer, indicating that orderly execution of trades would be 
difficult; hereinafter referred to as “the computer system failure”);   

2.  In  cases  where  a  computer  system  failure  has  occurred  or  excessive  number  of 
quotations is submitted for selective issues, the Exchange may change the trading hours 
for such issues;   

3. In case of the first trading day of the year; and   

4. Additionally, the cases where change of trading hour is deemed necessary.   

(2) The failure of member’s computer system mentioned in paragraph (1)1 shall refer to 
the  case  where  the  fact  of  falling  under  any  of  the  following  subparagraphs  has  been 
confirmed: (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 18, 2013; August 24, 2017) 

1. In the case of the securities other than debt securities, when the sum of the trading 
volume of the members who are experiencing a computer system failure (referring to 
the  cases  where  members  are  unable  to  transmit  quotations  to  the  Market  via  the 
member’s computer system, but excluding computer system failures that are limited to 
specific offices of the members or specific regions; the same hereinafter) amounts to 
or exceed 75/100 of the total trading volume (which is on the basis of total volume of 

17 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
trades executed during the one (1) year period retroactive from the last day of the month 
preceding  the  month  which  includes  the  date  the  system  failure  occurred  and  is 
calculated taking into account the cases of admission of new members as well as the 
membership withdrawal; the same hereinafter) of the members suffering from system 
failure. Provided that, even in the event where the sum of the trading volume of the 
members who are experiencing a computer system failure falls below 75/100 of the 
total trading volume, the Exchange may construe it as the system failure of members 
referred  to  in  paragraph  (1)1  when  deemed  necessary  given  the  market  conditions 
specified in each of the following items: 

(a) In cases where the sum of trading volume of the members who have computer 
systems  failure  in  the  KOSDAQ  market  amounts  to  or  exceed  75%  of  the  total 
trading volume of the KOSDAQ market; and 

(b)In  cases  where  normal  operation  of  the  market  is  difficult  due  to  the  failure 
occurred to each member system. 

2. In the case of debt securities, when the sum of the trading volume of the members 
of which computer systems have failed for each trading under each subparagraph of 
[§71-3(2)] of the Regulation is 75% or more of the sum of the trading volume of total 
members. Provided that, in cases where the Exchange deems that normal operation of 
the market is difficult due to the system failure of each member, it may be regarded as 
the system failure under paragraph (1)1.   

(3)  In  principle,  the  change  of  trading  hours  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1)1  shall  be  the 
successive extension of trading hours by the duration of a computer system failure from 
the  time  the  computer  system  is  back  in  full  operation.  Provided  that,  in  the  case  of 
extension of the closing hour of regular session (hereinafter referred to as "the market 
closing"), the Exchange may extend it until the time it deems necessary. (Amended on 
February 3, 2009) 

(4) Notwithstanding paragraph (3), in case of debt securities, the Exchange may not, when 
it changes the trading hours pursuant to paragraph (1), extend the closing time. (Amended 
on February 3, 2009) 

(5) With respect to the trading hours of  a regular session after the computer system is 
fully recovered from the failure, the Exchange may change it to the hours after letting a 
certain  period  of  time  elapse  from  the  time  of  system  recovery,  while  taking  into  the 
consideration such factors as the operating conditions of the Exchange computer systems 
and member’s computer systems, and quotation conditions.   

(6)  In  cases  where  the  trading  after  a  temporary  suspension  pursuant  to  [§6]  of  the 
Regulation  is  resumed  during  the  last  ten  (10)  minutes  before  the  closing  hour  of  the 
regular session, the Exchange shall extend the trading hour by more than ten (10) minutes 
after the trading resumption. Provided that these provisions may not apply to the trading 
of debt securities. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

18 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Section 2. Types of Trades 

§9. Designation of Types of Trades 

(1) “Case stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§7(1)2] of the Regulation shall refer 
to the case where the settlement date noted in paragraph (2)1 is the due date for holding 
reserve (if the relevant date is a  market holiday, it shall be the immediately preceding 
trading day; hereinafter referred to as "the due date for holding reserve"), which is set by 
the Bank of Korea. (Amended on December 30, 2011; October 29, 2024)     

(2) Pursuant to [§7(4)] of the Regulation, the types of debt securities trades shall be as 
follows; (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 30, 2011) 

1. Trading in the KRX KTB under subparagraph 3 of [§55] of the Regulation: Next 
day settlement trade.   

2. Trading of debt securities other than the trades noted in subparagraph 1: Same day 
settlement trade.   

(3) As a case of stock trading referred to in [§39(4)1&2] of the Regulation pursuant to 
[§7(4)] of the Regulation, when a bid quotation and an offer quotation are submitted by a 
same member {in the case of a member is given multiple ID numbers pursuant to [§12(3)], 
they shall be limited to the quotations placed by the same ID number; the same hereinafter 
in  [§52(2)]  and  [§53(2)]}  and  the  relevant  member  has  submitted  to  the  Exchange  a 
written application for the same day settlement trade in accordance with [Annex: Form 
No. 1] three (3) days before placing the quotations, the Exchange shall designate such 
trade as the same day settlement trade, if it is deemed necessary. (Amended on July 7, 
2006; March 19, 2009)   

(4) Pursuant to [§7(4)] of the Regulation, the trades that the Exchange conducts for the 
buy-in  in  accordance  with  [§22]  of  the  Securities  Market  Clearing  and  Settlement 
Business Regulation shall be designated as the same day settlement trade. [December 30, 
2011; February 27, 2025] 

§9-2. Guideline for Connection to Member system, etc. 

(1) “Matters stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in  [§8-2(1)] of the Regulation  shall 
refer to each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on February 28, 2014) 

1. Methods of network connection between the Exchange and members;   

2. Methods of requesting and allotting the communication lines between the Exchange 
and members, and the sessions;     

3. Specifications of security devices under [§82(2)] of the Regulation; 

19 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
4. Guidelines for allocation and operation of sessions of members; and 

5.  Other  matters  that  the  Exchange  deems  necessary  for  the  efficient  and  reliable 
operation of the system. 

(2) “Communication lines” in paragraph (1) shall refer to the physical circuits used in 
transmitting  and  receiving  quotations  and  trade  details  between  members  and  the 
Exchange,  and  “sessions”  shall  refer  to  the  logical  circuits  that  transmit  and  receive 
quotations and trade details between members and the Exchange. (Amended on February 
28, 2014) 

[December 28, 2011] 

Section 3. Quotations 

§9-3. Collective Quoting of Details of Orders relating to Multiple Accounts 

(1) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§9(1)] of the Regulation 
shall refer to the cases falling under any of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on 
February  3,  2009;  September  20,  2012;  September  10,  2019;  November  23,  2023; 
December 4, 2023) 

1.  Case  where  a  member  engaged  in  the  discretionary  investment  business  submits 
quotations using an account in its own name upon receiving entrustment of orders in 
order to manage individual discretionary investment property efficiently pursuant to 
Article 99(2)4 of the Enforcement  Decree of the  Financial  Investment  Services  and 
Capital Markets Act (hereinafter referred to as “the Enforcement Decree of the Act”). 
In such cases, the person responsible for the discretionary investment business shall be 
clearly noticeable;   

1-2. Case where a member engaged in the trust business submits the quotations using 
an account in its own name upon receiving entrustment of orders in order to manage 
individual trust property (excluding trust property intending to acquire or dispose the 
treasury stocks) efficiently pursuant to Article 109(1)5 of the Enforcement Decree of 
the  Act.  In  such  cases,  the  person  in  charge  of  the  trust  business  shall  be  clearly 
noticeable  and  a  member  who  intends  to  submit  quotations  for  debt  securities  shall 
report this to the Exchange in advance;   

2.  Case  of  submitting  quotations  based  on  the  order  details  using  an  account  in  the 
name  of  a  foreign  financial  investment  company  or  a  representative  investor  or  an 
account  in  the  name  of  an  investment  broker  to  manage  the  investment  of  foreign 
investor groups prescribed in the Regulations on Financial Investment Business;   

3.  Additionally,  cases  where,  according  to  the  relevant  laws  and  regulations,  it  is 
deemed necessary to quote order details using an account in investment broker’s name.   

20 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) When quoting order details relating to multiple accounts pursuant to paragraph (1), 
each member shall use a separate account. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

[August 28, 2007] 

§10. Types of Quotations 

(1)  The  types  of  quotations  that  the  members  can  place  for  each  class  of  securities 
pursuant  to  [§9(2)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  as  noted  in  each  of  the  following 
subparagraphs: (Amended on August 26, 2005; February 3, 2009; 2010; July 16, 2009; 
July 29, 2010; September 2, 2014; February 27, 2025) 

1. For stocks (excluding the stocks of ETF investment companies; the same hereinafter), 
DRs  of  foreign  stocks,  collective  investment  securities  of  ETFs  and  ETNs:  Limit 
quotation,  market  quotation, 
immediately 
executable limit quotation, best limit quotation, quotation for auction-based block trade, 
mid-price quotation, and stop-limit quotation; and (February 27, 2025) 

limit-to-market-on-close  quotation, 

2.  For  subscription  right  certificates,  subscription  warrants,  equity  linked  warrants 
(ELWs),  beneficiary  certificates  (excluding  the  beneficiary  certificates  of  ETFs 
investment trusts; the same hereinafter) and debt securities: Limit quotation.   

(2) Pursuant to [§9(3)] of the Regulation, the bid quotations for License & Permit Bonds 
(LPBs), from among those mentioned in [§61(2) through (4)], which were issued in the 
same month on the basis of the trading day, may be placed in the form of the quotations 
by class. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

§11. Quotation Receiving Hours 

(1) Pursuant to [§10(2)] of the Regulation, the quotation receiving hours shall be as noted 
in each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on May 13, 2005; March 19, 2009; 
July 29, 2010; December 6, 2010; May 19, 2015; June 21, 2016; April 3, 2019) 

1.  Regular  session:  From  thirty  (30)  minutes  before  the  opening  of  trading  hours 
(hereinafter referred to as “market opening”) to the market closing time. Provided that, 
in the case of regular session auction-based block trade, it shall be from  the market 
opening to thirty (30) minutes before the market closing time; and 

2. In  the case of off-hours sessions, the hours  as  classified in  each of the  following 
items: 

(a)  For the pre-hours sessions, the hours classified for each trading type as follows: 

(i) Off-hours closing price trade: From 08:30 to 08:40 hours; 

(ii)  Off-hours  block  trade,  off-hours  basket  trade  and  off-hours  auction-based 

21 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
   
block trade: From 08:00 to 09:00 hours 

(iii) [Deleted on April 3, 2019] 

(b) For the after-hours sessions, the hours classified for each trading type as follows: 

(i) Off-hours closing price trade: From the market closing time to 16:00 hours;   

(ii) Off-hours  call auction:  From 16:00  to  18:00 hours (In  the case of deciding 
closing prices, it shall be until the time when the relevant price is determined.) 

(iii) Off-hours block trade and off-hours basket trade: From 15:40 to 18:00 hours 

(2) The Exchange may change the quotation receiving hours specified in paragraph (1) in 
cases where it falls under any of the following cases:   

1. Where the trading hours were changed pursuant to the provisions of [§8]; and   

2. Other cases that are deemed necessary for market management.   

§12. Input of Quotation Details 

(1) Pursuant to [§11] of the Regulation, each member shall input each of the following 
quotation details to the computer system of the Exchange: (Amended on July 16, 2009; 
July 29, 2010; January 27, 2011; December 28, 2011; September 20, 2012; December 18, 
2013; September 2, 2014; December 10, 2014; March 6, 2015; February 24, 2016; March 
24,  2016;  March  25,  2016;  February  28,  2017;  December  6,  2018;  July  11,  2019; 
December 22, 2022; August 8, 2023; November 23, 2023; May 23, 2024) 

1. Classification of the regular session, pre-hours session or after-hours session;   

1-2. In the case of a regular session auction-based block trade, such classification;   

2. In the case of a quotation for after-hours session, the type of trade according to each 
subparagraph of [§33] of the Regulation;   

3. Issue or class;   

4. Quantity;   

5. Each of following quotation types;   

(a) In the case of stocks, DRs of foreign stocks, collective investment securities of 
ETFs  and  ETNs:  Limit  quotation,  market  quotation,  limit-to-market-on-close 
quotation, immediately executable limit quotation, best limit quotation, quotation for 
auction-based block trade, mid-price quotation, and stop-limit quotation; (Amended 
on February 27, 2025) 

22 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(b)  In  the  case  of  debt  securities:  Limit  quotation,  one-sided  market-making 
quotation, two-sided market-making quotation, market taking quotation, and bid for 
general collateral Repo; and 

(c) In the case of securities other than those mentioned in items (a) and (b): Limit 
quotation. 

6.  Price.  Provided  that  this  provision  shall  not  apply  to  the  market  quotations, 
immediately executable limit quotations, best limit quotations, quotation for auction-
based block trade, mid-price quotation, quotations for off-hours closing price trade and 
quotations placed to cancel the existing quotations; (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

    6-2. In the case of stop-limit quotation: Stop quotation [February 27, 2025] 

7. Classification for bid or offer; 

8. In the case of offer quotation, classification for each of following items: 

(a) Offer quotations falling under any subparagraph of [§17(1)] or [§44-2(1)] of the 
Regulation; 

(b)  Quotations  for  covered  short  sales  under  [§17(1)2]  or  [§44-2(2)]  of  the 
Regulation; and 

(c) Any other offer quotations. 

9. Member’s ID number; 

10. ID number of the branch; 

11. Account number;   

12. Order number; 

13. In the case of cancellation or correction quotations, the classification thereof and 
original order number;   

14. Classification of customer account transaction or self-account transaction; 

14-2. One of the following items based on the method of generating quotation: 

(a)  High-speed algorithmic trading quotation; 

(b) Algorithmic trading quotation excluding the quotation in item (a); or 

(c)  Quotations excluding quotations in items (a) and (b). 

23 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
    14-3.  In  the  case  of  submitting  quotations  through  high-speed  algorithmic  trading 

account, matters in each of the following items:   

(a)  A  number  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “high-speed  algorithmic  trading 
number”)  that  combines  the  trader  registration  number  and  risk  management 
number pursuant to  [§131(5)]. Provided that, in  the case of quotations falling 
under  items  14-2  (b)  and  (c),  it  is  limited  to  cases  where  the  self-match 
prevention  condition  pursuant  to  [§13-2]  and  the  mass  order  cancellation 
pursuant to [§17-2]. 

(b) Conditions in the case of quotations imposed the self-match prevention condition 

pursuant to [§13-2]; and 

        (c) Quotation group number in Annex Form 1-3 to apply the mass order cancellation 

pursuant to [§17-2]. 

15. In the case of quotation placed to purchase or dispose the treasury stocks, each of 
the following classifications: 

(a) Following classifications according to the purposes thereof 

(i) Trades conducted for the purpose of distributing at the time when stock options 
are exercised; 

(ii) Trades conducted according to the money trust contract of treasury stocks; and 

(iii) Trades conducted for the purpose other than those under (i) and (ii).   

(b) Following classifications according to the trading methods 

(i) Trades subject to [§35(4)] of the Regulation; 

(ii) From among the purchase of treasury stocks pursuant to [§39(4)1&2] of the 
Regulation, those subject to [§35(2)] of the Regulation; and 

(iii) Trades other than those under (i) (ii). 

16. Accounts shall be classified into the following items: 

(a)  In  the case of placing a quotation  pursuant  to each  subparagraph of [§9-3(1)] 
(including  the  case  of  placing  quotation  using  an  account  under  the  name  of 
customer  who  has  entered  into  an  agreement  for  discretionary  investment,  or  the 
account  opened  per  individual  trust  asset  under  the  name  of  member),  the 
classification for each of such cases;   

(b) In the case of placing a quotation through the account exclusively for the trading 

24 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
of stocks for risk hedging prescribed in Article 115(2) of the Enforcement Decree 
of the Restriction of Special Taxation Act, the classification of such accounts;   

(c)  In  the case of placing a quotation  for the  investment  of  collective investment 
securities of collective investment companies for foreign equity investment through 
securities savings  account  for foreign  equity  investment  prescribed in  Article  91-
17(1) of the Restriction of Special Taxation Act, the classification of such accounts;   

(d) In the case of placing a quotation through the account that is exclusively for the 
trading  of  stocks  that  are  subject  to  the  market-making  agreement  (hereinafter 
referred  to  as  the  “market-making  account”)  pursuant  to  Article  115(5)  of  the 
Enforcement Decree of the Restriction of Special Taxation Act, the classification of 
such accounts; 

(e)  In  the  case  of  placing  a  quotation  through  foreigner’s  consolidated  accounts 
prescribed in Article 6-7(7) of the Regulations on Financial Investment Business, 
the classification of such accounts; 

(f) In the case of placing a quotation through the account exclusively for arbitrage 
trading  that  is  prescribed  in  Article  115(12)  of  the  Enforcement  Decree  of  the 
Restriction of Special Taxation Act, the classification of such accounts; and 

(g) In the case of placing a quotation through the bond market-making account noted 
in the front part of [§99-9(5)], the classification of such accounts. 

17. In the case of a customer for whom the good faith deposit is collected pursuant to 
[§80(1)] of the Regulation, such classification; 

18. In the case of margin trading prescribed in the Regulations on Financial Investment 
Business, the classification for each of such trading; 

18-2. In the case of trading of stocks, etc. (referring to the “stocks, etc.” noted in [§15] 
of  the  Regulation;  the  same  hereinafter  in  [§14],  [§104],  and  [§108])  linked  with  a 
contract for difference (hereinafter referred to as the “CFD”) prescribed in Article 5-
59-2 of the Financial Investment Business Regulations, such classification; 

19. In the case of quotations for arbitrage trading and hedge trading, the classification 
under each of the following items:   

(a) Index arbitrage trading;   

(b) Sector index arbitrage trading;

arbitraging;

(e)  Arbitrage  trading  of  collective  investment  securities,  while  it  is  not  non-

(f) Arbitrage trading of ETNs while it is non-arbitrage trading;   

(g) Arbitrage trading of ETNs while it is not non-arbitrage trading; 

(h) DR arbitrage trading; 

(i) DR of foreign stocks arbitrage trading; 

(j) Hedge trading under [§18(2)6] of the Regulation and long hedge trading for the 
same purpose; 

(k) Hedge trading under [§18(2)7] of the Regulation and long hedge trading for the 
same purpose; 

(l) Hedge trading under [§18(2)7-2] of the Regulation and long hedge trading for the 
same purpose; and 

(m) Hedge trading under [§18(2)8] of the Regulation and long hedge trading for the 
same purpose. 

20. In the case of a quotation for trading a basket of stocks, the classification for each 
of the following items:   

(a) Non-arbitrage trading;   

(b)  Trading  for  the  purpose  of  creating  collective  investment  securities  of  ETFs, 
while it is non-arbitrage trade; and 

(c)  Trading  for  the  purpose  of  creating  collective  investment  securities  of  ETFs, 
while it is not non-arbitrage trade.

classification;

they  reside  in  Korea.  Provided  that,  in  the  case  of  foreigners  treated  as  citizens 
(hereinafter referred to as the “foreigner treated as a citizen”) under subparagraph 2 of

classified as not having foreigner identification means;

27.  Classification  of  inputting  methods  for  the  orders  [in  the  case  of  item  (e),  the 
quotation  price  shall  be  included]  noted  in  each  of  the  following  items  and  the 
identification  code  of  the  order-inputting  device  [excluding  item  (b)].  Provided  that 
these provisions shall not apply to the debt securities:   

(a) Method of inputting quotation information into an input device by an officer or 
employee of a member, upon receiving an entrustment from a customer in written 
form  or over telephone,  etc.:  IP address  and MAC address  of the input device of 
office;   

(b) Method of inputting the details of order into a member computer system directly 
by a customer through a wired communication device;   

(c) Method of inputting the details of order into a member computer system directly 
by a customer through a wireless communication device: ID number of the wireless 
device;   

(d) Method of inputting the details of order into a member computer system directly 
by a customer through a computer: IP address and MAC address; and   

(e) Method  of inputting  quotation  information  other  than those mentioned above: 
Unique identification code that can be used to identify the order-inputting device.   

    27-2. Specification of whether or not a trading market is designated [referring to the 
securities market under Article 8-2(4)1 of the Act] and multilateral trading company. 
Provided that, this does not apply to debt securities. [February 27, 2025] 

27 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
    27-3.  In  cases  where  a customer or  a  member receives the short selling  registration 
number  noted  in  Article  6-37,  Paragraph  2  of  the  Financial  Investment  Business 
Regulation (hereinafter referred to as “short selling registration number”), such short 
selling registration number (limited to stocks); and [March 26, 2025] 

28.  In  cases  where  an  entrustment  was  received  from  other  investment  traders  or 
brokers, the number that identifies the relevant investment trader or broker. 

(2)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1),  in  the  case  of  submitting  a  quotation  for  regular 
session block trading, regular session basket trading, off-hours block trading or off-hours 
basket  trading,  the  information  noted  in  each  of  the  following  subparagraphs  shall  be 
inputted: (Amended July 29, 2010; March 25, 2016; March 12, 2021; December 22, 2022; 
May 23, 2024) 

1.  Each  of  the  details  under  paragraph  (1).  Provided  that,  the  details  noted  in 
subparagraphs 5, 6-2, 14-3(b) and (c), 16(g), 21, 23 through 23-3 of paragraph (1) shall 
be excluded; (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

2. Classification for block trading or basket trading; and 

3.  Negotiation  number,  detailed  negotiation  number  and  names  of  negotiators. 
Provided that, in the case where the block trade in the regular trading session or the 
block trade in the after-hour trading session is made by the method in accordance with 
[§49(1)2], member number and account number of the other party and the time when 
the negotiation was completed shall be inputted. 

(3)  With  respect  to  the  member  ID  under  paragraph  (1)9  [including  the  cases  cited  in 
paragraph  (2)],  the  Exchange  may  issue  multiple  ID  numbers  to  a  member  when  it  is 
deemed  inevitable  to  do  so  due  to  a  delay  in  the  change  of  member  computer  system 
following the merger between the members.   

(4) In cases where the ID number of branch office or account number has been changed, 
the member shall notify the Exchange of the details of change without delay.   

(5)  When  placing  a  quotation  after  receiving  an  entrustment  from  other  investment 
brokers, the member shall input the account number and investor classification code on 
the basis of the customer who entrusted the order to the relevant investment broker.   

(6) In the case of the when issued trade stipulated in [§59-2] of the Regulation (hereinafter 
referred to as the “when issued trade”), the yield, instead of price, may be entered. In such 
cases, a quotation is deemed to be placed by the price calculated by the following formula: 
[November 18, 2015] 

Price=10,000-(Yield x 1,000)   

(7) In addition to paragraphs (1) through (6), in cases where other matters concerning the 
input  of  quotation  details  are  needed,  the  Exchange  shall  notify  such  matters  to  the 

28 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
members. (Amended on November 18, 2015) 

(Wholly amended on March 19, 2009) 

§12-2. Matters for Inspection of Quotation Suitability, etc. 

“Matters specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§11-2(1)] of the Regulation shall refer 
to the details under each of the following subparagraphs. Provided that, in cases where 
quotations  are  submitted  through  member  debt  securities  terminals  (referring  to  the 
terminals  that  are  connected  to  the  Exchange’s  system  by  members  using  programs 
provided  by  the  Exchange  under  the  authorization  of  the  Exchange,  to  perform  tasks 
related to the trading of debt securities; the same hereinafter), only those matters deemed 
necessary  by  the  Exchange  may  apply  thereto.  (Amended  on  March  8,  2012;  July  10, 
2014; March 6, 2015; July 10, 2019; November 28, 2019; July 23, 2020; December 22, 
2022) 

1. With respect to accounts, the matters in each of the followings: 

(a) Account numbers noted in [§12(1)11]; and 

(b) Account classifications noted in [§12(1)16]. 

2. With respect to issues, the maters in each of the followings: 

(a) Issue codes; and 

(b) Whether it is an issue, the trading of which is suspended under [§26] and [§49] 
of the Regulation, the KOSPI Market Listing Regulation and  the KOSPI Market 
Disclosure Regulation.   

3. Matters about quotation quantity noted in each of the followings:   

(a) Trading quantity unit under [§33];   

(b) Quotation quantity limit under [§14(1)3]; 

(c) Quantity limit on liquidity providing quotation under [§31-6(4) & (5)]; 

(d) Quantity limit of quotation submitted for trading treasury stocks under [§57(1)3]; 
and     

(e) In the case of debt securities, quantity limit under [§14(1)4(a) through 4(c)]. 

4. Matters about quotation price noted in each of the followings: 

(a) Quotation price unit under [§32(2)]; 

29 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(b) Limits on quotation prices under [§20] of the Regulation; 

(c) Quotation price limit under [§14(1)1&2-3]; 

(d) Price limit of liquidity providing quotation under [§20-5(1)] of the Regulation; 

(e) Price limit of quotation submitted for trading of treasury stocks under [§35(5) 
and 39(1)] of the Regulation; and 

(f) In the case of debt securities, price limit noted in [§14(1)4(d)].   

    4-2. Matters about stop price noted in each of the followings: [February 27, 2025] 

          (a) Limits on stop price under [§14(1)2-4(a)]; and [February 27, 2025] 

          (b) Limits on quotation price units under [§14(1)2-4(b). [February 27, 2025] 

5. Matters about quotation type noted in each of the followings: (Amended on February 
27, 2025) 

(a) Restriction on quotation type in each subparagraph of [§10(1)]; and (Amended 
on February 27, 2025) 

(b) Input restriction per quotation type under [§14(2)] [excluding subparagraph 2(b) 
of the same Paragraph].   

6. Matters about good faith deposit noted in each of the followings:     

(a) Whether or not the good faith deposit has been collected pursuant to [§89(1), (4) 
& (5)] of the Regulation; and 

(b)  In  the  case  of  ELWs  or  securities  noted  in  [§87-2(1)2]  of  the  Regulation, 
whether or not the good faith deposit pursuant to [§87-2] of the Regulation has been 
collected.

trading number pursuant to subparagraph 14-3(a) of [§12]: 

(a)  Whether quotations are submitted through the high-speed algorithmic trading 
account reported pursuant to [§104-3(3)] of the Regulation; and 

(b) Whether the high-speed algorithmic trading number linked to account in item (a)   
above  matches  the  high-speed  algorithmic  trading  number  inputted  pursuant  to 
subparagraph 14-3(a) of [§12]. 

8. Matters required for the market management noted in each of the followings:

(a)[Deleted on July 11, 2019]

§13. Validity of Quotations 

(1) Pursuant to the proviso to [§12(1)] of the Regulation, the quotation falling under any 
of the following subparagraphs shall be deemed invalid: (Amended on  May 13, 2005; 
March 19, 2009; July 29, 2010; December 22, 2022; April 12, 2023) 

1. Quotations entered (excluding cancellation quotations) during the trading suspension 
or halt under the provisions of [§25(1)], [§26(1)], [§27], [§49], [§50] and [§107] of the 
Regulation [including the temporary closing of markets pursuant to the provisions of 
[§6] of Regulation and the suspension of trading pursuant to the Listing Regulation and 
the KOSPI Market Disclosure Regulation (hereinafter in this Article referred to as the 
“trading  halt,  etc.”].  Provided  that  cancellation  quotations  (including  quotations  to 
which the mass order cancellation pursuant to [§17-2] is applied) inputted during the 
period of the relevant trading halt or suspension shall be recognized as effective;   

2. In the case of regular session, the quotations noted in each of following items:   

(a) Quotations received during the pre-hours session;   

(b)  In  the  case  of  individual  auctions  under  [§23]  and  [§24]  of  the  Regulation, 
quotations for auction-based block trade; and 

(c)  In  the  case  of  regular  session  auction-based  block  trades,  quotations  for 
individual auctions under [§23] and [§24] of the Regulation. 

3. In the case of off-hours sessions, the quotations noted in each of the following items; 

(a)  In  the  case  of  pre-hours  session,  the  quotations  received  during  the  regular 
session;   

(a-2) In the case of off-hours closing price trade, quotations for auction-based block 
trade; and 

(a-3)  In  the  case  of  off-hours  auction-based  block  trade,  quotations  for  off-hours 
closing price trade.   

(b)  In  the  case  of  the  after-hours  session,  the  quotations  received  during  the  pre-
hours session and the regular session; and   

31 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(c) In the case of off-hours call auction, the quotations for off-hours closing price 
trade.   

4. Among the quotations participated in the determination of the first trading price of 
an issue using the first trading price as the base price, the quotations with the prices 
that  are  above  the  upper  limit  price  or  below  the  lower  limit  price  after  the 
determination of the first trading price; 

    4-2. Mid-price quotations received before the quotation receiving hours for call auction 
to  determine  the  price  at  the  time  of  market  closing  noted  in  [§23(1)4]  of  the 
Regulations,  but  for  which  no  transaction  has  been  concluded  by  the  quotation 
reception time; and [February 27, 2025] 

5. Additionally, the quotations that the Exchange deems it improper to recognize their 
validity.   

(2) A quotation falling under any of the following subparagraphs shall be suspended its 
validity until the resumption time specified in the relevant subparagraph: (Amended on 
March 19, 2009; February 27, 2025) 

    1. In case of suspension of trading during the quotation receiving hours for call auction 
or  suspension  of  quotation  reception  in  accordance  with  [§50]  of  the  Regulations, 
quotations received before the relevant measures: When trading is resumed [February 
27, 2025] 

    2. Mid-price quotation in cases where there is no quantity of quotation other than the 
mid-price quotation on either the sell side or the buy side during the time of trading by 
means of continuous auction: When there is a quantity of quotation other than the mid-
price quotation on both bid and ask sides; and [February 27, 2025] 

    3.  Mid-price  quotation  in  cases  where  no  transaction  is  made  during  the  quotation 
receiving hours for call auction: When the method of executing transactions is changed 
to continuous auction and there are quotations other than mid-price quotation on both 
the bid and ask sides. [February 27, 2025] 

(3) In the case of quotations affixed with the conditions stipulated in subparagraph 2(a) 
of [§108], among the quantity of such quotations, the quantity of quotations falling under 
each of the following subparagraphs shall be construed as cancelled: (Amended on March 
19, 2009) 

1. In cases where the condition of immediate or cancel (“IOC”) is affixed, the quantity 
that are not executed;   

2. In cases where the condition of fill or kill (“FOK”) is affixed, if the total quantity 
quoted cannot be executed, the total quantity of such quotation.   

32 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§13-2. Validity of Quotations with Self-match Prevention Condition 

(1) Pursuant to the proviso to [§12(1)] of the Regulation, in the case where, among the 
quotations of high-speed algorithmic traders, the high-speed algorithmic trading numbers 
of  quotations  are  the  same  and  it  is  possible  to  execute  transactions  between  such 
quotations affixed with the following conditions, the quantity of the relevant quotation 
shall be deemed to be cancelled according to each of the following subparagraphs based 
on the condition imposed on the quotation received later:   

    1. A condition to cancel all of the balance of previously received quotation;   

    2. A condition to cancel the entire quantity of quotation received later; and   

    3.  A  condition  to  cancel  each  quantity  that  can  be  executed  between  buy  and  sell 

quotations. 

(2) Paragraph (1) shall apply only to the case of continuous trading under [§24] of the 
Regulation  during  the  regular  trading  session.  Provided  that  this  shall  not  apply  if  the 
relevant quotation is subject to the trading priority for simultaneous quotations pursuant 
to [§34(3)1].   

(3) In the case of quotations to which both the self-match prevention conditions under 
paragraph  (1)  and  the  IOC  condition  under  subparagraph  12(a)(i)  of  [§108]  are 
simultaneously affixed, the self-match prevention condition shall take priority over the 
IOC condition. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

[December 22, 2022] 

§14. Restrictions on Placement of Quotations 

(1) In accordance with [§12(2)] of the Regulation, a member shall not submit quotations 
falling  under  any  of  the  following  subparagraphs:  (Amended  on  August  26,  2005; 
February 3, 2009; March 19, 2009; July 16, 2009; July 1, 2010; July 29, 2010; January 
27, 2011; December 2, 2011; April 20, 2012; May 13, 2013’ February 28, 2014; April 7, 
2014; July 10, 2014; September 2, 2014; July 16, 2015; September 13, 2018; December 
6, 2018; July 11, 2019; November 28, 2019; May 26, 2020; July 23, 2020; June 8, 2021; 
June 8, 2022; December 22, 2022; April 12, 2023; August 8, 2023)   

1. In the case of determining the opening price of the issues using the first trading price 
as the base price: Any quotation of which price is above the maximum quotation price 
or below the minimum quotation price;   

2. [Deleted on April 12, 2023]   

2-2. In the case of a quotation for covered short sale that is subject to price restriction 
pursuant to [§18] of the Regulation, when falling under any of the followings:   

33 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(a) Case of determining the first price of an issue using the first trading price as the 
base price and a newly-listed issue noted in [§30(1)2a]; and 

(b) Case of determining the opening price of initially listed issue of subscription right 
certificates, subscription warrants and ELWs; 

2-3. In the case of a limit-to-market-on-close quotation: Any quotation falling under 
any of the following items: 

(a) Bid quotation placed at the upper limit price;   

(b) Offer quotation placed at the lower limit price; and   

(c) [Deleted on July 11, 2019] 

2-4.  In  the  case  of  a  stop-limit  quotation:  Any  quotation  falling  under  any  of  the 
following items: [February 27, 2025] 

(a) A quotation whose stop price exceeds the upper limit price or falls below the 
lower limit price; and [February 27, 2025] 

(b) A quotation whose stop price does not match the quotation price unit noted in 
[§32(2)]. [February 27, 2025] 

3.  In  the  case  of  stocks,  etc.:  Any  quotation  with  a  quantity  exceeding  the  amount 
specified  in  each  of  the  following  items  (excluding  quotations  for  regular  session 
auction-based  block  trading,  regular  session  basket  trading,  regular  session  block 
trading,  off-hours  auction-based  block  trading,  off-hours  block  trading,  off-hours 
basket  trading,  or  the  quotations  under  [§22]  of  the  Securities  Market  Clearing  and 
Settlement Business Regulation.): (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(a)  Where  the  amount  calculated  by  the  Exchange  for  every  trading  day  by 
multiplying the base price determined in [Annex 1-2] (referred to as “base price for 
the date of quotation placement” hereinafter in this Subparagraph) by the number of 
listed  securities  (referred  to  as  “market  capitalization  for  the  date  of  quotation 
placement” hereinafter in this Subparagraph) is KRX 10 trillion or more; a quantity 
calculated by dividing KRW 100 billion by the base price for the date of quotation 
placement  (a  quantity  less  than  the  trading  unit  of  the  regular  session  shall  be 
rounded off to the trading unit; the same hereinafter in this Subparagraph); 

(b) Where the market capitalization for the date of quotation placement is KRX 100 
billion or more but less than KRW 10 trillion; a quantity equivalent to 1/100 of the 
number of listed securities; 

(c) Where the market capitalization for the date of quotation placement is KRX 20 
billion or more but less than KRW 100billion; the quantity calculated by dividing 
KRW 1 billion by the base price for the date of quotation placement; and 

34 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(d) Where the market capitalization for the date of quotation placement is less than 
KRW 20 billion; the quantity equivalent to 5/100 of the number of listed securities. 

4. In the case of debt securities, the quotations falling under any of the following items:   

(a) In the case of a quotation per issue, a quotation with a quantity exceeding the 
outstanding balance of listed amount. Provided that when an order is entrusted from 
an individual under item (h) of [§104(1)6], it shall be a quotation with a quantity that 
exceeds the lesser of KRW twenty (20) billion (twenty (20) billion points for foreign 
currency-denominated debt securities) and the outstanding balance of listed amount. 

(b)  In  the  case  of  quotation  quantity  per  person  under  [§61]  exceeding  KRW  50 
million. Provided that this shall not apply to offer quotations specified in the sales 
entrustment contract under [§95] of the Regulation and to market-making quotations 
under [§99-4(1)2].   

(c) In the case of bid quotations per class (bid quotations per issue in the case of 
LPBs  mentioned  in  subparagraph  1  of  [§61])  placed  by  LPB  dealers  pursuant  to 
[§74], a quotation with a quantity exceeding KRW 15 billion (in the case of excellent 
LPB dealers noted in [§62-3(1)], a quotation quantity separately set by the Exchange 
within KRW 22.5 billion). (Amended on November 27, 2025) 

(d)  Bid  quotations  with  prices  exceeding  the  previous  day’s  closing  price  {if  no 
previous day’s closing price is available, it shall be the mark-to-market price under 
[§65(2)] of the Regulation, however, if no mark-to-market price is available, it shall 
be KRW 10,000 at face value for an initially-listed issue only on the date of listing 
and  10,000  points  for  foreign  currency-denominated  debt  securities}  by  the 
following  ratio  or  offer  quotations  with  the  prices  lower  than  the  previous  day’s 
closing  price  by  the  following  ratio.  Provided  that  this  provision  shall  not  be 
applicable during the period when trading is allowed pursuant to [§9] of the KOSPI 
Market Listing Regulation and when the Exchange deems it necessary for market 
management, the ratio may be set differently. (Amended on December 24, 2025) 

(i) For debt securities, excluding equity-related bonds: 30/100; and   
(ii) For equity-related bonds: 50/100.   

(e) Where the first trading price of an initially listed issue as equity linked bonds 
(including the beneficiary certificate noted in [§7(2)] is determined: Any quotation 
for covered short sales for which the price is restricted pursuant to [§44-3] of the 
Regulation.   

(f) Notwithstanding the  main sentence of item  (d), for the  issue of which closing 
price  of  the  day  and  mark-to-market  price  are  not  available,  the  quotations  that 
exceed KRW 15,000.   

35 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
5. In the case of falling  under each of the following subparagraphs, quotations with 
self-match prevention condition pursuant to [§13-2]: 

(a) Issues that are permitted to be traded for a certain period of time in accordance

scheduled to be delisted”); (Amended on February 27, 2025)

referred to as “temporary overheated issues”; (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(d)  Investment  precaution  issues  under  [§106-4(1)]  of  the  Regulation  (hereinafter 
referred to as “investment precaution issue”); and (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

        (e)  Low  liquidity  issues  subject  to  periodic  call  auction  noted  in  [§56-3(1)]  and 
different classes of stock issues subject to periodic call auction noted in [§56-4(1)]. 
(Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(2)  No  member  shall  place  quotations  falling  under  any  of  the  followings  for  each 
quotation type and condition: (Amended on May 13, 2005; March 19, 2009; July 29, 2010; 
October 22, 2012; May 13, 2013; March 25, 2016; February 28, 2017; July 11, 2019; July

1. Market quotations and limit-to-market-on-close quotations that fall under any of the

limit-to-market-on-close quotations); and [February 27, 2025]

pursuant to [§35(1)];

and [February 27, 2025]

management.
