price used in the trade executed by the right exercise or the value of the stock price 
index) and the price of underlying asset.   

6. Cases that the Exchange deems them necessary for the market management for the 
reasons  such as  the sudden change in  quotation  conditions  or trading  conditions  (in 
case of ELWs, quotation and trading conditions of underlying assets shall be included).   

[December 1, 2005] 

§31-6. Methods of submitting Liquidity Providing Quotations 

(1)  In  cases  where  it  is  difficult  to  determine  the  price  range  of  liquidity  providing 
quotations on the basis of the best quotation price pursuant to the proviso to [§20-5(1)] of 
the Regulation, each of the following subparagraphs shall apply: (Amended on March 3, 
2011) 

1.  Case  of  quotation  receiving  hours  for  call  auction,  the  price  range  determined 
pursuant to each subparagraph (excluding the proviso of each subparagraph) of [§20-
5(1)] of the Regulation shall apply by assuming that the expected best quotation price 
is the best quotation price; and   

2.  Case  where  there  are  no  quotations  on  both  of  the  offer  and  the  bid  sides,  the 
provisions of [§20-5(1)] of the Regulation shall apply to the case of determining the 
range of offer (bid) quotation, by assuming that the most recent price is the best bid 
(offer) price. In such cases, when the most recent price and the base price is different 
during the quotation receiving hours for the determination of first price, the most recent 

56 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
price shall be deemed the base price.   

(2)  In cases where the liquidity  providing quotations of the relevant  member have  not 
been submitted pursuant to the provisions of [§20-5(5)] of the Regulation, and where the 
liquidity  providing  quotations  on  either  side  of  offer  or  bid  for  collective  investment 
securities of ETFs, ETNs or ELWs are submitted, the member may place such quotations 
at a price that is deemed reasonable by taking into consideration such factors as the net 
asset value, indicative value or theoretical price. [August 28, 2007] (Amended on July 16, 
2009; September 2, 2014; July 20, 2021) 

(3) In cases where a liquidity providing quotation has already been submitted on any one 
side of offer or bid by the relevant member quotation pursuant to the provisions of [§20-
5(5)] of the Regulation, and where the liquidity providing quotations are submitted on the 
other  side,  the  quotations  shall  be  placed  at  a  price  where  the  quotation  spread  ratio 
calculated according to the method specified in each of the following subparagraphs are 
within the range pursuant to each subparagraph of [§20-4(1)] of the Regulation. In such 
cases, the quotation spread ratio of one (1) quotation price unit exceeds the range specified 
in each subparagraph of [§20-4(1)] of the Regulation, it shall be the price falling under 
one (1) quotation price unit. (Amended on August 28, 2007; December 27, 2007; July 16, 
2009; September 2, 2014; July 20, 2021) 

1.  In  the  case  of  stocks,  collective  investment  securities  of  ETFs  and  ETNs,  the 
quotation spread ratio calculated on the basis of the best quotation on the side to which 
the relevant member has placed the liquidity providing quotation; and   

2. In the case of ELWs, the quotation spread ratio calculated on the basis of liquidity 
providing quotation that the relevant member placed. In such cases, when the relevant 
member has placed more than two (2) liquidity providing quotations, it shall be based 
on the best quotation in terms of the price. 

(4) In cases where a member submits the liquidity providing quotations according to [§20-
5(3)] of the Regulation, the quantity of quotation shall exceed the quantity specified in 
each of the following subparagraphs. Provided that, in cases where the number of quantity, 
which is calculated by subtracting the number of quantity held by the member from the 
listed quantity, is less than the quantity specified in each of the following subparagraphs, 
the number of bid quotations among liquidity providing quotations shall be the quantity 
specified in each of the following subparagraphs and in cases where the best quotation 
price on the counter side is submitted as the price of liquidity providing quotation of stock, 
the quantity shall be higher than the quantity specified in subparagraph 1 and lower than 
the  quantity  of  best  quotation  on  the  counter-side  (if  bid  and  offer  quotations  are  not 
available on both side, this shall not apply): (Amended on April 16, 2009; July 16, 2009; 
March 3, 2011;February 28, 2014; September 2, 2014;October 1, 2015) 

1. In the case of stocks, as a quantity larger than ten (10) times the trading quantity unit, 
the quantity that the member who entered the agreement for liquidity provision with 
the company that listed the relevant stock has reported to the Exchange;   

57 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2.  In  the  case  of  collective  investment  securities  of  ETFs  and  ETNs,  the  quantity 
corresponding to one hundred (100) times the trading quantity unit; and   

3. In the case of ELWs, the quantity corresponding to ten (10) times the trading quantity 
unit  for  off  quotation;  and  the  quantity  corresponding  to  ten  (10)  times  the  trading 
quantity unit and KRW 5,000 for bid quotation. Provided that, as a bid quotation, in 
cases  where  the  quantity  held  by  the  member  (including  the  quantity  to  be  held 
subsequent to trade execution or borrowing: the same hereinafter in [§31-8]) exceeds 
the quantity obtained by subtracting the quantity equivalent to KRW 5,000 from the 
listed  quantity,  it  shall  be  the  quantity  corresponding  to  ten  (10)  times  the  trading 
quantity unit.   

(5)  In  cases  where  a  member  corrects  the  prices  of  the  liquidity  providing  quotations 
which are not yet executed, the quotation quantity shall be larger than the smaller of the 
quantities specified in each of the following subparagraphs. Provided that, in cases where 
the  price  of  liquidity  providing  quotation  of  stock  is  corrected  to  the  price  of  best 
quotation on the counter side, the quantity shall be higher than the smaller quantity noted 
in each of following subparagraphs and less than the quantity of best quotation on the 
counter side: (Amended on August 28, 2007; March 3, 2011)   

1. The total unexecuted quantity; and   

2. The quantity specified in each subparagraph of paragraph (4).   

(6) Any member intending to place the liquidity providing quotations for ELWs pursuant 
to the provisions of paragraphs (2) and (3) shall notify the Exchange the guidelines, which 
were  established  in  accordance  with  the  internal  procedures  in  advance,  for  the 
modification and calculation of implied volatility that are required for the determination 
of fair price within five (5) trading days after putting it into effect. [December 27, 2007] 

(7)  After  calculating  the  implied  volatility  on  the  basis  of  bid  and  offer  quotations 
submitted for ELWs by the liquidity providing members pursuant to paragraphs (2) and 
(3), the Exchange may make public the changes in daily implied volatility. [December 27, 
2007] 

(8)  The  liquidity  providing  members  shall  not  entrust  the  submission  of  liquidity 
providing quotations to another member. [May 7, 2021] 

(9)  In cases where the liquidity  providing  members open, change  (including  the cases 
where an issue for which liquidity providing is conducted through the concerned account 
is changed) or close a liquidity providing account (including the account for hedge trades 
related to the submission of the liquidity providing quotations under [§18(2)6 through 7-
2] of the Regulation) pursuant to [§20-5(2)] of the Regulation, the matters concerning the 
account shall be reported to the Exchange in accordance with [Annex: Form No. 2-8] no 
later  than  two  (2)  trading  days  prior  to  the  date  of  submitting  the  liquidity  providing 
quotations (or hedge trade quotations) through the account. [July 20, 2021] 

58 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[December 1, 2005] 

§31-7. Exceptions to Submission of Quotations on Both Sides 

Pursuant to the proviso to [§20-5(4)] of the Regulation, the liquidity providing quotations 
falling under any one of the following subparagraphs may not be submitted: (Amended 
on May 29, 2006; August 28, 2007; December 27, 2007; February 3, 2009; July 16, 2009; 
April 7, 2011; December 28, 2011; September 2, 2014; July 20, 2021) 

1. In the case of stocks, when either side of bid or offer quotations includes a liquidity 
providing quotation submitted by the relevant member, the quotations for that side;   

2. [Deleted on April 7, 2011] 

3. In the case of collective investment securities of ETF, ETNs and ELWs, when, as a 
result  of  submitting  a  liquidity  providing  quotation  for  either  side  of  offer  or  bid 
quotation, the quotation price spread ratio to the liquidity providing quotation that the 
relevant member has already submitted on the other side falls below the ratio stipulated 
in [§20-4(1)] of the Regulation (in case of falling under the latter part of [§31-6(3)], it 
shall be the ratio corresponding to one (1) quotation price unit), the quotations for such 
other side;   

4. Offer quotations that fall under [§31-8(1-2)] or bid quotation falling under [§31-8(1-
3)].  In  such  cases,  even  in  cases  where  the  submission  of  bid  or  offer  quotation  on 
either  side  is  restricted,  the  liquidity  providing  quotation  on  the  other  side  shall  be 
submitted; and         

5. In the case of submitting ask quotation for ELW pursuant to the proviso to [31-8/4], 
bid quotation.   

[December 1, 2005] 

§31-8. Restrictions on Submission of Liquidity Providing Quotations 

Pursuant to [§20-5(5)] of the Regulation, members shall not submit liquidity providing 
quotations in the case of falling under any of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on 
December 27, 2007; February 3, 2009; April 16, 2009; December 6, 2010; December 28, 
2011; October 1, 2015; July 20, 2021) 

1. Case of falling under subparagraph 2 of Article 71 of the Act;   

1-2. Case where the quantity held by the member is below the quantity specified in 
each subparagraph of [§31-6(4)], the offer quotation; 

1-3.  Case  where  the  quantity  held  by  the  member  corresponds  to  the  total  listed 
quantity, the bid quotation;   

59 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2. In the case of stocks, when quotations have been already submitted on any one side 
of offer or bid quotation, the liquidity providing quotations for the relevant side;   

3. In the case of ELWs, during the last five (5) trading days before the termination 
date of the right exercise period. Provided that this provision shall not apply to the 
case of ELWs based on the stock price indices;   

4. In the case of ELWs, when the quotation spread ratio based on the best quotation 
during the regular session is within the ratio pursuant to [§20-4(1)3] of the Regulation. 
Provided that this provision shall not apply to the case of submitting an ask quotation 
that is below the best quotation while no liquidity providing quotation of member has 
been submitted; and       

5. In the case of ELWs, in cases where, as a result of the member submitting a liquidity 
providing  quotation  on  either  bid  or  ask  side,  the  quotation  spread  ratio  with  the 
liquidity  providing  quotation  already  submitted  on  the  other  side  by  the  relevant 
member drops below the minimum ratio specified by the Exchange.   

[December 1, 2005] 

§31-9. Assessment of Liquidity Providing Members 

(1) The Exchange may assess the members who provide liquidity pursuant to the former 
part of  [§20-6(1)] of the Regulation  for the matters specified in  each of  the following 
subparagraphs on each quarter (in the case of ETNs, it shall be monthly; the same shall 
apply  from  this  Article  through  [§31-11])  and  make  public  the  assessment  result; 
(Amended on December 27, 2007; July 16, 2009; September 2, 2014; December 16, 2015; 
December 28, 2018; January 24, 2019; July 23, 2020) 

1. In the case of stocks: 

(a) The extent to which the obligation to submit the liquidity providing quotations 
has been fulfilled;   

(b) The degree of contribution to improving the quotation spreads of a relevant issue 
by submitting the liquidity providing quotations; 

(c) How active in submitting the liquidity providing quotations; and 

(d) Compliance with the securities-related laws and regulations and the Exchange’s 
business-related regulations with respect to the liquidity provision. 

2. In the case of collective investment securities of ETFs, ETNs and ELWs: 

(a) The matters specified in subparagraphs 1(a) and 1(c). Provided that, in applying 
subparagraph  1(a)to  collective  investment  securities  of  ETFs  and  ETNs,  the 

60 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
disparate  ratio  shall  be  calculated  and  assessed  by  the  method  determined  by  the 
Exchange based on the price that is formed during the regular trading session;   

(b) The size of spread of the quotation submitted as a liquidity providing quotation; 

(c) The quantity of liquidity providing quotations submitted; and 

(d) Compliance  with  the  securities-related laws  and regulations and the  business-
related regulations of the Exchange with respect to the liquidity provision. 

(2) When making an assessment pursuant to paragraph (1), in cases where a member falls 
under any of following subparagraphs, a lowest grade shall be assigned to the relevant 
member regardless of the performance of other issues which the relevant member supplies 
the liquidity for:(Amended on July 16, 2009; September 2, 2014; June 30, 2022) 

1.  In  the  case  of  stocks  and  ELWs,  if  no  liquidity  providing  quotation  has  been 
submitted to the issues, for which the member is obliged to submit liquidity providing 
quotation, for at least thirty (30) minutes on the average per day;   

2. In the case of collective investment securities of ETFs and ETNs, if there is an issue 
that falls under [§31-10(1)1(a)] for consecutive two (2) quarters among the issues for 
which  members  submit  liquidity  providing  quotations.  Provided  that  this  provision 
shall not apply in cases where the Exchange deems it necessary due to reasons such as 
a sudden change in market conditions, etc. 

(3)  Members  shall  notify  the  details  that  the  Exchange  requires  for  the  assessment, 
including the specifics about the non-submission of liquidity providing quotations during 
the concerned quarter as a result of falling under subparagraphs 4, 4-2 and 6 of [§31-5(2)] 
or subparagraphs 1 through 1-3 of [§31-8] pursuant to [§20-6(2)] of the Regulation to the 
Exchange by the end of the concerned quarter. (Amended on August 28, 2007; December 
27, 2007; November 27, 2008; December 28, 2018; July 23, 2020) 

(4)  In  addition  to  the  provisions  of  paragraphs  (1)  through  (3),  assessment  criteria, 
announcement  methods,  and  other  matters  necessary  for  the  assessment  of  liquidity 
providing  members  shall  be  separately  determined  by  the  Exchange.  (Amended  on 
December 28, 2018) 

[May 29, 2006]   

§31-10. Conditions for Replacement of Liquidity Providing Members 

(1) The “conditions stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the latter part of [§20-6(1)] 
of the Regulation shall refer to the cases falling under each of the following subparagraphs: 
(Amended July 16, 2009; September 2, 2014; July 23, 2020) 

1. In the case of collective investment securities of ETFs and ETNs, any of the cases 
falling under the followings:   

61 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(a)  Case  where  the  number  of  trading  days  when  the  obligation  to  submit  the 
liquidity providing quotations pursuant to [§20-4(1)2] of the Regulation has not been 
complied for at least one (1) hour or the number of days when the disparate ratio 
pursuant to [§20-4(2)&(3)] of the Regulation was not observed is twenty (20) days(in 
the case of ETNs, seven (7) days every month) or more in a quarter; and   

(b) Case where there is a liquidity providing member who has received the lowest 
grade (in the case of ETNs, the lowest grade for two (2) consecutive times) as a result 
of  the  assessment  carried  for  each  quarter  (in  the  case  of  collective  investment 
securities  of  ETFs,  the  assessment  of  the  quarter  in  which  the  initial  listing  date 
belongs shall be excluded, and in the case of ETNs, the assessment of the month in 
which the initial listing date belongs shall be excluded) pursuant to [§31-9(1)2]. 

2. In the case of ELWs, case where the number of trading days when the obligation for 
submission of liquidity providing quotations pursuant to [§20-4(1)3] of the Regulation 
was  not  complied  with  for  one  (1)  hour  or  longer  is  five  (5)  or  higher  per  month 
(excluding the month which includes the initial listing date).   

(2)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1),  in  cases  where,  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary 
because  of  falling  under  any  of  the  following  subparagraphs,  each  subparagraph  of 
paragraph (1) may not apply:   

1.  Case  where,  as  a  result  of  the  failure  of  computer  systems  of  the  Exchange  or 
members  who  supply  the  liquidity  providing  quotations,  it  is  not  possible  to  apply 
paragraph (1)1; 

2. Case where the price of underlying asset fluctuates drastically; and 

3. Case where it is not possible to submit the liquidity providing quotations due to the 
sudden changes in the political and economic conditions.   

[December 27, 2007] 

§31-11. [Deleted on August 20, 2021] 

Section 2-3. Market Makers 
[March25, 2016] 

§31-12. Submission Methods of Market-making Quotations, etc. 

(1) The “quotations that make the market as stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the 
main sentence of [§20-9(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to a quotation submitted through 
market-making  accounts in  the manner of meeting all the requirements  of each of the 
following subparagraphs: 

62 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. It shall be a limit quotation or a best limit quotation; 

2. It shall be submitted during the quotation receiving hours in a regular session; and 

3. In the case of a bid quotation, the quotation shall be submitted at a price lower than 
the price of the best offer quotation at the time of submission and in case of an offer 
quotation, the quotation shall be submitted at a price higher than the price of the best 
bid quotation at the time of submission. Provided that this provision shall not apply to 
the  case  where  there  is  no  residual  quantity  of  quotations  on  the  other  side  of  the 
quotation to be submitted. 

(2) In cases where the quotations under paragraph (1) are submitted at a call auction under 
[§23]  of  the  Regulation,  “the  best  offer  quotation”  and  “the  best  bid  quotation”  in 
paragraph (1)3 shall be construed as “the expected best offer quotation” and “the expected 
best bid quotation”, respectively, which are officially announced pursuant to [§126(1)1]. 
(Amended on December 6, 2018) 

(3)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1)3,  in  cases  where  a  market  maker  submits  an  offer 
quotation at a price lower than the price of the best bid quotation at the time of submission 
or a bid quotation at a price higher than the price of the best offer quotation at the time of 
submission, only a quotation that falls under any of the followings shall be deemed as a 
market-making quotation: (Amended on November 28, 2019) 

1. A quotation that has not been executed after having been submitted; and 

2. An offer quotation of a stock which is subject to the market-making agreement and 
meets  all  of the  requirements  under each of the following  items.  In such cases, the 
quantity of quotations of a market maker that are executed in excess of 70/100 of the 
market  maker’s balance  held  {referring  to  the  daily  balance held  specified in  [§31-
19(4)]; the same hereinafter in [§31-18]} on the previous day shall be excluded. 

(a)Single stock futures or single stock options of which underlying assets include the 
relevant stock shall not be listed on the market; and 

(b)The  executed  price  of  the  quotation  shall  decrease  by  more  than  4/100  in 
comparison with the base price of the day. 

(4)  In  cases  where  a  market  maker  intends  to  open,  change  or  close  a  market-making 
account, he/she shall report the matters related to the account to the Exchange by no later 
than two (2) trading days prior to the date of opening, changing or closing the account in 
accordance with [Annex: Form No. 2-4]. 

(5) “Issues stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to the main sentence of 
[§20-9(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to the issues specified in [Annex 2-2]. 

(6)  The  market  makers  shall  not  entrust  the  submission  of  market-making  quotations 
under paragraphs (1) through (3) to another member. [May 7, 2021] 

63 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[March 25, 2016] 

§31-13. Qualifications of Market Makers 

(1)  “Other  requirements  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§20-9(2)3]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on March 13, 
2021; July 15, 2022) 

1. In the case of falling under any of followings, one (1) year or more shall have elapsed 
since then: 

(a) Case where the qualification of market  maker has been suspended pursuant  to 
[§31-21]; and 

(b)Case where a member has a record of having been subject to a criminal sanction, 
or any measures equivalent to or heavier than penalty surcharge, business suspension, 
trading suspension, or member fine (limited to a fine amounting to KRW 10 million 
or more), on account of a violation of the relevant statutes on securities businesses 
and the business regulations of the Exchange in the course of performing the tasks of 
market-making related to stocks (referring to market-making tasks for stocks in the 
KOSPI and KOSDAQ markets and equity derivatives in the derivatives market). 

2.The person in charge of market-making tasks shall have no record of having been 
subject to a criminal sanction or any measures equivalent to or heavier than penalty 
surcharge or suspension within the latest one (1) year on account of violation of the 
relevant laws on securities businesses and the business regulations of the Exchange. 

3. Two (2) or more persons in charge of market-making tasks shall be appointed to 
perform market-making tasks. 

4.  An  internal  control  device  shall  be  available  to  allow  the  quotations  for  covered 
short  sales  under  [§17(2)]  of  the  Regulation  only  if  the  relevant  listed  stocks  are 
borrowed. 

(2) In cases where a market maker designates or changes the person in charge of market-
making tasks, such fact shall be reported to the Exchange in advance in accordance with 
[Annex: Form No. 2-5]. 

[March 25, 2016] 

§31-14. Selection of Market-making Target Issues 

(1) Pursuant to [§20-9(3)] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall assess the liquidity of 
eligible issues based on the criteria specified in [Annex 2-2], select and publish the low-
liquidity  issues  subject  to  market-making  agreements  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the 

64 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
“market-making target issues”). 

(2) [Deleted on September 7, 2017] 

[March 25, 2016] 

§31-15. Selection of Market Makers and Allocation of Market-making Target Issues 

(1) Each member may apply for market-making after the Exchange officially announces 
the list of market-making target issues pursuant to [§20-9(3)] of the Regulation. 

(2) The Exchange may determine the number of market makers by taking into account 
the  number  of  members  applied  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1)  and  the  number  of  market-
making target issues. 

(3) The Exchange shall assess eligibility of the applicants noted in paragraph (1) based 
on the criteria specified in [Annex 2-3] to select market makers and the selected market 
makers may choose market-making target issues by the order of priority. 

(4)  The  Exchange  shall  allocate  market-making  target  issues  in  accordance  with  the 
selections made by the market makers pursuant to paragraph (3). Provided that, in cases 
where  it  is  deemed  necessary,  the  Exchange  may  change  the  allocation  method  in 
consultation with market makers. 

[March 25, 2016] 

§31-16. Conclusion or Termination, etc. of Market-making Agreements 

(1) Any person who was selected by the Exchange as a market maker pursuant to [§31-
15(3)]  shall  enter  into  a  market-making  agreement  in  advance  with  the  Exchange  in 
accordance with [Annex: Form No. 2-6] in order to submit the market-making quotations 
for  the  market-making  target  issues  that  have  been  allocated  pursuant  to  [§31-15(4)] 
(hereinafter referred to as the “market-making issues”). 

(2)  The  Exchange  may  terminate  a  market-making  agreement  as  determined  in  the 
market-making agreement entered into with a market maker. 

(3) The Exchange may terminate the market-making agreement for the relevant issue in 
cases where any of the following causes occurs: [March 12, 2021] 

1.  Case where the average daily turnover ratio (excluding the last seven (7) trading 
days of each quarter) is assessed every quarter pursuant to [Annex 2-4], and it 
exceeds 15% for two (2) consecutive quarters. In such cases, the market-making 
for the relevant issue shall terminate at the end of the concerned quarter; 

2.  Case where the relevant issue is delisted; 

65 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
3.  Case  where  the  liquidity  provision  agreement  pursuant  to  [§20-3]  of  the 

Regulation was concluded and is in force; and 

4.  Other cases that the Exchange deems necessary for market management. 

(4) In cases where the market-making for a market-making is terminated according to a 
market-making  agreement,  the  market  maker  cannot  submit  quotations  of  the  relevant 
issue  through  the  market-making  account  after  the  date  of  termination.  Provided  that, 
where a market-making agreement has newly been entered into for the same issue before 
the market-making agreement expires, this provision shall not apply thereto. (Amended 
on November 28, 2019) 

(5) The Exchange may newly enter into a market-making agreement with other market 
makers for an issue of which market-making agreement has been terminated pursuant to 
paragraph  (2)  or  for  an  issue  which  has  not  been  allocated  as  a  market-making  issue 
pursuant  to  [§31-15(4)],  as  stipulated  by  the  Exchange  separately.  Provided  that  this 
provision shall not apply to the case where the remaining period from the effective date 
of  the  termination  of  the  market-making  agreement  to  the  expiry  date  of  the  previous 
market-making  agreement  is  shorter  than  two  (2)  months.  (Amended  on  February  28, 
2017) 

[March 25, 2016] 

§31-17. Obligation to maintain Market-making Quotations 

(1) Pursuant to [§20-10] of the Regulation, a market maker shall maintain the market-
making  quotations  in  the  manner  of  satisfying  all  the  requirements  under  each  of  the 
following subparagraphs. In such cases, the quotations that have been submitted during 
the  hours  for  the  trading  by  the  method  of  continuous  auction  under  [§24]  of  the 
Regulation  shall  be  deemed  as  having  been  submitted  to  perform  the  obligation  of 
maintaining market-making quotations, notwithstanding [§31-12(2)]. 

1. Quotations shall be maintained on both of offer and bid sides; 

2.The figure, which is obtained from dividing the difference between the price of an 
offer quotation and the price of a bid quotation of a market maker by the quotation 
price unit (hereinafter referred to as the “quotation price unit spread”), shall be within 
the obligatory spread that  is  determined in the market-making  agreement.  Provided 
that, in cases where the obligation to maintain market-making quotations on either side 
of bid or offer is exempted and the quotation situation falls under any of the following 
items, the figure specified in the relevant item shall be deemed as the quotation price 
unit spread: 

(a) Where there is a quotation on one side: The figure that is obtained from dividing 
the difference between the price of the best quotation on one side and the price of 
the market-making quotation on the other side by the quotation price unit; and 

66 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(b)  Where  there  is  no  quotation  on  one  side:  The  figure  that  is  obtained  from 
dividing the difference between the price of the best quotation on the other side and 
the price of the market-making quotation on the other side by the quotation price 
unit. 

3.  The  sum  of  the  amount  of  offer  market-making  quotations  and  the  sum  of  the 
amount of bid  market-making quotations  shall be at  least  the minimum  amount  for 
quotation maintenance specified in the market-making agreement, respectively. 

(2)  “Cases  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§20-10(1)]  of  the 
Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  cases  falling  under  each  of  the  following  subparagraphs: 
(Amended on November 28, 2019) 

1. Where it is within three (3) minutes after the market opening; 

2. Where it is the quotation receiving hours when the prices are determined by  call 
auction under [§23] of the Regulation; 

3.  Where  there  are  only  the  bid  quotations  at  the  upper  limit  price  or  the  offer 
quotations at the lower limit price for the relevant market-making issue; 

4.  When  the  value  of  trades  of  the  relevant  market-making  issue  concluded  by  the 
market-making quotations during a day exceeds 50/100 of the average daily trading 
value  {limited  to  the  value  of  traded  concluded  during  the  trading  hours  of  regular 
sessions by the methods of individual auction under [§23(1)2,3 & 5] of the Regulation 
and [§24] of the Regulation} during the assessment period specified in [Annex 2-2], 
where it is the period from such time to the time of market closing of the day; 

5. Where the relevant market-making issue was designated as an investment caution 
issue pursuant to [§5-2] of the Market Oversight Regulation, or as an investment alert 
issue or an investment risk issue pursuant to [§5-3] of the same Regulation; 

6. Where the relevant market-making issue was designated as an administrative issue; 

7. Where it is from the time when a cause for delisting has occurred to the relevant 
market-making issue to the time when the cause was resolved; and 

8. Other cases where the Exchange deems it is difficult to submit the market-making 
quotations due to the system failure, etc. 

[March 25, 2016] 

(3) Notwithstanding paragraph (1) above, if deemed necessary by the Exchange due to 
sudden changes in market conditions, etc., the obligatory spread under subparagraph 2 of 
the same paragraph may be widened, or the minimum amount for quotation maintenance 
under subparagraph 3 of the same paragraph may be reduced. [March 25, 2020] 

67 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§31-18. Exceptions in Obligation to maintain Two-sided Market-making Quotations 

Pursuant to [§20-10(2)] of the Regulation, in cases when a market maker falls under each 
of the following subparagraphs, the market maker may not be obligated to maintain either 
a  bid  or  offer  quotation  in  accordance  with  the  provisions  of  the  relevant 
subparagraph:(Amended on November 28, 2019) 

1. In the case of a bid quotation falling under any of the following items: 

(a)  Where  the  balance  held  (excluding  the  quantity  held  by  borrowing)  for  the 
relevant market-making issue exceeds 2/1000 of the number of listed stocks or the 
amount of balance held (referring to the amount calculated by multiplying the most 
recent price by the balance held excluding the quantity held by borrowing) exceeds 
KRW 100 million; 

(b)  Where  the  quantity,  which  is  calculated  by  subtracting  the  balance  held  of  a 
market maker from the number of listed stocks of the relevant market-making issue, 
falls  short  of  the  minimum  quotation  quantity  (referring  to  the  quantity  that  is 
needed to meet the minimum quantity for quotation maintenance specified in the 
market-making  agreement  pursuant  to  the  criteria  of  [Annex  2-4];  the  same 
hereinafter in this Article); and 

(c) Where the price difference between the best offer quotation and the lower limit 
price of the day is within the scope of obligatory spread specified in the  market-
making agreement. 

2. In the case of an offer quotation that falls under any of the following items: 

(a) [Deleted on November 28, 2019] 

(b) Where the balance held of a market maker for the relevant market-making issue 
falls short of the minimum quotation quantity; and 

(c) Where the price difference between the best bid quotation and the upper limit 
price of the day is within the scope of obligatory spread specified in the  market-
making agreement. 

[March 25, 2016] 

§31-19. Management of Balance of Market-making Account 

(1) Pursuant to [§20-10(2)] of the Regulation, a market maker shall report to the Exchange 
the number of stocks of each market-making issue held in the market-making account as 
of  the  day  before  the  starting  date  for  market-making  specified  in  the  market-making 
agreement, on the starting date for market-making in accordance with [Annex: Form No. 

68 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2-7].  Provided  that,  this  provision  shall  not  apply  to  the  issue  for  which  the  market-
making agreement has been entered into for the first time. 

(2) Market makers shall report the changes in quantity and the balance held in market-
making  accounts  for  each  market-making  issue  to  the  Exchange  in  accordance  with 
[Annex: Form 2-7] from the date of commencement of the market-making by the time of 
market opening on the following trading day. (Amended on November 28, 2019) 

(3) In cases where it needs to make corrections to the contents of the report made pursuant 
to paragraph (2), market makers shall report the corrections by 12:00 noon on the day 
which includes the reporting deadline. (Amended on November 28, 2019) 

(4) The Exchange shall manage the quantities reported by market makers for each market-
making issue pursuant to the provisions of paragraphs (1) through (3) as the daily balance 
held of the relevant market-making issue. [November 28, 2019] 

[March 25, 2016] 

§31-20. Assessment, etc. Of Market Makers 

(1)  Pursuant  to  [§20-11(2)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  Exchange  may  make  assessment  of 
each market maker on a quarterly basis for each market-making issue in accordance with 
the  assessment  criteria  under  [Annex  2-4]  on  the  extent  to  which  the  obligation  to 
maintain  market-making  quotations  was  fulfilled  and  the  activeness  in  market-making 
activities,  etc.  (hereinafter  referred 
the  “assessment  of  market-making 
to  as 
performance”). Provided that, this provision shall not be applicable to the market-making 
issues  of which  the number of days for obligatory  market-making is  less than five (5) 
during the relevant quarter. 

(2) The Exchange may notify the relevant market maker of the result of assessment of 
his/her market-making performance. 

(3)  The  Exchange  may  request  a  market  maker  to  submit  materials  that  are  deemed 
necessary for the assessment of market-making performance. In such cases, the market 
maker shall comply with the request without delay. 

(4) Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraph (1), in the case of each of the following 
subparagraphs, the assessment of the market-making performance may not be conducted. 
[December 6, 2018] 

1.  Where  it  is  necessary  to  be  excluded  from  the  assessment  of  the  market-making 
performance  for  a  certain  period  in  order  to  secure  a  preliminary  test  period  for 
participating  as  a  market  maker,  and  such  period  is  specified  in  the  market-making 
agreement; and 

2. Where a market maker who has failed to submit market-making quotations for any 
reasons  that are not  attributable to  the market  maker’s intent  or negligence, such as 

69 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
compliance with related statutes and internal control procedures, computer problems, 
market  fluctuation,  etc.  requests  the  Exchange  to  exclude  it  from  the  assessment  of 
market-making performance by specifying the reason and the exclusion period, and the 
Exchange recognizes it necessary.   

[March 25, 2016] 

§31-21. Suspension of Market Maker’s Qualification 

(1) Pursuant to [§20-11(2)] of the Regulation, in cases where a market maker falls under 
the criteria for suspension of qualifications stipulated in [Annex 2-4] as a result of the 
assessment of market-making performance, the Exchange may suspend the qualification 
of the relevant market maker. 

(2) The Exchange shall not designate the person whose qualification as a market maker 
has been suspended pursuant to paragraph (1) as a market maker for one (1) year period 
from the month following the month in which the suspension date falls. 

[March 25, 2016] 

§31-22. Payments to Market Makers 

(1) Pursuant to §20-11(2)] of the Regulation, the Exchange may make payments to market 
makers  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “payment  for  market-making”)  as  stipulated  in 
[Annex  2-4]  differentially  reflecting  the  results  of  assessment  of  market-making 
performance during the term of market-making agreement. Provided that the criteria on 
the  payments  for  market-making  may  be  set  differently  when  the  Exchange  deems  it 
necessary. (Amended on September 7, 2017) 

(2) The Exchange shall make  the payments for  market-making in  accordance with the 
time for making the payments specified in [Annex 2-4] after the end of the quarter when 
the assessment of market-making performance was conducted. (Amended on February 
28, 2017) 

[March 25, 2016] 

Section 3. Units of Quotation and Trading Quantity 

§32. Quotation Unit 

(1) The quotation quantity units under [§21] of the Regulation shall be the quantity under 
each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on August 26, 2005; February 3, 2009; 
July 16, 2009; September 2, 2014; December 22, 2022) 

70 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. For stocks: one (1) share;   

2. For DRs of foreign stocks: one (1) certificate;   

3.  For  collective  investment  securities  of  ETFs:  one  (1)  share  (for  the  beneficiary 
certificates of ETFs investment trust: one (1) unit; the same hereinafter); 

3-2. For ETNs: one (1) share   

4. For subscription right certificates: one (1) certificate;   

5. For subscription warrants: one (1) warrant;   

5-2. For ELWs: one (1) warrant; and   

6. For beneficiary certificates: one (1) unit.   

(2) The quotation price units under [§21] of the Regulation shall be the quantity under 
each of the following subparagraphs.: (Amended on May 13, 2005;  February 3, 2009; 
July 16, 2009; July 29, 2010; September 2, 2014; December 22, 2022; October 17, 2023)   

1.  For  stocks,  DRs  of  foreign  stocks,  subscription  right  certificates,  subscription 
the  following 

warrants,  and  beneficiary  certificates:  Price  specified 
subparagraphs   

in 

(a)  For  an  issue  of  which  the  price  per  share  (including  the  price  per  certificate, 
warrant and unit: the same hereinafter in this Article) is less than KRW 2,000: 
KRW 1. 

(b) For an issue of which the price per share is higher than or equal to KRW 2,000, 

but less than KRW 5,000: KRW 5;   

(c)  For an issue of which the price per share is higher than or equal to KRW 5,000, 

but less than KRW 20,000: KRW 10;   

(d) For an issue of which the price per share is higher than or equal to KRW 20,000, 

but less than KRW 50,000: KRW 50; 

(e)  For an issue of which the price per share is higher than or equal to KRW 50,000, 

but less than KRW 200,000: KRW 100;   

(f)  For an issue of which the price per share is higher than or equal to KRW 200,000, 

but less than KRW 500,000: KRW 500; and 

(g) For an issue of which the price per share is higher than or equal to KRW 500,000: 

KRW 1,000. 

2.  For  collective  investment  securities  of  ETFs  and  ETNs:  Price  specified  in  the 

following subparagraphs 

(a)  For an issue of which the price per share is less than KRW 2,000: KRW 1. 
(b) For an issue of which the price per share is higher than or equal to KRW 2,000: 

KRW 5.   

71 

 
 
 
 
 
 
   
 
 
 
 
 
 
3.  For ELWs: KRW 5.

72 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Section 4. Execution of Trades 

§34. Priority of Simultaneous Quotations 

(1) Pursuant to the part other than each subparagraph of [§22(3)] of the Regulation, among 
the  simultaneous  quotations,  the  quotations  with  larger  quantities  shall  have  a  priority 
over  the  quotations  with  smaller  quantities  (in  the  case  of  quotations  with  the  same 
quantity, the quotation received earlier by the Exchange computer system has a priority) 
until the quotation quantity reaches to the quantity under following subparagraph 1. In 
such case, for the quotations of which quantities exceed the quantity under subparagraph 
1,  the  priority  shall  be  applied  in  a  sequential  order  from  subparagraph  2  in  the  same 
manner as stated in the former part. (Amended on December 22, 2022) 

1. 100 times the trading unit;   
2. 1/2 of the residual quantity. In such cases, the quantity below the trading unit shall 
be rounded to the trading unit; and   
3. The total residual quantity.   

(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), for ETF collective investment securities, ETNs and 
ELWs,  quotations  for  customer  account  transactions  shall  have  a  priority  over  the 
quotations for the self-account transactions.  In such case, in applying paragraph 1, the 
priority  is  applied  between  quotations  for  customer  account  transactions  and  between 
quotations for self-account transactions. (Amended on December 22, 2022) 

(3) The priorities among simultaneous quotations under paragraphs (1) and (2) shall apply 
until the point of time under each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on March 
19, 2009; April 12, 2023) 

1. In the case of a bid quotation placed at the upper limit price or an offer quotation 
placed  at  the  lower  limit  price  noted  in  [§22(3)]  of  the  Regulation,  until  the  whole 
quantity thereof is executed; 

2. In the case of the market quotation noted in [§22(3)] of the Regulation, until the time 
such quotation price is regarded as a price other than the upper limit price or the lower 
limit price; and   

3. In the case of the quotation at the highest or lowest price of an issue using the first 
trading price as the base price pursuant to [§22(3)] of the Regulation, until the time 
when  the  first  trading  price  pursuant  to  [§37(1)]  of  the  Regulation  is  determined. 
Provided that, in cases where that first trading price is the lowest price of quotation 
price  unit,  it  shall  be  until  the  entire  quantity  of  offer  quotations  with  the  lowest 
quotation price is executed. 

§35. Range of Quotations Participating in Call Auctions, etc. 

(1)  The  range  of  quotations  to  be  included  in  call  auction  pursuant  to  [§23(2)]  of  the 

73 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Regulation  shall  be  the  quotations  received  during  each  of  the  hours  specified  in  the 
following  subparagraphs  and  during  the  time  which  the  Exchange  randomly  specifies 
within thirty (30) seconds since then, and shall include the quotations received earlier, but 
not yet executed, if there are any.: (Amended on July 25, 2007; June 24, 2014; May 19, 
2015; December 22, 2022) 

1. In the case of determining the price pursuant to [§23(1)1] of the Regulation, from 
the beginning of the quotation receiving hours of the regular session mentioned in [§11] 
to the market opening time; Provided that, in the case of being applied with [§26-2(1)2], 
it shall be until the time extended for 2 minutes from the point of market opening; 

2. In the case of determining the price pursuant to [§23(1)2&3] of the Regulation, for 
the first ten (10) minutes from the time of reopening of the market or resumption of 
trading. Provided that, in cases where, in view of such factors as the quotation condition, 
the  extension  of  the  relevant  period  is  deemed  necessary,  it  may  be  the  period 
determined by the Exchange; 

3. In the case of price determination pursuant to [§23(1)4] of the Regulation, for the 
last  ten  (10)  minutes  before  the  market  closing,  and  in  cases  where  the  time  of  the 
market reopening or trading resumption pursuant to subparagraph 2 is within the last 
twenty  (20) minutes before the market  closing time, from such point of time to  the 
market closing time. Provided that, in the case of being applied with [§26-2(1)], it shall 
be until the time extended for 2 minutes from the point of market closing; and 

4. In the case of price determination pursuant to [§23(1)5] of the Regulation (excluding 
the case where the relevant price falls under [§23(1)1&4]), for the two (2) minutes from 
the time when the trade execution method is changed. Provided that, in cases where the 
periodic call auction to determine the prices  at the time of market close pursuant to 
subparagraph 3 has started before passing two (2) minutes from the time when the trade 
execution  method  is  changed,  it  shall  be  until  ten  (10)  minutes  before  the  market 
closing, but the quotation received during that time shall be deemed to be the quotation 
participated in deciding the price pursuant to [§23(1)4]. 

(2) Pursuant to the proviso to [§23(1)] of the Regulation, in the case where the price of 
each subparagraph (excluding subparagraph 4) of the same paragraph is not determined 
with the quotations noted in paragraph (1), the price shall be determined by switching to 
continuous trading specified in [§24] of the Regulation. [December 22, 2022] (Amended 
on February 25, 2025)   

§36. Base Prices Used for Determination of Prices at Call Auctions 

The “prices determined in the Enforcement Rule” in the proviso to the part other than 
each subparagraph of [§23(5)] of the Regulation shall be each of followings: (Amended 
August 26, 2005; January 27, 2011; September 2, 2014; December 10, 2014, November 
26, 2020; April 12, 2023; February 27, 2025) 

1. In the case of determining the first trading price of the issues using the first trading 

74 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
price  as  the  base  price,  if  there  is  a  price  equal  to  the  appraisal  price  determined 
pursuant to [§30(1)3] and [Annex 1], such appraisal price; and, if there is no price equal 
to the appraisal price, the price closest to such appraisal price;   

2. In the case of determining the first trading price of issues falling under subparagraphs 
2, 4, 5, and 6 of [§30(1)] and [§30(4)], if there is a price equal to the base price, such 
base price; and if there is no price equal to base price, the price closest to the base price; 
and   

3. In the case of determining the first trading price of issues listed as a subscription 
right certificate, subscription warrant, and ELW, the simple arithmetic average of the 
highest  and lowest  prices.  In such cases, if such price  does  not  match the quotation 
price unit, it shall be the price closest to such price, among the prices that are higher 
than such price and that match the quotation  price unit.  (Amended on  February 27, 
2025)   

§37. Range of Quotations Excluded from Determination of Special Quotations 

Pursuant to the [§23(7)] of the Regulation, in cases where the trading does not resume 
during the day after having been halted or suspended during the quotation receiving hours 
under  each  subparagraph  of  [§35(1)],  no  quotations  received  during  the  day  shall 
participate in the determination of special quotations. (Amended on December 22, 2022) 
(Wholly amended on March 19, 2009) 

§38. [Deleted on May 19, 2015] 

§39. Trading Halt, etc. in Stock Market, etc. 

(1) The “cases specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to the part of [§25(1) 
other than each subparagraph] shall refer to the cases falling under any of the following 
subparagraphs, and in this case, the trading in the stock market, etc. shall not be halted. 
[May 19, 2015] 

    1. In applying [§25(1)2], case where it does not fall by 1% or more from the KOSPI at 
the time of the trading halt under [§25(1)1], or where, though it does fall by 1% or 
more, it does not last for one (1) minute; and 

2. In applying [§25(1)3], case where it does not fall by 1% or more from the KOSPI at 
the time of the trading halt under [§25(1)2], or where, though it does fall by 1% or 
more, it does not last for one (1) minute.   

(2) The trading halt under [§25(1)1&2] of the Regulation shall apply only to the cases 
where the trading falls under the halt criteria for the first time in a trading day, and the 
trading shall not be halted during the last forty (40) minutes before the market closing 
time. Provided that the halt or conclusion of the trading under [§25(1)3] shall apply during 
the last forty (40) minutes before the market closing time. (Amended on May 19, 2015) 

75 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(3) In cases where trading cannot be resumed because the computer system failure has 
occurred just before the trading resumption, the trading shall be resumed at the time when 
the computer system is fully recovered from such failure.   

(4) The trading halt for one (1) minute under [§25(1)1] of the Regulation shall start and 
calculate from one (1) minute after the market opening. [November 26, 2020]

§41-2. Change of Trade Execution Methods by Issue 

(1) “Rates specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§26-2(1)1] shall be as noted in each 
of the following subparagraphs. Provided that, in applying subparagraphs 1 through 3, 
the rates of 3% and 6% shall be adjusted to 2% and 4% respectively for the quotation 
receiving hours for the determination of closing prices, and, in the case of the quotation 
receiving hours for the determination of closing prices of underlying assets (in the case 
of stock indices, it refers to the constituents of the relevant index; the same hereinafter in 
this  Article)  on  the  last  trading  day  of  the  futures  or  options  in  the  equity  derivatives 
markets under [§3(2)1] of the Derivatives Market Business Regulation, the rates of 2% 
and  4%  shall  be  adjusted  to  1%  for  the  relevant  underlying  assets.  (Amended  on 
September 2, 2014; May 19, 2015; September 7, 2017; July 11, 2019; October 13, 2022) 

1. Stocks 

(a) For KOSPI 200 constituents: 3% 

(b) For other issues: 6% 

2. Collective investment securities of ETFs and ETNs 

(a)Where the changes in KOSPI 200, KOSPI 100 (referring to a stock price index 
that is calculated by the Exchange based on the market capitalization method where 
the index for the top 100 issues in descending order of market capitalization from 
among the KOSPI 200 constituents as of the base date falling on January 4, 2000 is 
put at 1,000 points; the same hereinafter), KOSPI 50 (referring to a stock price index 
that is calculated by the Exchange based on the market capitalization method where 
the index for the top 50 issues in descending order of market capitalization from 
among the KOSPI 200 constituents as of the base date falling on January 4, 2000 is 
put  at  1,000  points;  the  same  hereinafter),  KRX  100  (referring  to  a  market 
capitalization  weighted  stock  price  index  based  on  100  issues,  from  among  the 

77 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
stocks listed on the KOSPI Market and the stocks listed on the KOSDAQ Market, 
which is calculated by the Exchange using the base index of 1,000 on the base date 
of  January  2,  2001;  the  same  hereinafter),  indices  composed  only  of  debt 
securities (including indices that are deemed similar thereto by the Exchange), 
and  securities  pursuant  to  Article  4-52,  Paragraph  (1)  of  the  Regulations  on 
Financial  Investment  Business  and  the  derivatives  that  use  the  relevant 
securities as underlying assets are linked to one (1x) time or less (including the 
cases  where  indices  are  linked  in  the  negative  direction):  3%  (Amended  on 
April 27, 2026) 

(b)Where other prices or indices are linked: 6% 

3. For DRs of foreign stocks and beneficiary certificates: 6% 

(2)  “Rates  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  of  [§26-2(1)2]  shall  refer  to  10% 
respectively for stocks, ETFs, ETNs, DRs of foreign stocks and beneficiary certificate. 
[May19, 2015] 

(3) The change of trade  execution methods, etc.  noted in  [§26-2(1)] of the Regulation

2 and 3 of [§23(1)] of the Regulation when resuming the halted or suspended trading

§41-3. Public Announcement on Changes of Trade Execution Methods etc. by Issue 

(1) In cases where it has changed the trade execution methods, etc. pursuant to [§26-2(1) 
& (3)] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall officially announce such fact immediately. 
(Amended on May 19, 2015) 

(2)  In making the public announcement pursuant  to  paragraph  (1), the Exchange shall 
include the name of issue, the timing of the change or release therefrom and the details of 
the change of the trade execution methods, etc. in the announcement. 

[June 24, 2014] 

79 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§42. Methods of Trade Execution in Case of Computer System Failures 

(1) Pursuant  to  [§27] of the Regulation, in cases  where a  computer system  failure has 
been confirmed and it is deemed that the system failure is likely to continue, the Exchange 
may take any of the following measures: (Amended on February 28, 2014; January 15, 
2026) 

    1. Cancellation of quotations that caused computer system failure; or [January 15, 2026] 

    2.  Suspension  of  receiving  quotations  (referring  to  the  suspension  of  receiving  new 
quotations, correction quotations, and cancellation quotations; the same hereinafter) or 
halt of trading. In this case, if the restoration of details of quotations is impossible or it 
is necessary to promptly recover from a computer system failure, quotations that have 
not been concluded by the time of suspension of receiving quotations or halt of trading 
may be cancelled. [January 15, 2026] 

(2) When the computer system is back to normal operation after the quotation receiving 
was suspended or trading was halted pursuant to paragraph (1)2, the receipt of quotations 
or trading shall resume from the time determined by the Exchange. In such cases, if the 
quotations and trade details cannot be recovered due to natural disasters or for inevitable 
reasons that are comparable to natural disasters, restoration may proceed except for such 
areas. [February 28, 2014] (Amended on January 15, 2026) 

(3) In cases where the failure of the member computer system continues for an extended 
period of time and it is expected that the member system would not be recovered well 
after the market closing, or failure of the member computer system has occurred during 
the last thirty (30) minutes before the market closing time and it is unlikely that the system 
would be back to normal operation before the market closing, the Exchange may close 
the day’s trading at the time when such failure occurs.   

(4) In cases where the Exchange computer system is not back to normal operation for an 
extended period of time, the receipt of quotation or trading may be resumed by using a 
backup system. Provided that, when it is deemed that the execution of trade by the use of 
backup system is difficult due to the failure of such backup system, the day’s trading may 
be closed at the time when such system failure occurs.   

(5) The first trading price, when trading is resumed pursuant to the foreparts of paragraphs 
(2) and (4), shall be determined by the method of call auction. In such cases, the range of 
quotations participating to determine the relevant price shall be decided by the Exchange 
at each time. (Amended on February 28, 2014) 

(6)  In  cases  of  computer  system  failure  other  than  those  mentioned  in  paragraphs  (1) 
through (5), the method of executing trades shall be those determined by the Exchange at 
each time such failure occurs. (Amended on February 28, 2014) 

§43. Methods of Trade Execution of Excessively Quoted Issues 

80 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(1) [Deleted February 28, 2014]] 

(2) [Deleted February 28, 2014] 

(3) Pursuant to [§27] of the Regulation, in cases where there is a possibility of a computer 
system failure due to excessive influx of quotations, the Exchange may take any of the 
following measures: (Amended on February 28, 2014; January 15, 2026) 

    1. Suspension of receiving quotations or halt of trading. In this case, if the restoration 
of details of quotations is impossible or there is a risk of computer system failure during 
restoration,  quotations  that  have  not  been  concluded  by  the  time  of  suspension  of 
receiving quotations or halt of trading may be cancelled; or [January 15, 2026] 

    2. Closing of trading of the day. [January 15, 2026]   

(4) If the Exchange determines that the computer system is back to normal operation and 
the  risk  of  computer  system  failure  due  to  excessive  influx  of  quotations  has  been 
eliminated following the suspension of receiving quotations or the halt of trading under 
paragraph (3)1, the receiving of quotations or trading shall resume at a time determined 
by the Exchange. [February 28, 2014] (Amended on January 15, 2026) 

(5)  In  the  case  where  trading  is  resumed  pursuant  to  paragraph  (4),  [§42(4)]  of  the 
Regulation shall apply to the determination of the first price mutatis mutandis. [February 
28, 2014] (Amended on January 15, 2026) 

(6) In cases where trading is closed due to the excessive influx of quotations during the 
quotation  receiving  hours  for  call  auction,  the  trading  may  be  executed,  taking  into 
account the quotation conditions, with the quotations received until the time when such 
trading is closed.   

(7) Provisions of [§42(6)] shall apply mutatis mutandis to the method of executing trade 
of excessively quoted issues. (Amended February 28, 2014) 

§44. Extent of Correction of Transaction Errors 

Transaction errors under [§28] of the Regulation shall be classified into either transaction 
errors made by the Exchange or transaction errors made by a member, and the extent of 
correction thereof shall be each of the followings: (Amended on December 22, 2022) 

1. For the errors made by the Exchange: Transactions where the details of trade are not 
consistent with the details of quotations, which resulted from an error caused by system 
failure, failure in program execution or an error occurred in the course of inputting the 
details of trade execution; and   

2. For the errors made by members: Transactions where the details are not consistent 
with the details of orders, which resulted from an error caused while processing the 
orders received from customers, inputting such order details into the member’s system 

81 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
or transmitting the quotation details to the Exchange computer system. In such case, if 
there is an error of an overseas affiliate, etc. of a member in the course of the member’s 
receiving of customers’ orders of the overseas affiliates, etc., this error is considered 
as an error of the member.   

§45. Methods of Correcting Transaction Errors 

(1) The Exchange shall correct the transaction errors by each of the following methods. 
(Amended on June 21, 2016) 

1. In the case of transaction errors made by the Exchange:   

If it is possible, the Exchange shall correct the transaction details according to the 
original quotation information, and in other cases, the correction shall be made after 
having the member to take over the relevant trade as a self-account transaction; and   

2. In the case of transaction errors made by a member: 

In the case of errors relating to the issue, quantity, price or sell/buy classification, 
such errors shall be corrected after the relevant member took over the relevant trade 
as a self-account transaction, and in cases of the errors relating to classification of 
the  customer  account  transaction  and  self-account  transaction  resulted  from  such 
causes  as  the  breakdown  in  program  execution,  the  correction  shall  be  made  as 
required.  Provided  that,  this  provision  shall  not  apply  to  the  case  of  large-scale 
transaction errors specified in [§47-2]. 

(2) When taking over the issue pursuant to paragraph (1), in case of a member who have 
not obtained business permit for investment dealing business, it shall be accomplished by 
way of such member entrusting the trade as a self-account transaction to another member. 
(Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(3) In the case of the transaction errors made by a member, the correction shall be made 
only in cases where the relevant member submits to the Exchange a request for correction 
of  transaction  error  according  to  [Annex:  Form  No.  3],  via  the  electronic  information 
delivery medium chosen separately by the Exchange by the time of market closing on the 
following  trading  day.  (Amended  on  July  7,  2006;  August  3,  2009;  June  21,  2016; 
November 28, 2019)   

§46. Agreement for Correction of Transaction Errors 

In correcting an error made by the Exchange, the Exchange shall enter into an agreement 
with its members in accordance with [Annex: Form No. 4], in order to process the portion 
of a trade where an error has occurred as the relevant member’s self-account transaction.   

§47. Settlement of Profits and Losses 

(1) In cases where transaction errors are corrected by letting the relevant member to take 

82 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
over the relevant issue as its self-account transactions, the Exchange shall settle any profit 
or loss incurred in the course of error correction.   

(2) Securities transaction tax, all commissions, and the amount equivalent to member fees 
relating  to  the correction of transaction errors shall be counted as a loss when settling 
profits and losses pursuant to paragraph (1).   

(3) The Exchange shall settle all profits and losses without delay, upon receiving the bills 
for settlement of transaction errors in  accordance with the agreement for correction of 
transaction  errors.  Provided  that,  of  the  transaction  errors  made  by  the  Exchange,  the 
profits and losses incurred due to the errors made by the company operating the Exchange 
computer system shall be settled separately.   

§47-2. Requirements for Relief of Large-scale Transaction Errors 

The “transactions that meet the requirements stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the 
main sentence of [§28-2(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to the trades that satisfy all of 
the requirements under each of the following subparagraphs for each account (hereinafter 
referred to as the “large-scale transaction errors”). (Amended on February 28, 2017) 

1. It shall not be a trade that was executed by the method of call auction under [§23] of 
the Regulation; 

2. It shall not be a trade that was executed by the market-making quotations; 

3. The time period between the first occurrence and the conclusion of the trade shall be 
within thirty (30) minutes; 

4. Out of the issues with transaction errors of the relevant account, there shall be one 
(1) or more of issues of which execution price falls under each of the following items 
(hereinafter referred to as the “issues subject to relief”): 

(a) In the case of having purchased by error: The price that went up by over ten (10) 
percent (in the case of ELWs, 15/100; the same hereinafter in this subparagraph and 
[§47-4(3)]), compared to the most recent price immediately before the execution of 
the relevant trade (in cases where there is no most recent price, it shall be the first 
execution price and shall hereinafter be referred to as the “base price for the relief of 
transaction errors”); and 

(b) In the case of having sold by error: The price that went down by over ten (10) 
percent, compared to the base price for the relief of transaction errors. 

5.  The  sum  of  the  amounts  obtained  by  multiplying  the  difference  between  the 
execution price of the issue with transaction errors of the relevant account and the base 
price for the relief of transaction errors (referring to the amount obtained by subtracting 
the selling execution price from the base price for the relief of transaction errors or the 

83 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
amount obtained by subtracting the base price for the relief of transaction errors from 
the  buying  execution  price)  by  the  execution  quantity  of  the  relevant  trade  shall  be 
KRW 10 billion or more. In such cases, the sum shall be calculated by each of the stock 
market, the collective investment securities of ETFs market, the ETN market, the ELW 
market and the beneficiary certificate market; 

6. The trades shall continuously be executed by same kind of errors; and 

7. Additionally, there shall be a need for relief of the trades for the reliable and efficient 
settlement. 

[June 21, 2016] 

§47-3. Requesting for Relief of Large-scale Transaction Errors 

(1) Any member intending to request for relief of large-scale transaction errors pursuant 
to  [§28-2(2)]  of  the  Regulation  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “request  for  relief”) 
(including a case where the request for relief is made by the customer who caused the 
large-scale transaction errors) shall make the request for relief by way of inputting the 
details of the relevant large-scale transaction errors into the Exchange computer system 
via the member computer system or the member securities terminals. Provided that, in 
the case of emergencies including system failures, etc., the request for relief may be made 
by way of submitting are quest prepared in accordance with [Annex: Form No. 5] to the 
Exchange. 

(2) The request for relief shall be made within thirty (30) minutes from the time when the 
large-scale  transaction  errors  occurred.  Provided  that  the  Exchange  may  extend  the 
deadline for the request in cases that are deemed unavoidable including member computer 
system failures, etc. 

(3)  The  member  who  has  made  the  request  for  relief  shall  submit  the  explanatory 
materials concerning the large-scale transaction errors to the Exchange without delay. 

(4) In cases where some of the details of the request for relief are omitted or the details 
of the relevant explanatory materials are deemed insufficient, the Exchange may require 
resubmission. 

(5) When receiving the request for relief from a member, the Exchange shall make public 
the fact of receiving the relevant request for relief, etc. without delay and shall notify such 
fact to the counter party member. 

[June 21, 2016] 

§47-4. Methods of Relieving Large-scale Transaction Errors 

(1) Pursuant to [§28-2(2)] of the Regulation, after reviewing the details of the request for 

84 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
relief and the explanatory materials, the Exchange may relieve the large-scale transaction 
errors, in cases of satisfying all of the requirements noted in each of the subparagraphs of 
[§47-2]. 

(2) The Exchange shall  make the decision on whether or not to  relieve the large-scale 
transaction errors by 17:00 hours on the next trading day of the day when the request for 
relief was received (hereinafter referred to as the “date of the request for relief”) and make 
it public without delay and shall notify it to the member who requested for the relief and 
the  counter  party  member.  The  relevant  member  shall,  in  cases  where  the  large-scale 
transaction errors occurred from customer account transactions, notify it to the relevant 
customer without delay. 

(3) When it was decided to relieve the large-scale transaction errors, the Exchange may 
change the settlement prices of the issues subject to relief between the Exchange and the 
clearing member to the prices noted in each of the following subparagraphs: 

1. In the case of having bought by error: The price (if this price does not match the 
quotation price unit, it shall be the price closest to that price, among the prices that are 
higher than that price and that match the quotation price unit) that is ten (10) percent 
higher  than  the  base  price  for  the  relief  of  transaction  errors;  and  (Amended  on 
February 27, 2025) 

2.  In  the  case  of  having  sold  by  error:  The  price  (if  this  price  does  not  match  the 
quotation price unit, it shall be the price closest to that price, among the prices that are 
lower than that price and that match the quotation price unit) that is ten (10) percent 
lower than the base price for the relief of transaction errors. (Amended on February 27, 
2025) 

(4) Notwithstanding paragraph (3), in cases where the counter party member has traded 
the issues subject to relief before the fact of receiving the member’s request for relief was 
made public pursuant to [§47-3(5)] (hereinafter referred to as the “sequential transaction”) 
and  the  relevant  trade  satisfies  all  the  requirements  noted  in  each  of  the  following 
subparagraphs, the Exchange may determine the settlement prices differently. 

1. The counter party member shall make the request for change of settlement prices to 
the Exchange in accordance with [Annex: Form No. 5-2]. In such cases, provisions of 
[§47-3(1), (3)&(4)] shall apply mutatis mutandis, but the deadline for the request shall 
be from 08:00 to 10:00 hours on the next trading day of the date of the request for relief 
stipulated in [§47-3] (the deadline for the customer’s request to the member shall be 
by the date of the request for relief); 

2. It shall be the cases of trading the issue purchased or sold as a result of the large-
scale transaction errors within the executed quantity of the relevant transaction through 
the same account, and of falling under each of the following items:   

(a) Case of having sold the issues purchased; or 

85 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(b) Case of having purchased the issues sold. 

3.  It  shall  be  a  trade  executed  by  way  of  continuous  auction  under  [§24]  of  the 
Regulation during the trading hours of the regular session. 

(5) When determining the settlement prices pursuant to paragraph (4), the Exchange shall 
consider the calculation of trading volume weighted average based on the sequence of 
trade executions and the prices specified in each of the following subparagraphs, etc.: 

1. For the case of paragraph (4)2(a), the price specified in each of the following items: 

(a) Where the execution price is lower than the price specified in paragraph (3)2, but 
higher than the execution price of large-scale transaction errors: the execution price 
(if the prices does not match the quotation price unit, it shall be the price closest to 
that  price,  among  the  prices  that  are  higher  than  that  price  and  that  match  the 
quotation price unit); and (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(b) Where the execution price is equal to or lower than the execution price of large-
scale transaction errors: the execution price of large-scale transaction errors (if this 
price does not match the quotation price unit, it shall be the price closest to that price, 
among the prices that are lower than that price and that match the quotation price 
unit). (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

2. For the case of paragraph (4)2(b), the price specified in each of the following items: 

(a)Where the execution price is higher than the price specified in paragraph (3)1, but 
lower than the execution price of large-scale transaction errors: the execution price 
(if this price does not match the quotation price unit, it shall be the price closest to 
that  price,  among  the  prices  that  are  higher  than  that  price  and  that  match  the 
quotation price unit); and (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(b)Where the execution price is equal to or higher than the execution price of large-
scale transaction errors: the execution price of large-scale transaction errors (if this 
price does not match the quotation price unit, it shall be the price closest to that price, 
among the prices that are lower than that price and that match the quotation price 
unit). (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(6) The counter party member who was notified of the receipt of the request for relief 
from  the Exchange  pursuant  to  [§47-3(5)]  shall,  if there  are  customers  who fall  under 
subparagraphs 2 and 3 or paragraph (4), notify them of the details of paragraph (4)1 on 
the date of request for relief. 

(7)  In  cases  where  the  Exchange  determines  to  relieve  large-scale  transaction  errors 
resulted from customer account transactions, the member shall calculate the settlement 
prices for the customers by applying the settlement prices that were changed pursuant to 
paragraph (3) or (5). 

86 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(8) Notwithstanding paragraphs (3) and (5), in the event that it is deemed necessary for 
the market management considering the trading and market conditions comprehensively, 
the Exchange may change the prices specified in paragraphs (3) and (5). 

(9) The Exchange shall keep the records and documents related to the relief of large-scale 
transaction errors for ten (10) years. 

[June 21, 2016] 

Section 5. Special Cases concerning Trade Execution 

§48. [Deleted July 7, 2006] 

§48-2. Regular Session Auction-based Block Trade 

(1) Pursuant to the latter part of [§30-2(1)1] of the Regulation, the guidelines to be used 
in calculation of trading volume weighted average price shall be each of the following 
subparagraphs: 

1.  It  shall  be  calculated  by  dividing  the  total  trading  value  of  relevant  issue  for  the 
period from the time of execution of relevant auction-based block trade to the market 
closing time of regular session by the total trading volume of the same period; 

2. In calculating the total trading value and trading volume noted in subparagraph 1, 
the regular session auction-based block trade, regular session block trade and regular 
session basket trade shall be excluded; and 

3. From among the amounts calculated pursuant  to subparagraph 1, the amount less 
than  KRW  1  shall  be  discarded,  but  in  cases  where  the  trading  volume  weighted 
average price is  lower than the closing price, the amount less than KRW 1 shall be 
rounded off. 

(2)  “Price  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§30-2(1)2]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the base price (including the appraisal price).   

(3) The quotations participating in the regular session auction-based block trade pursuant 
to [§30-2(3)] of the Regulation shall satisfy the quantity requirement where the amount 
obtained by multiplying the quotation quantity by the base price (the appraisal price, if 
the base price is not available) of the relevant issue is KRW 500 million or higher.   

(4) Pursuant to [§30-2(3)] of the Regulation, the trading unit of regular session auction-
based block trade shall be one-hundred (100). 

(5) Pursuant to [§30-2(3)] of the Regulation, the regular session auction-based block trade 
shall not be executed for the issues designated as administrative issue and issue scheduled 

87 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
to be delisted. 

[July 29, 2010] 

§49. Regular Session Block Trading 

(1)  The  regular  session  block  trading  pursuant  to  [§31(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be 
applied by inputting the details negotiated by the selling and buying parties, such as the 
issue,  quantity,  and  price,  in  accordance  with  any  of  the  following  subparagraphs: 
(Amended on December 22, 2022)   

    1.  Method  in  which  details  of  negotiation  are  notified  to  the  member  system  and 
Exchange  system  via  the  electronic  network  for  block  trading,  etc.  (referring  to  the 
electronic  system  operated  by  the  Exchange  for  the  purpose  of  notifying  and 
confirming the agreement or negotiated details of block trading and basket trading; the 
same  hereinafter)  and  the  member  places  the  quotations  in  accordance  with  the 
negotiated details; or   

    2.  Method  in  which  the  member  places  the  quotations  by  inputting  details  of 
negotiation to the Exchange system via the member system or the member securities 
terminal. 

(2) The provisions of [§52(2) through (7)] shall  apply  mutatis mutandis to the regular 
session block trading. (Amended on December 22, 2022)   

§50. Regular Session Basket Trading 

(1) A request for regular session basket trading pursuant to [§31(1)] of the Regulation 
shall be made by notifying the details negotiated, including the name of issue, quantity 
and price, between the selling and buying parties to the member system and the Exchange 
system  via  the  electronic  network  for  block  trading,  etc.  and  the  member  placing  the 
quotations in accordance with the negotiated details.   

(2) In making a request for regular session basket trading under paragraph (1), if there are 
no trades executed in the regular session by the individual auction methods under [§23] 
and [§24] of the Regulation until the relevant quotation was received, the quotation shall 
be made at the base price of the day. [July 11, 2019] 

(3) The provisions of [§52(3) through (7)] and [§53(2) through (4)] shall apply mutatis 
mutandis to the regular session basket trading. (Amended on July 7, 2006; July 11, 2019)   

§51. Off-hours Closing Price Trading 

(1) When applying [§34(1)] of the Regulation, in the case of the pre-hours session for an 
issue whose the previous day’s closing price does not match the quotation price unit and 
an issue that undergoes an ex-dividend, ex-right or ex-distribution on the day when the 
quotations are placed, be the closing price of the previous day shall be deemed to be the 

88 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
base price of the day. (Amended on February 3, 2009; February 27, 2025) 

(2) [Deleted February 28, 2014]   

(3) Pursuant to [§34(2)] of the Regulation, from among the quotations for the off-hours 
closing  price  trade,  a  quotation  received  earlier  shall  have  priority  over  a  quotation 
received later. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

§51-2. Off-hours Call Auction 

(1) The “cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§34-2(1)] of the 
Regulation shall refer to any of the following subparagraphs: [February 27, 2025] 

1. Issues for which no trading was made during the regular market trading hours on the   
Day; and [February 27, 2025] 

2. Issues notified by the multilateral trading company as those to be traded on the day. 
In  this  case,  KRX  may  exclude  stocks  if  it  is  unable  to  receive  notification  on  or
