confirm the stocks subject to trading at the multilateral trading company due to system 
failure, etc. [February 27, 2025] 

(2)  The  range  of  quotations  that  participate  in  the  determination  of  price  by  off-hours 
periodic call auction pursuant to [§34-2(2)] of the Regulation shall be those quotations 
received during the period from the beginning of quotation receiving hours for off-hours 
periodic call auction to the each time when ten (10) minutes have elapsed (hereinafter 
referred to as “unit-execution time in this Article, and in the case applied by [§26-2(1)1], 
it  shall  be  until  the  time  extended  for  two  (2)  minutes  after  the  unit  execution  time), 
followed by the time the Exchange randomly decides within thirty (30) seconds and when 
there are unexecuted portion of quotations received earlier, those unexecuted quotations 
shall be included. (Amended on June 24, 2014; May 19, 2015) 

(3) [Deleted on May 19, 2015] 

(4) [Deleted February 28, 2014] 

(5)  The  provision  of  [§22(2)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis  to  the 
priority of quotations for the off-hours periodic call auction pursuant to [§34-2(4)] of the 
Regulation.   

[May 13, 2005]   

§51-3. Off-hours Auction-based Block Trade 

(1)  Pursuant  to  the  latter  part  of  [§34-3(1)1]  of  the  regulation,  the  trading  volume 
weighted average price shall be calculated according to the guidelines noted in each for 
the following subparagraphs:   

89 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. It shall be calculated by dividing the total trading value of the relevant issue for the 
period from the opening time to the closing time of regular session by the total trading 
volume for the same period; and   

2. The provision of [§48-2(1)2 & 3] shall apply mutatis mutandis to off-hours auction-
based block trade.   

(2) The “price specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§34-3(1)2] of the 
Regulation shall refer to the base price.   

(3) The provisions of [§48-2(3) through (5)] shall apply mutatis mutandis to the off-hours 
auction-based block trade. 

[July 29, 2010] 

§52. Off-hours Block Trade 

(1) The off-hours block trade pursuant to [§35(1)] of the Regulation shall be applied by 
inputting the details of negotiation, such as the name of issue, quantity and price agreed 
between the buying and selling parties, in accordance with any of each item of [§49(1)] 
during the quotation receiving hours for off-hours sessions. In such cases, when a member 
receives an entrustment from a stock-listed corporation which intends to trade the treasury 
stocks by method of off-hours block trading after having obtained an approval from the 
Financial Services Commission pursuant to [§39(4)2] of the Regulation, the member shall 
submit  the  documents  proving  such  fact  before  placing  quotations.  (Amended  on 
February 3, 2009; December 22, 2022) 

(2) In the case of submitting a request pursuant to paragraph (1), either the bid or offer 
quotation shall be made by a single member, and the quotation quantity shall be at least 
5,000 times (500 times in the case of collective investment securities of ETFs and ETNs) 
the trading unit of regular session or the amount obtained by multiplying the quotation 
quantity by the share price shall be at least KRW 50 million. In the case of the trading 
between  foreigners  under  Article  6-7(1)6  of  the  Regulations  on  Financial  Investment 
Business, both of the customers entrusting bid order and offer order shall be foreigners. 
(Amended on August 28, 2008; February 3, 2009; December 30, 2009; February 28, 2014; 
May 12, 2014; September 2, 2014; January 27, 2026) 

(3) The details of negotiation determined according to the agreement between the buying 
and selling parties pursuant to paragraph (1) may be changed only in the event when both 
parties  have  consented  before  the  member  places  the  quotation  according  to  such 
negotiated details. (Amended on July 7, 2006; February 3, 2009) 

(4) Quotation price unit for off-hours block trade shall be KRW 1.   

(5) [Deleted February 28, 2014] 

(6) In cases where, due to such reasons as the failure of interface system of the electronic 

90 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
network for block trading, it is deemed difficult to submit the request for off-hours block 
trade, the member may accomplish the trade by submitting the negotiated details of off-
hours block trade by using such methods as electronic mail to the Exchange and placing 
the quotation according to the negotiated details notified. (Amended on March 19, 2009) 

(7) Notwithstanding paragraphs (1) and (6), in cases where the details of negotiation for 
off-hours block trade cannot be notified due to such reasons as the failure of the interface 
system of electronic network for block trading, the relevant off-hours block trading shall 
not be executed. (Amended on March 19, 2009) 

(8)  In  the  case  of  placing  the  quotations  for  the issues  that  their  closing prices  on  the 
previous day do not match the quotation price unit and that undergo ex-dividends, ex-
rights, share-split or reverse stock split on the day when the quotation is placed pursuant 
to the latter part of [§35(5)] of the Regulation, it shall be applied based on the base price. 
(Amended on September 8, 2006; February 3, 2009; April 20, 2012; February 28, 2017; 
February 27, 2025) 

(9) The provisions of [§57(1)1] shall apply mutatis mutandis to the cases where a member 
received an entrustment from a stock-listed corporation that intends to trade its treasury 
stocks by way of off-hours block trade (including the selling of treasury stocks by trust 
company). [September 8, 2006] (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

§53. Off-hours Basket Trade 

(1) A request for off-hours basket trading pursuant to [§36(1)] of the Regulation shall be 
made by notifying the details of negotiation, including the name of issue, quantity and 
price,  agreed  between  the  buying  and  selling  parties  to  the  member  system  and  the 
Exchange’s system via the electronic network for block trading, etc. during the quotation 
receiving hours for off-hours sessions, and the member placing the quotation according 
to such negotiated details. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(2)  In  the  case  of  making  a  request  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1),  either  side  of  the  bid 
quotation or offer quotation shall be made by a single member, and on the other side, the 
quotation for each issue comprising the basket shall have been placed by a single member. 
In  the  case  of  trading  between  foreigners  under  Article  6-7(1)6  of  the  Regulations  on 
Financial Investment Business, both of the customers entrusting bid order and offer order 
shall be foreigners. (Amended on August 28, 2008; February 3, 2009) 

(3) The same basket number shall be given to the issues comprising the same basket, and 
when a member places more than two (2) quotations for off-hours basket trade, a different 
number shall be assigned to each basket.   

(4) Pursuant to [§36(3)] of the Regulation, the number of issues comprising a basket and 
quantity requirement shall be each of the followings: (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

1. The number of issues comprising a basket shall be no less than five (5); and   

91 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2. The quantity requirement of basket shall be that the sum of the amounts, which is 
obtained by multiplying the quotation quantity of each issue comprising the basket by 
its price, is at least KRW 200 million. (Amended on January 27, 2026) 

(5) The provisions of [§52(3) through (7)] shall apply mutatis mutandis to the off-hours 
basket trade. (Amended on July 7, 2006; February 3, 2009) 

§54. Exceptions in Off-hours Trading 

In the case of falling under any of the following cases, the Exchange may not execute the 
off-hours closing price trade, off-hours call auction, off-hours auction-based block trade, 
off-hours  block  trade  and  off-hours  basket  trade  pursuant  to  [§33]  of  the  Regulation: 
(Amended on May 13, 2005; May 13, 2008; July 29, 2010; January 27, 2011; February 
28, 2014; September 2, 2014, November 26, 2020; April 12, 2023)   

1. Where the trading hours of the regular session are changed pursuant to [§8(1)1 & 2];   

2.  Where  trading  of  all  issues  is  conducted  using  the  backup  system  pursuant  to 
[§42(4)];   

3. Case of the basket trade where trading of some of the issues comprising a basket for 
off-hours basket trade is executed using the backup system;   

4. For the issues falling under any of the following items, the cases where such issue 
was traded in the pre-hours session; and   

(a) The issues using the first trading price as the base price and initially listed issues 
under [§30(1)2];   

(b)Issues, the trading of which is resumed after having been suspended;   

(c)Issue scheduled to be delisted (limited to the first trading day, except for the off-
hours auction-based block trading); and   

(d) Issues designated as administrative issue (limited to the off-hours auction-based 
block trading).   

5.  In  addition,  the  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary  for  the  market 
management.   

§55. Methods of Determining First Trading Price of Initially Listed Issues 

(1) “Issue specified in the Enforcement Rules" in [§37(1)] of the Regulation shall be an 
issue  using  the  first  trading  price  as  the  base  price:  (Amended  on  August  26,  2005; 
February 3, 2009; January 27, 2011; April 20, 2012; May 12, 2014; December 10, 2014; 
July 23, 2020)   

92 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) Pursuant to [§37(2)] of the Regulation, the range of quotations shall be the quotations 
received from  the beginning  of quotation  receiving hours of the regular  session to  the 
market  opening  time  and  the  time  randomly  set  by  the  Exchange  within  30  seconds 
thereafter. Provided that, in cases where the price is not determined with the quotations 
noted in the main clause, the price shall be determined by switching to continuous trading 
noted in [§24] of the Regulation. (Amended on February 3, 2009; December 22, 2022) 

(3)  The  quotations  noted  in  paragraph  (2)  shall  be  the  quotation  received  within  the 
following prices: (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

1. An issue using the first trading price as the base price (excluding an issue scheduled 
to be delisted); The lowest quotation price and the highest quotation price pursuant to 
[Annex 1] 

2. A newly-listed issue noted in [§30(1)2a]: The highest price limit and the lowest price 
limit pursuant to [§31(3)] 

[Wholly amended on April 12, 2023] 

§56. Methods of Executing Trade of Issues Scheduled to Be Delisted 

(1) The method of trade execution of the issues scheduled to be delisted under [§38] of 
the  Regulation  shall  be  the  call  auction.  In  such  cases,  [§23(4)  through  (6)]  of  the 
Regulation shall apply mutatis mutandis. (Amended on October 22, 2012; May 19, 2015)   

(2) The range of quotations participating in the determination of prices under paragraph 
(1) shall be the quotations received by the time when the Exchange randomly decides 
within thirty (30) seconds after each of the following time: (Amended on March 19, 2009; 
October 22, 2012; February 28, 2014; May 19, 2015, February 27, 2025) 

1. Market opening time;   

2. The unit execution times according to each of following items: 

(a)  The  time  occurring  every  thirty  (30)  minutes  from  the  market  opening  time. 
Provided that, in cases where trading is resumed pursuant to [§40(5)] of the KOSPI 
Market  Disclosure  Regulation  and  [§40(2)],  and  if  the  period  from  the  trading 
resumption time to the execution time unit is less than ten (10) minutes, it shall be 
until the next execution time unit; and         

(b) In cases where the trading has been resumed pursuant to [§6(2)] and [§25] of the 
Regulation and [§42(2)], the time occurring every thirty (30) minutes from the trade 
resumption time. Provided that, if the execution time unit is ten (10) minutes before 
the market closing time, it shall be until the market closing time. 

3. Market closing time. 

93 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(3) Notwithstanding paragraphs (1) and (2), the provisions of [§29], [§31] through [§34-
2], [§35] and [§36] of the Regulation shall apply mutatis mutandis to the trades executed 
by  the  methods  other  than  the  individual  auction  during  the  trading  hours  of  regular 
sessions. In such cases, “ten (10) minutes” in [§51-2(2)] of these Enforcement Rules shall 
be construed as “thirty (30) minutes”. Provided that [§34-2(3)], [§35(2)] and [§36(2)] of 
the Regulation shall not apply. (Amended on May 13, 2005; July 29, 2010; October 22, 
2012; May 19, 2015; February 27, 2025)   

§56-2. Trade Execution Methods, etc. of Temporary Overheated Issues, etc. 

(1)  The  method  of  trade  execution  of  temporary  overheated  issues  and  investment 
precaution issues under [§38-2] of the Regulation shall be the call auction. In such cases, 
[§23(3) through (7)] of the Regulation shall apply mutatis mutandis. (Amended on May 
19, 2015; February 28, 2017; July 23, 2020) 

(2) The provisions of [§56(2)] shall apply mutatis mutandis to the temporary overheated 
issues, investment precaution issues and the call auction issues with abnormally soaring 
price. (Amended on February 28, 2017; July 23, 2020) 

(3) Notwithstanding paragraphs (1) and (2), the provisions of [§29] through [§36] of the 
Regulation shall apply mutatis mutandis to the trades executed by the methods other than 
the individual auction during the trading hours of regular sessions. In such cases, “ten (10) 
minutes”  in  [§51-2(2)]  of  these  Enforcement  Rules  shall  be  construed  as  “thirty  (30) 
minutes.” (Amended on May 19, 2015; February 27, 2025) 

(4) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), in applying [§23(7)] of the Regulation, if the trading 
does not resume during the day after having been halted or suspended during the quotation 
receiving  hour  under  paragraph  (2),  the  quotations  restricted  to  participate  in  the 
determination of special quotation prices shall refer to the quotations received during the 
day. 

(5) The periods for changing the trade execution methods of the call auction issues with 
abnormally soaring prices shall be as follows. Provided that, in cases where it is deemed 
necessary  for  the  market  management,  the  Exchange  may  determine  such  periods 
differently: [February 28, 2017] 

1.  In  the  case  of  falling  under  [§7-2(1)1]  of  the  Enforcement  Rules  of  the  Market 
Oversight  Regulation:  Three  (3)  trading  days  from  the  day  following  the  date  of 
request; and 

2.  In  the  case  of  falling  under  [§7-2(1)2]  of  the  Enforcement  Rules  of  the  Market 
Oversight Regulation: From the day following the date of designation as investment 
risk  issue  pursuant  to  [§3-4]  of  the  Enforcement  Rules  of  the  Market  Oversight 
Regulation to the previous day of the date of release therefrom. 

(6) In cases where it is deemed necessary for the investor protection and market stability 
due to  sudden changes in the market  situation, etc., the following  additional measures 

94 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
may be taken pursuant to the proviso to the part other than subparagraphs of [§38-2] of 
the Regulation: [February 28, 2017] 

1. Change of the price change limits pursuant to [§20(2)] of the Regulation; 

2. Change of the rates specified in paragraphs (1) and (2) of [§41-2]; and 

3. Other measures that are deemed necessary for the market management. 

(7) When making changes in the trade execution methods pursuant to the part other than 
each subparagraph of paragraph (5) or taking additional measures pursuant to paragraph 
(6), the Exchange shall officially announce such fact immediately. [February 28, 2017] 

[October 22, 2012] 

§56-3. Methods of Trade Execution of Low Liquidity Issues 

(1) “An issue of which the trade frequency is deemed to be significantly low according 
to the criteria set by the Enforcement Rules” in [§38-3(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to 
an issue with low liquidity subject to period call auction that is selected according to the 
criteria specified in [Annex 2-2] (hereinafter referred to as the “low liquidity issue subject 
to call auction”). (Amended on December 28, 2018; September 22, 2020) 

(2) The trade execution of a low liquidity issue subject to call auction shall be conducted 
by the way of call  auction under [§23] of the Regulation.  Provided that this  provision 
shall not apply to an issue that falls under the criteria for exclusion under [Annex 2-2] or 
is released from the list of low liquidity issues subject to periodic call auction during the 
applicable period.   

(3) [Deleted on December 28, 2018] 

(4)  The  provisions  of  [§23(3)  through  (7)]  of  the  Regulation  and  [§56(2)]  shall  apply 
mutatis  mutandis  to  the  low  liquidity  issues  subject  to  call  auction.  (Amended  on 
November 26, 2020) 

(5) Notwithstanding paragraphs (2) and (4), the provisions of [§29] through [§36] of the 
Regulation shall apply to the trades executed by the methods other than the individual 
auction during the trading hours of regular sessions. In such cases, “ten (10) minutes” in 
[§51-2(2)] shall be construed as “thirty (30) minutes”. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(6)  The  matters  necessary  for  the  application  of  the  selection,  additional  selection, 
applicable period, etc. of the low liquidity issues subject to periodic call auction other 
than those stipulated in paragraphs (1) and (2) shall be set forth in [Annex 2-2]. (Amended 
on December 28, 2018) 

[March 25, 2016] 

§56-4.  Trade  Execution  Methods  of  Different  Classes  of  Stock  Issues  with 

95 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Insufficient Number of Listed Stocks 

(1)  “An  issue  whose  number  of  listed  stocks  falls  short  of  the  criteria  set  by  the 
Enforcement Rules” in [§38-3(2)] of the Regulation shall refer to different classes of stock 
issue with less than five hundred thousand (500,000) listed stocks (hereinafter referred to 
as the “different classes of stock issue subject to call auction”). 

(2) The number of listed stocks in paragraph (1) shall be assessed on the last trading day 
of  each  quarter,  and  in  cases  where  it  falls  under  the  criteria  in  paragraph  (1),  the 
concerned  issue  shall  be  selected  as  the  different  classes  of  stock  issue  subject  to  call 
auction during the following quarter of the quarter in which the assessment date belongs. 

(3)  The  trade  execution  method  of  the  different  classes  of  stock  issue  subject  to  call 
auction shall be the call auction pursuant to [§23] of the Regulation. 

(4) [§23(3) through (7)] of the Regulation and [§56(2)] of the Enforcement Rules shall 
apply mutatis mutandis to the different classes of stock issues subject to call auction. 

(5) Notwithstanding paragraphs (3) and (4), the provisions of [§29] through [§36] of the 
Regulation shall apply to trades other than those executed by the individual auction during 
the trading hours of regular sessions. In such cases, “ten (10) minutes” in [§51-2(2)] shall 
be construed as “thirty (30) minutes”. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(6) In cases where the low liquidity issue subject to call auction pursuant to [§56-3(1)] is 
selected as the different classes of stock issue subject to call auction pursuant to paragraph 
(1), paragraphs (1) through (5) shall have priority over [§56-3] during the selected period. 

[September 22, 2020] 

§57. Methods of Trading Treasury Stocks of Stock-listed Corporations 

(1) Pursuant to [§39(3)] of the Regulation, in cases where a member intends to trade the 
treasury stocks of a stock-listed, the quotation methods for such trade shall be each of the 
following subparagraphs: (Amended on December 1, 2005; December 27, 2007; February 
3, 2009; April 20, 2012; April 12, 2023) 

1.  The  member  shall  submit  to  the  Exchange  an  application  for  trading  of  treasury 
stocks of stock-listed corporations in accordance with [Annex: Form No. 6] on the day 
before placing the quotations (it shall be from the market closing time to 18:00 hours). 
In  such  cases,  the  member  may  submit  the  relevant  details  through  the  electronic 
information delivery medium, which the Exchange designates separately;   

2. The quotations shall be placed at the price in accordance with each subparagraph of 
[§39(1)] of the Regulation, and in the following cases, the “previous day’s closing price” 
in each subparagraph of [§39(1)] of the Regulation shall be the price specified in each 
item.  In  such  cases,  for  the  issues  undergoing  ex-dividends,  ex-rights,  stock  split, 

96 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
reverse stock split,  and  for the  newly-listed issues  on the same day of placing  such 
quotation, the base price of the day shall deem to be the closing prices of the previous 
day, and for the issues using the first trading price as the base price, the appraisal prices 
of  the  day  shall  deem  to  be  the  closing  prices  of  the  previous  day,  respectively: 
(Amended on February 27, 2025) 

        (a) For issues using the first trading price as the base price: Appraisal price of the 

day; and [February 27, 2025] 

        (b) For issues whose previous day’s closing prices do not match the quotation price 
unit, for issues undergoing ex-dividends, ex-rights, stock split, reverse stock split, 
and for the newly-listed issues on the day of placing such quotation: Base price of 
the day. [February 27, 2025] 

3. The quotation quantity shall be less than the largest of the following quantities (the 
quantity  below  the  trading  unit  shall  be  discarded;  the  same  hereinafter  in  this 
subparagraph). Provided that, in cases where such quantity exceeds 1/100 of the total 
number of shares issued, it should be the amount less than 1/100 the total number of 
shares issued:   

(a)  The  quantities  equivalent  to  10/100  of  the  number  of  treasury  stocks  to  be 
acquired  (or  disposed  of),  which  the  stock-listed  corporation  reported  to  the 
Financial Services Commission for such purpose; and   

(b) The quantities equivalent to 25/100 of the average daily trading volume of one 
(1) month retroactive from one (1) day before the day when the board of the stock-
listed corporation made the decision on the acquisition (or disposal) of the treasury 
stocks.   

    4.  In  cases  where  “higher  price  of  the  last  price  and  the  best  bid  quotation”  in 
[§39(1)2(a)]  of  the  Regulation  or  “lower  price  of  the  last  price  and  the  best  offer 
quotation” in [§39(1)2(b)] of the Regulations is “the last price” but does not match the 
quotation  price  unit,  the  upper  limit  and  the  lower  limit  shall  be  calculated  in  the 
following manner: [February 27, 2025] 

        (a) In the case of higher limit: 

        Among the price that is lower than the last price and matches the quotation price 
unit, the price that is five (5) quotation price unit higher than the closest price to such 
price. [February 27, 2025] 

        (b) In the case of lower limit: 

        Among the price that is higher than the last price and matches the quotation price 
unit, the price that is five (5) quotation price unit lower than the closest price to such 
price. [February 27, 2025] 

97 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) After placing a quotation pursuant to paragraph (1), the member shall be prohibited 
to cancel such quotation. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(3) In cases of the issues where no transactions occurred during the regular session, “the 
most recent  execution price” in [§39(1)2] of the Regulation shall be construed as “the 
base price of the day”. When the expected best quotation price is announced pursuant to 
[§126(1)1] of the Regulation, “the best bid quotation” and “the best offer quotation” in 
the same subparagraph shall be construed as “the expected best bid quotation” and “the 
expected best offer quotation”, respectively. [September 8, 2006] (Amended on February 
3, 2009, April 25, 2013; May 19, 2015; February 27, 2025) 

§58. Special Cases Concerning Trading Methods of Treasury Stocks of Stock-listed 
Corporations 

(1)  In  cases  where  a  member  intends  to  purchase  the  treasury  stocks  of  stock-listed 
corporations in accordance with the methods specified in [§40(1)] of the Regulation, the 
quotation shall be placed in accordance with each of following methods: (Amended on 
April 20, 2012; February 27, 2025) 

1. Quotation prices shall be the prices specified in each subparagraph of [§40(2)] of the 
Regulation. In such cases, [§57(1)2] of the Regulation shall apply mutatis mutandis; 
and (Amended on February 27, 2025)     

2. Quotation quantity shall be equal to or less than the number of shares intended to 
acquire.   

(2) For the matters concerning the trading other than those mentioned in paragraph (1), 
[§57] shall apply thereto.   

§59. Trading Methods of Treasury Stocks of Stock-listed Corporations under Trust 
Contract and Special Cases Thereof 

Provisions of [§57] and [§58] shall apply mutatis mutandis to the case where a member 
intends to trade the treasury stocks under money trust contract by a method stipulated in 
[§41] of the Regulation. In such cases, “purchase of treasury stocks” shall be construed 
as  “purchase  of  treasury  stocks  under  money  trust  contract”,  the  quotation  quantity 
mentioned in [§57(1)3] shall be the quantity that is less than 1/100 of total number of 
shares issued, and the quotation quantity mentioned in [§58(1)2] shall be less than the 
quantity where the amount obtained by multiplying such quantity by its price does not 
exceed the total of the relevant trust asset.   

CHAPTER IV. TRADING OF DEBT SECURITIES 

Section 1. Common Provisions 

98 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§60. Application Scope 

This Chapter shall apply to the trading of debt securities. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

§61. License & Permit Bonds 

The  LPBs  under  subparagraph  2  of  [§43]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be,  from  among  the 
bonds noted in each of the following subparagraphs, the bonds which are issued during 
the current or previous month based on the trading date, and the quotation quantity per 
person  (referring  to  the  sum  of  new  quotation  quantity  and  the  unexecuted  quotation 
quantity; the same hereinafter in this Article.) being equal to or below KRW 50 million 
in par value. In such cases, the quotation quantity per person shall apply to the bid and 
offer quotations by bond respectively and be calculated by totaling the quotation quantity 
placed  in  the  joint  account  for  LPBs  under  [§77(1)]  of  the  Regulation:  (Amended  on 
December1, 2005; July 21, 2006; July 10, 2014) 

1. National Housing Bonds Type I;   

2. Seoul Railroad Bonds and Seoul Regional Development Bonds (hereinafter referred 
to as “the Seoul Railroad Bonds, etc.”);   

3. Regional development bonds issued by the metropolitan cities and provinces under 
the Local Public Enterprises Act; and   

4. Busan Railroad Bonds, Daegu Railroad Bonds, Incheon Railroad Bonds, Gwangju 
Railroad  Bonds  and  Daejeon  Railroad  Bonds  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  "the 
metropolitan railroad bonds, etc.").   

5. [Deleted on December 1, 2005]   

§62. Designations of LPB Dealers 

(1) Pursuant to [§44] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall designate a person as a new 
LPB dealer when the person submits to the Exchange an application for designation of 
LPB  dealer  in  accordance  with  [Annex:  Form  No.  7]  (hereinafter  referred  to  as 
"application  form"  in  this  Article)  during  the  period  specified  by  the  Exchange  in 
December of each year (hereinafter referred to as “application period”) and meets all of 
the following requirements: (Amended on December 18, 2007; November 27, 2025) 

    1.  The  net  capital  ratio  under  Article  3-6,  Paragraph  3  of  the  Financial  Investment 
Business Regulations for the half year immediately preceding the half year in which 
the application date falls shall be 100% or higher; [November 27, 2025] 

    2. Equity capital for the half year immediately preceding the half year in which the 
application date falls must be at least KRW 300 billion; [November 27, 2025] 

    3. As of the end of the year in which the application date falls, there shall be at least 

99 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
three (3) employees with at least three (3) years of experience in bond trading and at 
least one (1) employee with at least one (1) year of experience in securities and fund 
settlement; and [November 27, 2025] 

    4.  The  performance  of  proprietary  trading  of  LPBs  from  December  of  the  year 
preceding the year in which the application date falls to November of the year in 
which  the  application  date  falls  (limited to  trading  concluded  through  continuous 
trading pursuant to Article 48 of the Regulations) shall be KRW 400 billion or more. 
[November 27, 2025] 

(2) The Exchange shall redesignate as an LPB dealer a person who is an LPB dealer as of 
the  application  closing  date,  if  the  person  meets  all  of  the  following  requirements: 
Provided that, even if the person does not meet the requirements in subparagraph 2, the 
Exchange may redesignate the person as an LPB dealer if it deems necessary for market 
management due to reasons such as a rapid increase in the issuance of LPBs, a sudden 
change  in  the  financial  market,  etc.  (Amended  on  December  18,  2007;  November  17, 
2010; March 25, 2016; June 8, 2021; December 4, 2023; November 27, 2025)   

    1. All requirements of each subparagraph of paragraph (1) (excluding subparagraph 4) 

shall be met. [November 27, 2025] 

    2. The annual assessment score pursuant to [§62-3(1)] shall be 150 points or higher. 

[November 27, 2025] 

(3)  The  Exchange  shall  designate  LPB  dealers  each  December.  In  this  case,  the 
designation  period  shall  be  one  (1)  year,  starting  January  1  of  the  following  year. 
(Amended on November 27, 2025) 

(4) The Exchange shall not designate any member who falls under any of the following 
subparagraphs as an LPB dealer for three (3) years from the following year: (Amended 
on November 27,2025) 

    1. Members who were not redesignated as an LPB dealer pursuant to paragraph (2); or 

[November 27, 2025] 

    2. Members whose designation as an LPB dealer has been revoked pursuant to [§63]. 

[November 27, 2025] 

(5) In addition to paragraphs (1) through (4), the matters necessary for the designation of 
LPB  dealers  shall  be  determined  separately  by  the  Exchange.  [December  18,  2007] 
(Amended on November 27, 2025) 

§62-2. Assessment of LPB Dealers 

(1) The Exchange shall conduct semi-annual assessments of LPB dealers in accordance 
with Annex 2-5 and calculates semi-annual assessment scores. In this case, the Exchange 
may notify the relevant member of the semi-annual assessment scores. 

100 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) The Exchange may request LPB dealers to provide any information deemed necessary 
for the assessment under paragraph (1). In such cases, LPB dealers must respond without 
delay. 

[November 27, 2025] 

§62-3. Designations of Excellent LPB Dealers 

(1) The Exchange may designate LPB dealers whose annual assessment scores (referring 
to  the  sum  of  the  first  and  second  half  assessment  scores  of  the  year  in  which  the 
assessment was conducted pursuant to [§62-2(1)]; the same hereinafter) are within the 
top 30% as excellent LPB dealers. Provided that this excludes LPB dealers who violate 
any of the provisions of Article 74, Paragraphs 1 through 3 for six or more trading days 
during the annual assessment score calculation period. 

(2)  Provisions  of  [§62(3)]  shall  apply  to  the  designation  and  designation  period  of 
excellent LPB dealers mutatis mutandis. 

[November 27, 2025] 

§63. Revocation of Designation as LPB Dealer 

The Exchange may revoke the designation as LPB dealer in any of the following cases. 
Provided,  however,  that  where  subparagraph  2  applies,  the  designation  may  not  be 
revoked if the Exchange deems it necessary for market management due to reasons such 
as a rapid increase in the issuance of LPBs, a sudden change in the financial market, etc.: 
(Amended on December 18, 2007; March 23, 2011; February 28, 2014; March 25, 2016; 
December 4, 2023; November 27, 2025) 

1. Where an LPB dealer applies for withdrawal from such designation;   

2. Where the sum of the most recent two (2) semiannual assessment scores (referring 
to the score calculated by adding the assessment score for the first half of the year in 
which the evaluation was conducted pursuant to [§62-2(1)] and the assessment score 
for  the  second  half  of  the  previous  year;  the  same  hereinafter)  of  an  LPB  dealer 
(excluding LPB dealers who have been designated for the first time) is less than 150 
points;   

3. Where any of paragraphs (1) through (3) of [§74] are violated for ten (10) or more 
trading  days  by  type  of  bond  during  the  period  for  calculating  the  sum  of  the  most 
recent  two  semiannual  assessment  scores  or  the  period  for  calculating  the  annual 
assessment scores; or 

4.  Where  it  is  deemed  that  in  conjunction  with  the  trading  of  LPBs,  an LPB  dealer 
hinders the market operation or seemingly undermines the fairness in the market. 

101 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§64. Working Group for LPB Dealers 

(1) The Exchange may establish and operate a working group for LPB dealers (hereinafter 
in this Article referred to as "the working group") consisting of the following persons:   

1. Heads of the bond departments of LPB dealers; and   
2. Head of the Bond Market Operations of the Exchange.   

(2) The working group shall deliberate the following matters:   

1. The operational method of LPB dealers;   
2. The quantity of bid quotation pursuant to [§74(1)]; and   
3. In addition, the matters necessary for the trading of LPBs.   

Section 1-2. Administration of Quotations and Price Limits 

§64-2. Notification Method of Quotations for Covered Short Sales 

(1) Pursuant to [§44-2(6)] of the Regulation, each member shall submit to the Exchange 
the notification of quotations for covered short sales in accordance with [Annex: Form 
No. 7-2] via the postal service, in-person or facsimile on the day the quotation for covered 
short sale was placed.   

(2) In cases where the member has inputted the quotation for covered short sales pursuant 
to [§12(1)8(b)], it shall be deemed that the notification noted in paragraph (1) has been 
submitted. (Amended on March 19, 2009) 

[February 3, 2009] 

§64-3. Price Limit on Quotations for Covered Short Sales, etc. 

Pursuant to [§44-3(3)] of the Regulation, in the case of falling under any of the following 
subparagraphs, the proviso to [§18(1)] of the Regulation shall not apply: (Amended on 
March 6, 2009; July 10, 2014) 

1. Case where the opening price has not been determined; and 

2. Case where, when the opening price is the same as the immediately preceding price 
(referring to a price that is the base for restricting the input of quotation price noted in 
[§14(1)4(d)], the price that is different from the relevant price has not been determined.   

[February 3, 2009] 

Section 2. Units of Quotation and Trading Quantity 

102 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§65. Quotation Units 

(1) The quotation quantity units of debt securities under [§45] of the Regulation shall be 
each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

1. For debt securities except those denominated in foreign currencies: KRW 10,000 at 
par value; and   

2.  Foreign  currency  denominated  debt  securities:  10,000  basis  points  (the  lowest 
denomination of a certificate shall be deemed 10,000 basis points).   

(2) The quotation price units of debt securities under [§45] of the Regulation shall be each 
of  following  subparagraphs:  (Amended  on  February  3,  2009;  June  21,  2016;  June  14, 
2023) 

1.  For  debt  securities  except  those  denominated  in  foreign  currencies  and  the 
benchmark  issues  stipulated  in  subparagraph  3(a)  of  [§55]  of  the  Regulation 
(hereinafter referred to as the “benchmark issues”), the quotation price units classified 
in each of the following items:   

(a)  Where the term to maturity is shorter than two (2) years: KRW 0.1; 

(b) Where the term to maturity is two (2) years or longer but shorter than ten (10) 

years: KRW 0.5; and 

(c)  Where the term to maturity is ten (10) years or longer: KRW 1. 

2. For foreign currency denominated debt securities, the quotation price units classified 
in each of the following items: 

(a)  Where the term to maturity is shorter than two (2) years: 0.1 point; 

(b) Where the term to maturity is two (2) years or longer but shorter than ten (10) 

years: 0.5 point; and 

(c)  Where the term to maturity is ten (10) years or longer: 1 point. 

3. For benchmark issues, the quotation price units classified in each of the following 
items: 

(a)  Where the term to maturity is shorter than ten (10) years: KRW 0.5; and 

(b) Where  the  term  to  maturity  is  ten  (10)  years  or  longer  and  in  the  case  of  the 

inflation indexed treasury bonds: KRW 1. 

§66. Trading Quantity Units 

103 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
The trading quantity units of debt securities (excluding debt securities traded on the KRX 
KTB)  under  [§45]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  each  of  the  followings:  (Amended  on 
October 12, 2006; February 3, 2009; December 13, 2012; February 28, 2014; September 
10, 2019; May 23, 2024) 

1. LPBs: KRW 1,000 at par value;   

2. Foreign currency denominated debt securities: 10,000 basis points; 

3. [Deleted on February 28, 2014] 

4.  Short-term  bonds,  etc.  under  Article  59  of  the  Act  on  Electronic  Registration  of 
Stocks, Bonds, etc.: KRW 100 million at par value; and 

5.  Debt  securities  other  than  those  mentioned  in  subparagraphs  1  through  4:  KRW 
10,000 at par value. (Amended on December 24, 2025) 

Section 3. Execution of Trades 

§67. Priority of Simultaneous Quotations 

(1) The simultaneous quotations stipulated in [§46(2)3] of the Regulation shall apply only 
to LPBs, and the priority thereof shall be determined in the manner prescribed in each of 
the followings: (Amended on February 28, 2014; December 22, 2022) 

1. Bid quotations by issue shall have priority over those by class; 

2. [Deleted on December 22, 2022] 

3. Among the bid quotations, the bid quotations for customer account transactions and 
the bid quotation for self-account transactions placed by LPB dealers shall have priority 
over other bid quotations; and 

4. Among the ask quotations, the bid quotation noted in [§76(5)] shall have priority 
over other ask quotations. 

(2) Among the quotations that do not take priority over each other after applying the order 
of priority pursuant to each subparagraph of paragraph (1), the quotation with the larger 
quantity has priority (in the case of the same quantity, the quotation received earlier by 
the Exchange computer system has priority over those received later) over the quotations 
with smaller quantity until the quantity reaches the figure in subparagraph 1 below. For 
the  quotations  that  exceed  the  quantity  specified  in  subparagraph  1,  their  priority  is 
determined according to the same method mentioned above, in a sequential order, starting 
from  with  the  quantity  specified  in  subparagraph2.  (Amended  on  February  28,  2014; 
December 22, 2022) 

104 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. KRW 10 million; 

2. KRW 50 million; 

3. KRW 100 million; 

4. KRW 300 million; 

5. KRW 500 million; and 

6. Residual quantity. 

§67-2. Call auction 

“Debt securities specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§47(1)3] of the 
Regulation refers to LPBs. [November 18, 2015] 

§68. Range of Simultaneous Quotations 

The range of simultaneous quotations prescribed in [§47(2)] of the Regulation (including 
the quotations that participate in  the periodic  call  auction of  debt  securities except  for 
LPBs) shall be the quotations received during the period specified in each of the following 
subparagraphs  and  include,  if  any,  unexecuted  quotations  that  were  received  earlier. 
Provided  that,  in  cases  where  trades  have  not  been  executed  with  the  quotations 
mentioned above, the range shall include all quotations until the time when the first price 
is determined: (Amended on February 28, 2014) 

1.  In  the  case  of  determining  the  price  pursuant  to  [§47(1)1]  of  the  Regulation,  the 
range shall be from the beginning of the quotation receiving hours of the regular session 
mentioned in [§11] to the market opening; and   

2. In the case of determining the price pursuant to [§47(1)2&3] of the Regulation, the 
range shall be quotations received during the first ten (10) minutes from the time of 
reopening of the market or the resumption of trading.   

§69. Resumption of Trading after Trading Suspension of Individual Issues 

(1) In cases where the trading resumes after having been suspended pursuant to [§49(1)] 
of the Regulation, the timing of trading resumption shall be determined according to the 
following subparagraphs: (Amended on July 23, 2020) 

1. In the case of trading suspension pursuant to [§49(1)1] of the Regulation: The timing 
of  trading  resumption  shall  be  determined  considering  the  quotation  situations  and 
trading conditions; 

2. In the case of trading suspension pursuant to [§49(1)2] of the Regulation: the timing 
of  trading  resumption  shall  be  the  trading  day  after  the  day  on  which  an  issue  is 
designated as an investment precaution bond issue; and 

105 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
3. In the case of trading suspension pursuant to [§49(1)3] of the Regulation: The timing 
of trading resumption shall be determined considering the market situations and trading 
conditions. 

(2) When suspending or resuming trading pursuant to [§49] of the Regulation, such fact 
shall be officially announced immediately. 

(Wholly amended on November 18, 2015) 

§70. Measures to Take and Methods of Trade Execution in Case of Computer System 
Failure 
(Amended on January 15) 

(1) Pursuant to [§50] of the Regulation, when the occurrence of a computer system failure 
has been confirmed and it is deemed that the failure is likely to continue, the Exchange 
may take any of the following measures: (Amended on January 15, 2026) 

    1. Cancellation of quotations that caused computer system failure; or [January 15, 2026] 

    2. Suspension of receiving quotations or halt of trading. In this case, if the restoration 
of  details  of  quotations  is  impossible  or  it  is  necessary  to  promptly  recover  from  a 
computer  system  failure,  quotations  that  have  not  been  concluded  by  the  time  of 
suspension of receiving quotations or halt of trading may be cancelled. [January 15, 
2026] 

(2) When the computer system is back to normal operation after the quotation receiving 
was suspended or trading was halted pursuant to paragraph (1)2, the receipt of quotations 
or trading shall resume from the time determined by the Exchange. [January 15, 2026] 

(3) In cases where the computer system failure persists for a prolonged period, the trade 
shall be executed in accordance with each of the following methods: (Amended on August 
24, 2017) 

1. Execution of trade during the failure of member computer system:   

In  cases  where the computer system  failure has not  been restored by specified time 
before the market closing, it shall be deemed that the day’s trading has been closed at 
the time when the system failure occurred.   

2. Execution of trade during the failure of Exchange computer system:   

In cases where it is deemed that the computer system failure would continue well into 
the  market  closing  time  and  the  trade  execution  would  not  be  possible,  it  shall  be 
deemed  that  the  day’s  trading  has  been  closed  at  the  time  when  the  system  failure 
occurred.   

(4) In cases where the trading resumes pursuant to paragraph (2), the first price shall be 

106 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
determined  by  the  methods  of  trade  execution  set  forth  in  each  of  the  following 
subparagraphs: [February 28, 2014] (Amended on August 24, 2017; January 15, 2026) 

1. Trading under [§71-3(2)4] of the Regulation (hereinafter referred to as “trades in 
the KRX BondsAll”)   

The method of call auction under [§47] of the Regulation. In such cases, the range of 
quotations participating in determining the relevant price shall be determined by the 
Exchange each time. (Amended on January 15, 2026) 

2. Trading of LPBs   

The method of continuous trading under [§48] of the Regulation. (Amended on January 
15, 2026) 

(5) The methods of trade execution in the event of computer system failures other than 
those stipulated in paragraphs (3) and (4) shall be determined by the Exchange for each 
time when a failure occurs. (Amended on February 28, 2014; January 15, 2026) 

§71. Measures to Take and Method of Trade Execution in Case of Excessive Influx 
of Quotations 
(Amended on January 15, 2026) 

(1) [Deleted on February 28, 2014] 

(2) [Deleted on February 28, 2014] 

(3) In cases where there is a possibility of a  computer system failure due to excessive 
influx of quotations, the Exchange may take any of the following measures: (Amended 
on February 28, 2014; January 15, 2026) 

    1. Suspension of receiving quotations or halt of trading. In this case, if the restoration 
of details of quotations is impossible or there is a risk of computer system failure during 
restoration,  quotations  that  have  not  been  concluded  by  the  time  of  suspension  of 
receiving quotations or halt of trading may be cancelled; or [January 15, 2026] 

    2. Closing of trading of the day. [January 15, 2026]   

(4) If the Exchange determines that the risk of computer system failure due to excessive 
influx of quotations has been eliminated following the suspension of receiving quotations 
or the halt of trading under paragraph (3)1, the receiving of quotations or trading shall 
resume at a time determined by the Exchange. [January 15, 2026] 

(5)  In  the  case  where  trading  is  resumed  pursuant  to  paragraph  (4),  [§70(4)]  of  the 
Regulation shall apply to the determination of the first price mutatis mutandis. [January 
15, 2026] 

107 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(6) In cases where trading is closed due to the excessive influx of quotations during the 
quotation receiving hours for call auction under [§47] of the Regulation, the trading may 
be executed, taking into account the quotation conditions, with the quotations received 
by the time when such trading is closed. [January 15, 2026] 

(7) In addition to paragraphs (5) and (6), the method of trade execution in the event of 
excessive  influx  of  quotations  shall  be  determined  by  the  Exchange  at  each 
time.(Amended on February 28; January 15, 2026) 

§72. Provisions Applied Mutatis Mutandis 

The  provisions  of  [§44]  through  [§47]  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis  to  the  case  of 
transaction errors of debt securities. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

Section 4. Special Cases concerning Trade Execution 

§73. Reporting of Dealing of LPBs 

(1) Each member shall, when trading LPBs as a self-account transaction in OTC market 
pursuant to [§52] of the Regulation, report the details such as the issue name, quantity, 
price,  classification  for  bid  or  offer,  and  trading  time  of  each  trade  to  the  Exchange 
without delay. In such  cases, the reporting  shall be made by way of transmitting  such 
information to the Exchange computer system via the member computer system.   

(2) The market price, which is the base of the self-account transaction of LPBs in OTC 
market pursuant to paragraph (1), shall be the reported market price.   

§74. Bid Quotation, etc. of LPB Dealers 

(1) Each LPB dealer shall, for the trading of LPBs, place the bid quotations by class with 
amounts  no less than those specified in  each of  the following  subparagraphs,  for each 
issuing month of LPBs, before the market opening and during the last twenty (20) minutes 
before the market closing time each day. In such cases, subparagraph 1 shall apply to the 
first trading day of bonds issued in the previous month. (Amended on December 1, 2005; 
July 21, 2006; May 7, 2010; December 4, 2023)   

1. Bonds issued during the current month:   

(a) Type I National  Housing Bonds: KRW 2.4 billion before market opening and 

KRW 1.2 billion during the last twenty (20) minutes before the market closing 

time; 

(b) Seoul Railroad Bonds, etc.: KRW 200 million;   

(c) Regional Development Bonds: KRW 400 million; and 

(d) Metropolitan Railroad Bonds: KRW 200 million. 

108 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(e) [Deleted. December 1, 2005]   

2. Bonds issued in the previous month:   

(a) National Housing Bonds Type I: KRW 200 million;   

(b) Seoul Railroad Bonds, etc.: KRW 100 million; 

(c) Regional Development Bonds: KRW 100 million; and   

(d) Metropolitan Railroad Bonds: KRW 100 million.   

(e) [Deleted on December 1, 2005] 

(2)  LPB  dealers  are  obligated  to  submit  bid  quotations  for  the  offer  orders  entrusted 
pursuant to [§75(1)1] and offer quotations for self-account transaction placed pursuant to 
[§76(5)].  In  such  cases,  the  Exchange  may  request  LPB  dealers  to  place  necessary 
quantity of bid quotations after taking into consideration the prevailing quotation situation 
in the market. (Amended on December 18, 2007) 

(3)  LPB  dealers  shall  notify  the  price  required  to  calculate  the  reported  market  price 
(hereinafter referred to as the “price reported by LPB dealers") by 17:30 after the market 
closing by transmitting the price into the Exchange computer system. (Amended on June 
21, 2016; November 23, 2016) 

§75. Trading of LPBs at Market Closing 

(1)  The  range  of  quotations  noted  in  [§53(3)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  each  of  the 
followings. In such cases, it shall be deemed that such quotations have been placed at the 
reported market prices: (Amended on February 28, 2014) 

1. Offer Quotations   

Offer quotations for customer account at the price lower than the reported market price, 
which are received during the last twenty (20) minutes before the market closing time 
(including the unexecuted quotations among the offer quotations for customer account 
at the price lower than the reported market price, which were received earlier).   

2. Bid Quotations   

Each of the following quotations. In such cases, if bid quotations by class under [§10] 
is feasible, the bid quotations by issue shall be excluded:   

(a)  Bid  quotations  for  self-account  transaction  of  LPB  dealers  that  are  received 
during the last twenty  (20) minutes before the market  closing time (including  the 
unexecuted quotations among the bid quotations with a price higher than the reported 
market prices for dealing of LPB dealers that were received earlier); and (Amended 
on February 28, 2014) 

109 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(b) From among the quotations with a price higher than the reported market price, 
which are  received during the last twenty  (20) minutes before the market closing 
time,  the  bid  quotations  for  customer  orders  noted  in  [§104(1)6h]  (including  the 
unexecuted quotations among the entrusted bid quotations at the price higher than 
the reported market price, which were received earlier).   

(2)  The  priority  among  the  quotations  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1)  shall  be  each  of  the 
followings. In such cases, the time sequence shall not be considered; in cases where the 
quotation  quantity  is  the  same,  the  priority  shall  be  assigned  in  the  order  they  are 
registered in the Exchange computer system: (Amended on February 28, 2014; November 
18, 2015; November 23, 2016; December 22, 2022) 

1.  In  cases  where  total  quantity  of  offer  quotations  exceeds  total  quantity  of  bid 
quotations:  The  offers,  which  were  submitted  through  a  joint  account  for  LPB 
(hereinafter referred to as “the joint account”) noted in the proviso to [§77(1)] of the 
Regulation by the members (hereinafter referred to as the “selling agent”) who entered 
into a selling  agent  contract  pursuant  to  [§95] of the Regulation,  shall have priority 
over other offers, and the offers with  a smaller quantity shall have priority over the 
offers with larger quantities.   

2.  In  cases  where  total  quantity  of  bid  quotations  exceeds  total  quantity  of  offer 
quotations, the following items shall apply: 

(a) The own bid quotations of an LPB member shall have the priority over other bid 
quotations  until  the  own  bid  quotations  reach  45/100  of  the  total  offer  quotation 
quantity (the quantity below the trading unit, if any, shall be discarded). In such cases, 
between the own bid quotations of an LPB member, the bid quotation with a larger 
quantity shall have the priority over the bid quotation with a smaller quantity up to 
the quantity determined by the proportional distribution. 

(b) In the case of the offer quotation quantity except item (a), the bid quotation with 
a higher quantity, among bid quotations based on the residual quantity, shall have the 
priority over the bid quotation with a lower quantity up to the quantity determined by 
the  proportional  distribution  (the  quantity  below  the  trading  unit,  if  any,  shall  be 
added to the quotation with the highest quantity at first). 

§75-2. Negotiated Trade 

(1) “Trading of debt securities stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§53-2(2)3] of the 

Regulation shall be the trading in the KRX BondsAll. (Amended on January 15, 2026) 

(2) The quotation for negotiated trades under [§53-2(1)] of the Regulation (hereinafter 
referred to as “negotiated trade”) shall be classified as follows: 

1.  Request  quotation:  A  quotation  which  is  placed  by  a  person  who  requests  fora 
quotation  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “quotation  requester”)  by  designating  the 

110 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
quantity or the price (in the case of Repo trades, it refers to the Repo rate; the same 
hereinafter in this Article). Provided that, for the Repo trades and the trading in the 
KRX BondsAll, both of quantity and price shall be designated. 

2.  Proposal  quotation:  A  quotation  which  is  placed  by  a  person  who  proposes  a 
quotation  in  response  to  a  request  quotation  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “quotation 
proposer”) by designating the price or the quantity. Provided that, for the Repo trades, 
only the price can be designated, and for the trading in the KRX BondsAll, either the 
price or quantity shall not be designated. 

(3) The quotation quantity unit of negotiated trades shall be each of the followings: 

1. For Repo trades, KRW 10,000 in purchase price; and 

2. For the trades other than subparagraph 1, KRW 10,000in face value. 

(4) The quotation price unit of negotiated trades shall be each of the following: 

1. For Repo trades, Repo rate stipulated in [§89(2)]; and 

2.  For  the  trades  other  than  subparagraph  1,  the  quotation  price  units  specified  in 
[§65(2)]. 

(5) The trading unit of negotiated trades shall be each of the followings: (Amended on 
May 23, 2024) 

1. For the trading in the KRX KTB, KRW 100 million in face value; 

2. For Repo trades, KRW 100 million in purchase price; and 

3. For the trading in the KRX BondsAll, KRW 100 million in face value. 

(6) When submitting a request quotation, the quotation requester shall designate quotation 
proposers within the numbers specified in each of the following. Provided that, in case of 
Repo trades, a quotation proposer may not be designated. 

1. For the trading in the KRX KTB, ten (10) proposers; 

2. For Repo trades, five (5) proposers; and 

3. For the trading in the KRX BondsAll, one (1) proposer. 

(7)  The  effective  time  period  of  a  request  quotation  shall  be  the  time  in  each  of  the 
followings and a transaction shall become valid when an agreement is made in accordance 
with the method set by the Exchange. 

1.  For  the  trading  in  the  KRX  KTB,  five  (5)  minutes  after  the  receipt  of  request 
quotation; and 

2. For Repo trades, thirty (30) minutes after the receipt of request quotation. In such 

111 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
cases,  if  a  proposal  quotation  is  submitted,  the  effective  time  restarts  from  the 
submission of such quotation and the quotation requester may extend the effective 
time by five (5)-minute intervals. 

(8) In the case of the trading in the KRX BondsAll, the quotation of negotiated trades for 
foreign currency denominated debt securities and the quotation of negotiated trades for a 
foreign customer shall not be submitted. 

(9) In the case of Repo trades, the trading period shall be within 365 days (market holidays 
shall be included in calculating trading periods). The quantity of bonds that are used as 
collateral shall be the quantity of which the appraisal amount calculated by the following 
formula exceeds the purchase price and the minimum bond quantity shall be the amount 
in the unit of KRW 10,000.   
∙Appraisal amount = (Total face value of collateral bonds x Market value/10,000)/ (1+Haircut) 

(10)  Other  necessary  matters  with  regard  to  negotiated  trades  than  those  stated  in 
paragraphs (1) through (9) shall be determined by the Exchange. 

[March 24, 2016] 

§76. Reported Trading of Debt Securities 
(Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(1) The reported trading of debt securities under [§54] of the Regulation can be conducted 
when it falls under any of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on August 26, 2005; 
December 20, 2006; February 3, 2009; December 6, 2010; March 23, 2011; November 
18, 2015; March 24, 2016; September 10, 2019; December 22, 2022; May 23, 2024)   

1. Where the trading of convertible bonds pursuant to subparagraph 1 of [§43] of the 
Regulation is executed after the market closing;   

2. Where a selling agent places a bid quotation at the reported market price of the day 
for a sell order received from the sales agent after the market closing; 

3.  Case  of  executing  the  trade  of  debt  securities,  which  the  foreigners  or  foreign 
corporations intend to trade pursuant to Article 168 of the Act;   

4. Case where, among the bonds stipulated in each subparagraph of [§61], the trade of 
the bonds issued during the current and previous months on the basis of a trading day 
is executed;   

4-2. Where the trade, as when issued trade, is executed on the bidding day; 

4-3. Where the trade is executed in the KRX KTB; 

5.  Where  the  treasury  bond  primary  dealers  noted  in  [§55(2)]  of  the  Regulation 
(hereinafter  referred  to  as  “primary  dealer”)  enters  the  repurchase  agreements 

112 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(hereinafter referred to as “Repos”) with the Korean government or the Bank of Korea 
in order to resolve the concern about unsteady supply of and demand for treasury bonds 
noted in  Article 4(1)1(a) of the State Bond Act (hereinafter referred to as “treasury 
bonds”);   

6. Where the government bond financing agencies trade Repos with primary dealers, 
for  the  government  bond  financing  under  the  “Regulations  on  Issuance  of  Treasury 
Bonds  and  Operation  of  Primary  Dealer  System”  of  the  Ministry  of  Strategy  and 
Finance (hereinafter referred to as “Regulation on Operation of Treasury Bonds”); and   

7. Case where, besides the Repo trades in accordance with subparagraphs 5 and 6, the 
parties that submitted the participation agreement pursuant to [§71] of the Regulation 
trade Repos among them.   

(2) The trading hours for reported trading of debt securities shall be each of the followings: 
(Amended on August 26, 2005; December 20, 2006; February 3, 2009; November 18, 
2015; March 24, 2016; June 21, 2016; February 21, 2019; April 3, 2019) 

1.  From  the  market  closing  to  18:00  hours  in  the  case  of  subparagraphs  1  and  2  of 
paragraph (1);   

2. From the market opening to 18:00 hours in the case of subparagraphs 3 and 4 of 
paragraph (1). Provided that the trading hours under subparagraph 1 shall apply to the 
cases falling under subparagraphs 1 and 2 of paragraphs (1);   

2-2. From the market opening to 16:00 hours in the case of paragraph (1)4-2;   

    2-3. From 08:30 to 16:00 hours in the case of paragraph (1)4-3;   

3. From the market opening to the market closing time in the case of subparagraphs 5 
and 6 of paragraph (1); and 

4. From the market opening to 15:40 hours in the case of paragraph (1)7.   

(3)  Any  member  who  intends  to  conduct  the  reported  trading  of  debt  securities  shall 
request  such trading  by  way of transmitting  the name of issue, quantity,  bid  and offer 
quotations at the same price to the Exchange computer system via the member computer 
systems  or  member  debt  securities  terminals  during  the  trading  hours  mentioned  in 
paragraph (2). Provided that, in the case of the reported trade pursuant to paragraph (1)6, 
while considering that a bid quotation is a general collateral Repo transaction, the issue 
name  may  be  substituted  with  another  issue  until  the  day  before  the  repurchase  date 
pursuant to [§25] of the Securities Market Clearing and Settlement Business Regulation. 
(Amended on February 3, 2009; April 27, 2009; May 23, 2024; February 27, 2025)   

(4) Once the reported trading pursuant to paragraph (3) is requested, the Exchange shall 
deem  that  the  relevant  trade  has  been  executed  at  the  quotations  reported  and  the 
settlement has been concluded at the same time. Provided that, this provision shall not 

113 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
apply to subparagraphs 4-2, 4-3, 6 and 7 of paragraph (1). (Amended on August 26, 2005; 
December 20, 2006; November 18, 2015; March 24, 2016)   

(5) Any member who has requested the reported trading falling under paragraph (1)2 shall 
submit  an  offer  quotation  for  the  entire  quantity  before  the  market  opening  on  the 
following day at price not more than the price obtained by adding KRW 1 for each elapsed 
day to the reported market price of the previous day. (Amended on May 7, 2010; June 21, 
2016; September 10, 2019; November 20, 2020; December 4, 2023) 

(6)  The  trading  under  the  provisions  of  paragraph  (1)5  shall  be  governed  by  the 
Agreement for Participation under the provisions of [§71] of the Regulation.   

(7) In the case of reported trading pursuant to paragraphs (1)6 and (1)7, the trading period 
shall be less than 360 days. [December 20, 2006] (Amended on April 27, 2009) 

Section 5. Trading in KRX KTB 

§77. Definitions 

The  terms  used  in  this  section  shall  have  the  same  meanings  given  to  them  in  the 
Regulation.   

§78. Designation of Non-Benchmark Issues 

(1)  “Issues  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  subparagraph  3(b)  of  [§55]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to issues in each of the followings; (Amended on May 23, 2024) 

1. Treasury bonds that are not the benchmark issues. In this case, they shall include the 
strip  bond  in  which  the  principal  amount  and  coupon  payment  are  sold  separately 
[hereinafter referred to as the “STRIPS (Separate Trading of Registered Interest and 
Principal of Securities”) prescribed in Subparagraph 12 of [§2] of the “Regulation on 
Operation of Treasury Bonds”; and 

    2. Foreign exchange stabilization fund bonds (limited to those denominated in Korean 

won) noted in Article 13(7) of the Foreign Exchange Transaction Act. 

(2)  “Issues  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules"  in  subparagraph  3(c)  of  [§55]  of  the 
Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  monetary  stabilization  bonds  and  deposit  insurance  fund 
bonds. (Amended on February 28, 2014) 

§79. Receipt of Quotations, etc. 

(1) Notwithstanding [§11(1)1], the quotation-receiving hours for the trading in the KRX 
KTB  pursuant  to  [§57(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  the  trading  hours  of  the  regular 
session.   

114 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) “Within the range specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the latter part of [§57(2)] of 
the  Regulation  shall  mean  “within  the  price  specified  in  each  subparagraph  of  Article 
31(3)  of  the  “Regulation  on  Operation  of  Treasury  Bonds  for  each  benchmark  issue”. 
(Amended on May 23, 2024)   

(3)  The  number  and  quantity  of  market-making  quotations  on  both  sides  pursuant  to 
[§57(2)] of the Regulation shall be the number and quantity specified in Article 31(1) and 
(2)  of  the  Regulation  on  Operation  of  Treasury  Bonds.  In  this  case,  if  the  quantity  of 
quotations exceeds KRW 1 billion, it shall be considered that as many quotations as the 
quantity of quotations divided by KRW 1 billion have been submitted. [May 23, 2024] 
(Previous paragraph (3) moved to paragraph (5) on May 23, 2024) 

(4)  Notwithstanding  paragraphs  (2)  and  (3),  the  Exchange  may  determine  the  spread, 
number or quantity of market-making quotations on both sides if it deems necessary given 
the market conditions, etc. [May 23, 2024] (Previous paragraph (4) moved to paragraph 
(6) on May 23, 2024) 

(5) The one-sided market-making quotations pursuant to [§57(4)] may be submitted only 
if they are deemed necessary by the Exchange given the market conditions, etc. [February 
28,  2014]  (Moved  from  previous  paragraph  (3),  previous  paragraph  (5)  moved  to 
paragraph (7) on May 23, 2024) 

(6)  The  primary  dealer  who  has  placed  the  market-making  quotations  on  both  sides 
pursuant to [§57(2)] of the Regulation shall place the market-making quotations for both 
sides again within ten (10) minutes, if either of the relevant market-making bid or offer 
has been executed in full quantity (including the case where the remaining quantity on 
either  one  side  is  less  than  the  number  or  quantity  of  the  market-making  quotations 
pursuant to paragraph (3). (Amended on October 23, 2009; May 23, 2024) (Moved from 
previous paragraph (4), previous paragraph (6) moved to paragraph (8) on May 23, 2024) 

(7) With respect to the quotations under [§57(4)] of the Regulation, a condition that falls 
under any of the following subparagraphs may be affixed. [February 28, 2014] (Moved 
from previous paragraph (5), previous paragraph (7) moved to paragraph (9) on May 23, 
2024) 

1. IOC condition: The quantity of which trade can be executed at the time of receiving 
relevant quotations shall be subject to trade execution, while the unexecuted remainder 
shall be cancelled.   

2.  FOK  condition:  If  the  entire  quantity  can  be  executed  for  trading  at  the  time  of 
receiving relevant quotations, trading will be executed. Otherwise, the entire quantity 
shall be cancelled.   

(8) No member can input quotations falling under each of the following subparagraphs 
for the trading in the KRX KTB: [November 28, 2019] (Moved from previous paragraph 
(6) on May 23, 2024) 

115 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1.  For  individual  auctions:  Any  quotation,  the  amount  of  which  exceeds  the 
outstanding balance of listed amount or is KRW 100 billion or more; and 

2. For negotiated trading or reported trading under [§76]: Any quotation, the amount 
of which exceeds the outstanding balance of listed amount or KRW 999 billion. 

(9) Notwithstanding the main sentence of [§14(1)4(d)], in the case of trading in the KRX 
KTB, members may not input bid quotations with prices higher or offer quotations with 
prices  lower  than  the  following  ratios  based  on  the  previous  day’s  closing  price; 
[November 28, 2019; November 23, 2021] (Amended on December 24, 2025) 

    1. Benchmark issue (excluding 50-year treasury bonds) and when-issued security under 
Article 2, Subparagraph 14 of the Regulation on Operation of Treasury Bonds: Ratios in 
each of the followings: [December 24, 2025] 

        (a) If the maturity is 10 years or less: 5 % [December 24, 2025] 

        (b) If the maturity is more than 10 years: 10% [December 24, 2025] 

    2. Issues other than those in subparagraph 1: [December 24, 2025] 

        (a) If the remaining maturity is 10 years or less: 10% [December 24, 2025] 

        (b) If the remaining maturity is more than 10 years: 20% [December 24, 2025] 

(10) A primary dealer may file an application with the Exchange for the designation of a 
bond market-making account pursuant to [§99-9(5)] to place market-making quotations 
on both sides pursuant to [§57(2)] of the Regulation. [May 23, 2024] 

§79-2. Special Cases for Submitting Market-making Quotations on Both Sides, etc. 
(Amended on May 23, 2024) 

(1) Pursuant to [§57(6)] of the Regulation, the primary dealers shall, during the trading 
hours of the regular session, submit the two-sided market-making quotations for issues 
that  the  Exchange  designates  pursuant  to  Subparagraph  1  of  Article  19-2(1)  of  the 
Regulation on Operation of Treasury Bonds. In this case, the spread, the number, and the 
quantity of the two-sided market-making quotations shall be as follows and the method 
of  designating  an  issue  subject  to  the  two-sided  market-making  quotations  shall  be  as 
stipulated in [Annex 2-6], however, the Exchange may determine the spread, the number 
and/or the quantity, and the issue designation method of the two-sided market-making 
quotations  differently  if  it  deems  necessary  considering  the  market  conditions,  etc.: 
(Amended on August 24, 2017; May 23, 2024; October 29, 2024; March 25, 2026) 

1. Quotation spread: Price specified in each item of Subparagraph 5 of Article 19-2(1) 
of the Regulation on Operation of Treasury Bonds; and 

    2.  Number  and  quantity  of  quotations:  The  number  and  the  quantity  specified  in 

116 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Subparagraph 2 and 4 of Article 19-2(1) of the Regulation on Operation of Treasury 
Bonds. In this case, if the quantity of quotations exceeds KRW 1 billion, it shall be 
considered that as many quotations as the quantity of quotations divided by KRW 1 
billion have been submitted. 

(2)  Pursuant  to  [§57(6)]  of  the  Regulation,  a  preliminary  primary  dealer  in  charge  of 
market-making quotations pursuant to Articles 31 and 39 of the Regulation on Operation 
of Treasury Bonds (hereinafter referred to as “preliminary primary dealer”) shall submit 
the two-sided market-making quotations for benchmark issues during the trading hours 
of the regular session. In this case, with respect to the matters relating to the spread, the 
number,  and  the  quantity  of  two-sided  market-making  quotations,  the  provisions  of 
[§79(2) through (4)] shall apply mutatis mutandis. 

(3)  Pursuant  to  [§57(6)]  of  the  Regulation,  primary  dealers  and  preliminary  primary 
dealers may submit the two-sided market-making quotations for non-benchmark issues 
(excluding treasury bonds with a remaining maturity of less than one (1) year, 50-year 
maturity  treasury  bonds,  and  inflation-linked  treasury  bonds)  under  Article  2, 
Subparagraph  4  of  the  Regulation  on  Operation  of  Treasury  Bonds  during  the  trading 
hours of the regular session. In this case, main sentence of [§99-6(1)2], main sentence of 
[§99-6(2)2],  and  [§99-6  (3)]  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis  to  the  spread,  number,  and 
quantity of the two-sided market-making quotations. [March 25, 2026] 

(4)  If  either  of  the  bid  or  offer  market-making  quotations  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1) 
through (3) has been executed in full quantity (including the case where the remaining 
quantity  on  either  one  side  is  less  than  the  number  or  quantity  of  the  market-making 
quotations pursuant to paragraph (1)2,    [§79(3)], or the main sentence of [§99-6(2)2], 
the primary dealer shall place the market-making quotations for both sides again within 
ten (10) minutes. [May 23, 2024] (Amended on March 25, 2026) 

(5) A STRIPS primary dealer or preliminary primary dealer may apply to the Exchange 
for the designation of a bond market-making account under [§99-9(5)] in order to place 
two-sided market-making quotations in accordance with paragraphs (1) or (2). [May 23, 
2024] (Amended on March 25, 2026) 

[June 21, 2016] 

§80.  Suspension  of  Validity  of  Two-sided  Market-making  Quotations  and 
Restoration Thereafter 

(1) [Deleted on February 28. 2014] 

(2) Pursuant to [§58(2)] of the Regulation, the suspension of validity of two-sided market-
making quotations submitted by primary dealers and preliminary primary dealers shall be 
limited to the quotation-receiving hours, and there shall be no limit on the frequency of 
suspension. (Amended on February 28, 2014; May 23, 2024; March 25, 2026) 

(3)  With  respect  to  the  suspended  two-sided  market-making  quotations  by  primary 

117 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
dealers and preliminary primary dealers, the validity of the relevant quotations shall be 
construed as having been suspended until their validity become reinstated. (Amended on 
February 28, 2014; May 23, 2024; March 25, 2026) 

§81. Restriction on Quotations 

For the trading in the KRX KTB, the two-sided market-making quotations shall not be 
placed if they fall into any one of the following subparagraphs:   

1. Where an offer price is lower than or equal to a bid price;   

2. Where the price or quantity of either an offer or a bid quotation is omitted; and   

3. Where the spread between such quotations exceeds the quotation spread pursuant to 
[§79(2)],  [§79-2(1)1],  the  latter  part  of  [§79-2(2)],  or  the  latter  part  of  [§79-2(3)]. 
Provided that, in cases where the number of spread prices of the two-sided market-
making quotations is multiple, it is limited to cases where the spread of market-making 
quotations exceeds the maximum spread based on the prices. (Amended on March 25, 
2026) 

(Wholly amended on February 28, 2014) 

§81-2. Cancellation and Change of Two-sided Market-Making Quotations 

(1) In the case of canceling the two-sided market-making quotations that have not been 

concluded  in  the  trading  of  KRX  KTB,  the  entire  quantity  shall  be  canceled, 

notwithstanding [§17(1)]. 

(2) In the case of changing the two-sided market-making quotations in the trading of the 

KRX KTB, the price of market-making quotations may be changed only if it satisfies the 

spread requirement pursuant to [§79(2)], [§79-2(1)1], the latter part of [§79-2(2)], or the 

latter part of [§79-2(3)]. Provided that, in the case where the number of spread prices of 

the  two-sided  market-making  quotations  is  multiple,  the  price  of  market-making 
quotations may be changed only if the spread of market-making quotations satisfies the 

maximum spread based on the prices. (Amended on March 25, 2026) 

[May 23, 2024] 

§82. Measures to Take and Methods of Trade Execution in Case of Computer System 
Failures 
(Amended on January 15, 2026) 

(1) In cases where a computer system failure has been confirmed and it is deemed that 

118 

 
 
 
 
 
 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
 
 
 
 
 
 
such system  failure is  likely  to  continue,  the Exchange may  take any of  the following 
measures: (Amended on February 28, 2014; January 15, 2026) 

    1. Cancellation of quotations that caused computer system failure; or [January 15, 2026] 

    2. Suspension of receiving quotations or halt of trading.  In this case, the validity of 
quotations received before the suspension of receiving quotation or of the quotations 
received before the halt of trading shall not be recognized. [January 15, 2026] 

(2)  When  the  computer  system  is  back  to  normal  operation  after  the  suspension  of 
receiving quotations or the halt of trading under paragraph (1)2, the receipt of quotations 
or trading shall resume from the time determined by the Exchange. [January 15, 2026] 

(3) In cases where a computer system failure persists for a prolonged period, the trade 
shall be executed according to each of the followings methods:   

1. Methods of trade execution during the failure of member computer system:   

In cases where the system failure has not been restored until a specified time after the 
market closing, it shall be construed that the trading of the day was closed at the time 
when  the  system  failure  has  occurred.  Provided  that,  in  cases  where  the  computer 
system failed during the last thirty (30) minutes before the market closing time and it 
is deemed that the failure would be unlikely to be restored by the market closing time, 
the Exchange may close the trading of the day at the time such failure has occurred.   

2. Methods of trade execution during the failure of Exchange computer system:   

In  cases  where,  due  to  a  computer  system  failure,  a  normal  execution  of  trades  is 
difficult until a specified time after the market closing, the Exchange shall record all 
quotations received until such time and execute them by method of continuous auction 
under [§59] of the Regulation. Provided that, in cases where it is anticipated that trade 
execution would not be possible because the system failure would not be restored until 
the specified time after the market closing, it shall be construed that the trading of the 
day has been closed at the time when such system failure occurred.   

(4) In cases where the trade execution is resumed pursuant to paragraph (2), the first price 
shall be determined by continuous auction under [§59] of the Regulation. [February 28, 
2014] (Amended on August 24, 2017; January 15, 2026) 

(5) [Deleted on May 23, 2024] 

(6) In addition to paragraphs (3) and (4), the methods of trade execution in the event of a 
computer system failure shall be determined by the Exchange at each case. [February 28,
