2014] (Amended on November 28, 2019; January 15, 2026) 

§82-2. Mass Cancellation of Quotations 

119 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(1) In the case where there are unavoidable circumstances, such as system failure, error, 
etc., in relation with trading in the KRX KTB, a member may apply for mass cancellation 
of quotations to the Exchange, through the member debt securities terminal or the member 
computer system. 

(2)  A  member  who  wishes  to  apply  for  mass  cancellation  of  quotations  through  the 
member  debt  securities  terminal  may  apply  for  quotations  only  submitted  through  the 
member debt securities terminal by some or all of traders affiliated to the member, and 
the Exchange may, after confirming the quotation status of the member, process the mass 
cancellation of quotations submitted by some or all of the traders affiliated to the member.     

(3)  A  member  who  wishes  to  apply  for  mass  cancellation  of  quotations  through  the 
member  computer  system  shall  report  to  the  Exchange  the  account  that  submits  the 
quotations  (limited  to  quotations  submitted  through  the  member  computer  system)  for 
mass cancellation and the manager of that account by 6 p.m. the day before the trading 
day using the Appendix Form 7-5. 

(4) Paragraph (3) shall apply mutatis mutandis to the closure or change of an account and 
the change of the manager of the relevant account pursuant to paragraph (3). 

(5)  A  member  who  applies  for  mass  cancellation  of  quotations  through  the  member 
computer system shall input matters in each of the followings into the Exchange computer 
system;   

1. Account number reported to the Exchange pursuant to paragraph (3); 

    2. Quotation processing type and its contents. In this case, the quotation  processing 

contents are classified as follows: 

        (a) Cancellation of all quotations received by account noted in subparagraph 1; and 

(b)  Blocking  of  additional  new  orders,  correction  orders,  cancellation  orders, 
suspension  and  resumption  of  the  validity  of  two-sided  market-making 
quotations (hereinafter referred to as “receipt of orders, etc.” in this Article). 

3. Other matters that the Exchange deems necessary. 

(6) In the case where a member applies for mass cancellation of quotations through the 
Exchange  computer  system,  the  Exchange  shall  conduct  the  mass  cancellation  of 
quotations, after verifying the details in each subparagraph in paragraph (5), and block 
the receipt of orders, etc. through the relevant account. 

(7)  After  a  member  applies  for  mass  cancellation  of  quotations  through  the  member 
computer system, the member may request the Exchange to lift the block on the receipt 
of orders, etc. through the relevant account ten (10) minutes after the application has been 
made, and, if the member does not request the lifting of the block on the receipt of orders, 
etc., the Exchange may lift the block on the receipt of orders, etc. after the market closing 

120 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
of the day. 

(8) Notwithstanding paragraphs (1) through (7), the Exchange may not accept to process 
the mass cancellation of quotations or lift the block on the receipt of orders, etc. in case 
of a system failure or other cases when it deems necessary for market management.   

(9) A member who applies for mass cancellation of quotations shall record and maintain 
data related to the mass cancellation of quotations, including details of system failures, 
etc., for ten (10) years. 

[May 23, 2024] 

§83. Measures to Take and Methods of Trade Execution in Case of Excessive Influx 
of Quotations 
(Amended on January 15, 2026) 

(1) [Deleted on February 28, 2014] 

(2) In cases where there is a possibility of a  computer system failure due to excessive 
influx of quotations, the Exchange may take any of the following measures: [February 28, 
2014] (Amended on January 15, 2026) 

    1. Suspension of receiving quotations or halt of trading.  In this case, the validity of 
quotations received before the halt of trading shall not be recognized; or [January 15, 
2026] 

    2. Closing of trading of the day. [January 15, 2026]   

(3) If the Exchange determines that the risk of computer system failure due to excessive 
influx of quotations has been eliminated following the suspension of receiving quotations 
or the halt of trading under paragraph (2)1, the receiving of quotations or trading shall 
resume at a time determined by the Exchange. [January 15, 2026] 

(4)  In  the  case  where  trading  is  resumed  pursuant  to  paragraph  (3),  [§82(4)]  of  the 
Regulation shall apply to the determination of the first price mutatis mutandis. [February 
28, 2014] (Amended on January 15, 2026) 

(5) In addition to paragraph (4), the method of trade execution in the event of excessive 
influx  of  quotations  shall  be  determined  by  the  Exchange  at  each  case.  (Amended  on 
February 28, 2014; November 28, 2019; January 15, 2026) 

§84. Trading Quantity Unit in KRX KTB 

(1) The trading quantity unit of the KRX KTB under [§59(2)] of the Regulation shall be 
KRW 1 billion at par value. Provided that, the par value of the STRIPS shall be KRW 
100 million. (Amended on October 12, 2006; March 6, 2015; June 21, 2016) 

121 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1),  the  trading  quantity  unit  of  negotiated  trades  and 
reported trades in the KRX KTB shall be as follows: [May 23, 2024] 

    1. Negotiated trades: Quantity in face value noted in [§75-2(5)1]; and 

    2. Reported trades: KRW 100 million in par value. 

§84-2. When-Issued Trades 

(1)  The  “cases  that  are  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in[§59-2(3)]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the cases when the settlement date is the due date for holding 
reserve set by the Bank of Korea. (Amended on October 29, 2024) 

(2) Pursuant to [§59-2(5)] of the Regulation, the party who are eligible for participating 
in the when-issued trade shall be the government bond dealers. (Amended on March 24, 
2016) 

(3) The issues eligible for the when-issued trade shall be newly issued the treasury bonds 
(inflation-indexed  treasury  bonds  noted  in  the  “Regulation  on  Operation  of  Treasury 
Bonds” shall be excluded). (Amended on June 21, 2016) 

(4) The quotation unit for when-issued trade shall be KRW one (1). 

(5) The trading amount of the when-issued trade shall be calculated by using the coupon 
rate that is decided by the bidding of the relevant treasury bonds. 

(6) In cases where the Ministry of Strategy and Finance cancels the when-issued trade 
and  notifies  this  to  the  Exchange  as  a  case  falling  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs,  the  trade  shall  be  deemed  as  cancelled  pursuant  to  [§59-2(4)]of  the 
Regulation: 

1. Where the relevant treasury bond is not issued; 

2. Where the actual issuance amount of the relevant treasury bonds is significantly less 
than the issuance amount that was notified; 

3. The net sales amount of the relevant when-issued trade exceeds the actual issuance 
amount significantly; and 

4.  Other  cases  where  the  ordinary  settlement  of  the  relevant  when-issued  trade  is 
deemed impossible. 

[November 18, 2015] 

§85. Mutatis Mutandis Application 

The provisions of the Sections 1 through 4 of Chapter IV shall apply mutatis mutandis to 

122 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
the matters relating to trading in the KRX KTB, which are not stipulated in this Section. 
(Amended on February 3, 2009) 

Section 6. Trading of Bond Repurchase Agreement 

§86. Definitions 

The  terms  used  in  this  section  shall  have  the  same  meanings  given  to  them  in  the 
Regulation.   

§87. Eligible Bonds 

The  “bonds  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  subparagraph  4  of  [§61]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the bonds (excluding the equity-related bonds) falling under each 
of  the  following  subparagraphs:  (Amended  on  May  18,  2007;  December  6,  2010; 
December 26, 2016; February 21, 2019) 

1. [Deleted on February 21, 2019] 

2.  Issues  of  which  the  credit  ratings  published  by  the  credit  rating  companies  that 
obtained authorization for credit rating business pursuant to Article 335-3 of the Act 
(hereinafter referred to as the “credit rating company”; when the credit ratings given 
by  credit  rating  companies  are  different,  the  lowest  rating  shall  apply;  the  same 
hereinafter) are AA or above.   

§88. Repo Term and Repurchase Date 

(1) The types of Repo terms noted in [§62(1)] of the Regulation shall be overnight, two 
(2) days, three (3) days, four (4) days, seven (7) days, fourteen (14) days, twenty one (21) 
days, thirty (30) days, sixty (60) days, and ninety (90) days. (Amended on December 6, 
2010) 

(2) The repurchase date for each Repo term noted in [§62 (1)] of the Regulation shall be 
the 2nd day, 3rd day, 4th day, 5th day, 8th day, 15th day, 22nd day, 31st day, 61st day, and 91st 
day, respectively, counting from the day on which the purchase price is settled. (Amended 
on December 6, 2010) 

§89. Quotation Quantity Unit, etc. 

(1) The quotation quantity unit under [§63] of the Regulation shall be KRW 10,000 in 
purchase price.   

(2) The quotation price unit under [§63] of the Regulation shall be Repo rate expressed 
up  to  the  second  decimal  place  (figures  below  the  second  decimal  place  shall  be 
discarded). Provided that, the quotation price unit for Repo trades pursuant to [§76(1)6] 
shall be the Repo rate expressed up to the third decimal place (numbers shall be rounded 

123 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
up to the fourth decimal place). (Amended on February 28, 2014) 

(3) The quantity unit for trading mentioned in [§63] of the Regulation shall be KRW 1 
billion in face value. (Amended on February 28, 2014) 

(4) The quotation receiving hours under [§63] of the Regulation shall, notwithstanding 
[§11(1)1], be the trading hours of a regular session. [February 3, 2009]   

§90. Haircut and Calculation of Market Value 

(1) The haircut under [§65(1)] of the Regulation shall be 2%.   

(2) The market value under [§65(2)] of the Regulation shall be the previous day’s mark-
to-market price.   

(3) The mark-to-market price under [§65(2)] of the Regulation (hereinafter referred to as 
“the mark-to-market price”) shall be calculated by simply averaging the appraisal prices 
of  the  relevant  purchased  bonds,  which  were  announced  by  the  bond  price  appraisal 
agencies on each trading day. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(4) Matters concerning the designation of the bond price appraisal agencies mentioned in 
paragraph (3) shall be determined by the Exchange, while taking into account such factors 
as the public confidence, both  the national  and international,  in  such agencies and the 
price appraisal models employed by them. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(5) In the case of calculating the amount for Repo trade pursuant to [§76(1)5], the amount 
less than KRW 10 shall be discarded. [December 6, 2010] 

§91. [Deleted on February 27, 2025] 

§92. [Deleted on February 27, 2025] 

§93. [Deleted on February 27, 2025] 

§94. [Deleted on February 27, 2025] 

§95. [Deleted on February 27, 2025] 

§96. [Deleted on February 27, 2025] 

§96-2. Procedures for Early Termination of Repo Trade 

(1) In cases where it is necessary to terminate Repo trade according to [§70(1)7] of the 
Regulation,  either  the  buyer  or  seller  of  the  Repo  shall  inform  the  Exchange  of  its 
intention for early termination by 13:30 of the day of actual termination. In such cases, 
the Exchange shall notify the counterparty of the receipt of request for early termination 
without  delay  and  the  counterparty  who  has  received  the  notification  shall  inform  the 

124 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Exchange of whether or not to accept the request for early termination by 14:30 of the 
same day. (Amended on June 21, 2016) 

(2) The requesting period for early termination of Repo trade according to paragraph (1) 
shall be the Repo trading period, excluding the trading days, repurchase days and market 
holidays.   

[December 6, 2010] 

§97. Return of Additional Margin 

The return of additional margin under [§70(3)] of the Regulation shall be accomplished 
according to the method noted in each of the following subparagraphs:   

1. In the case of margin bonds: 

The sum of (a) the margin bonds, (b) the income not actually returned to the buyer and 
the seller, among the incomes received by the seller and the buyer during a period from 
the  payment  date  of  such  margin  bonds  to  the  repurchase  date,  and  (c)  the  accrued 
interest, which is calculated by applying the applicable interest rate to such income for 
a period from the income payment date to the repurchase date, shall be returned.   

2. In the case of cash margin: 

The sum of the cash margins and the accrued interest, which is calculated by applying 
the applicable interest rate to such cash margins for a period from the payment date of 
such cash margin to the repurchase date, shall be returned.   

§98. Participation Agreement 

The  participation  agreement  under  the  provisions  of  [§71(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall 
include each of the following details:   

1. Details about the calculation of the net exposure, and the payment and handling of 
additional margin;   

2. Details on handling of income;   

3. Details about the methods and procedures for the conclusion of Repo trading;   

4. Details about the settlement of purchase prices and repurchase prices; and   

5. Other details necessary for the participation in Repo trading.   

§99. Provisions Applicable Mutatis Mutandis 

(1) With respect to the matters related to Repo trading which are not specified in this 

125 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Section, Section 1 through Section 4 (excluding §64-2, §64-3,§70 and §71) of Chapter 
IV shall apply mutatis mutandis..   

(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), the provisions of [§82] shall apply mutatis mutandis 
to  the  methods  of  trade  execution  in  the  event  of  computer  system  failures,  and  the 
provisions of [§83] shall apply mutatis mutandis to the methods of trade execution for 
excessively-quoted issues. 

Section 7. Bond Market-making Members 

§99-2. Definitions 

The  terms  used  in  this  Section  shall  have  the  same  meanings  as  given  to  them  in  the 
Regulation. (Wholly amended on July 16, 2015) 

§99-3. Designation of Bond Market-making Members and Termination Thereof 

(1) Pursuant to [§71-3] of the Regulation, a person who intends to be designated as a bond 
market-making member shall submit an application for designation in accordance with 
[Annex: Form No. 7-3] (referred to as “designation application” hereinafter in this Article) 
for trade of each subparagraph of [§71-3(2)] of the Regulation (excluding the Repo trade; 
the same hereinafter in this Article) to the Exchange within the period specified by the 
Exchange for each quarter of year. (Amended on March 24, 2016) 

(2) In cases where a person who submitted the designation application is eligible for the 
participation in the trading specified in each subparagraph of [§71-3(2)] of the Regulation, 
the Exchange shall designate the person as a bond market-making member for the relevant 
trading type. Provided that, in order to be designated as a bond market-making member 
for the trading of LPBs, the person shall fall under any of the following subparagraphs: 
(Amended on December 22, 2022) 

1. LPB dealers; and 

2. Selling agents. 

(3) Notwithstanding paragraphs (1) and (2), a person who is eligible for the participation 
in the Repo trading shall be deemed as a bond market-making member for Repo trades, 
and in cases where a person who is not a bond market-making member for trading in the 
KRX KTB or KRX BondsAll participates in the negotiated trades in such market, he/she 
shall be deemed as a bond market-making member for the relevant trade only. [March 24, 
2016] 

(4)  In  cases  where  a  bond  market-making  member  falls  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs, the Exchange may terminate the  designation as  a bond  market-making 
member. (Amended on December 26, 2016; May 7, 2021; August 4, 2022; October 29, 
2024) 

126 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. In cases where the relevant member has filed an application for termination of the 
designation; 

2. In cases where, for the trading in the KRX KTB, the number of trading days that 
meet both the requirement of the basic number of market-making issues stipulated in 
subparagraph 1(a)(1) of [Annex 4] and the requirement of the basic market-making 
time stipulated in subparagraph 1(b)(1) of [Annex 4] is less than half (the first decimal 
place shall be rounded up) of the total trading days during the evaluation period; 

3.  In  cases  where,  for  the  trading  of  LPBs,  the  bond  market-making  member  came 
under none of the subparagraphs of the proviso to paragraph (2);   

4. In cases where the relevant member receives a criminal sanction, a penalty surcharge, 
business  suspension,  trading  suspension,  or  disciplinary  measure  of  member  fine 
(limited  to  cases  of  KRW  10  million  or  more)  by  violating  securities  laws  and 
regulations  and  the  Exchange’s  business  regulations  in  the  course  of  carrying  out 
market-making tasks for debt securities [referring to market-making tasks in the debt 
securities  market  and  interest  rate  product  market  (limited  to  the  government  bond 
futures market) in the derivatives market; and 

5. In cases where a member violates [§99-4(4)]. 

(5)  The  Exchange  shall  not  designate  the  bond  market-making  member  whose 
designation has been terminated pursuant to subparagraphs 1, 2, 4 and 5 of paragraph (4), 
as a bond market-making member for four (4) quarters from the next quarter of the quarter 
to  which  the  termination  date  belongs  (referred  to  as  the  “period  of  restriction  for  re-
designation” hereinafter in this Article). (Amended on March 24, 2016;  December 26, 
2016; May 7, 2021)   

(6)  Notwithstanding  paragraphs  (4)2  and  (5),  the  Exchange  may  not  terminate  the 
designation or may stipulate the period of restriction for re-designation differently in any 
of the following cases: (Amended on December 26, 2016; October 29, 2024)   

1.  In  cases  where  it  is  necessary  to  continue  to  designate  a  bond  market-making 
member due to concerns about a rapid decline in market liquidity, etc.;   

2.  In  cases  where  it  is  difficult  for  a  bond  market-making  member  to  fulfill  its 
obligation to place market-making quotations due to a sudden change in the financial 
market, a serious failure of electronic systems, etc.; 

3. In cases where the bond market-making member is a primary dealer or a preliminary 
primary dealer and it is necessary to continue to designate the relevant member as a 
bond market-making member; and (Amended on March 25, 2026) 

4. In other cases where the Exchange deems necessary for market management. 

127 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(7) The necessary matters related to the designation and termination of designation as a 
bond market-making member other than those stated in paragraphs (1) through (6) shall 
be determined by the Exchange. (Amended on March 24, 2016; December 26, 2016)   

(Wholly amended on July 16, 2015) 

§99-4. Submission methods, etc. of Market-Making Quotations 

(1) Pursuant to [§71-4(1)] of the Regulation, the market-making quotations that may be 
submitted by bond market-making members are as follows. Provided that, in the case of 
market-making quotations of negotiated trades, only one-sided market-making quotations 
(referring  to  the request  quotation  stipulated in  [§75-2(2)1] of the Regulation) may be 
submitted: (Amended on March 24, 2016) 

1. Two-sided market-making quotations for the trading in the KRX KTB;   

2. One-sided market-making quotations for each bid and offer for the trading of LPBs; 

2-2. One-sided market-making quotations (referring to the quotation that is received 
first for the relevant trade) for the Repo trades; and 

3. Two-sided market-making quotations for the trading in the KRX BondsAll. 

(2)  When  submitting  two-sided  quotations  pursuant  to  subparagraphs  1  and  3  of 
paragraph (1), quotations falling under any of the following subparagraphs shall not be 
submitted: (Amended on May 23, 2024) 

1. Where the offer price is equal to or lower than the bid price; 

2. Where the price or quantity of either the offer or the bid is omitted;   

3. Where the quotations exceed the spread of market-making quotations stipulated in 
[§99-6(1)1,2 and 4]. Provided that, in the case where the number of spread prices of 
the two-sided market-making quotations pursuant to [§99-6(1)1 or 2] is multiple, it is 
limited  to  cases  where  the  spread  of  market-making  quotations  exceeds  the  spread 
based on the maximum prices; and 

4. Where the quantity falls short of the quantity of market-making quotations stipulated 
in [§99-6(2)3]. 

(3) When submitting one-sided quotations pursuant to paragraph (1)2, quotations falling 
under any of the following subparagraphs shall not be submitted: (Amended on May 23, 
2024) 

1. Where the price or quantity of bid or offer is omitted;   

2.  Where  the  spread  exceeds  the  spread  of  market-making  quotations  stipulated  in 

128 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[§99-6(1)3]; 

3. Where the quantity falls short of the quantity of market-making quotations stipulated 
in [§99-6(2)3]; 

4. Bid quotations by class of bonds; and 

5. Case of trading of LPBs at market closing under [§75]. 

(4) The bond market-making members shall not entrust the submission of market-making 
quotations under paragraph (1) to a third party. [May 7, 2021] 

(Wholly amended on July 16, 2015) 

§99-5. Debt Securities Subject to Submission of Market-making Quotations 

Bond  market-making  members  may  submit  market-making  quotations  for  any  of  the 
following debt securities: (Amended on March 24, 2016; June 21, 2016; December 26, 
2016; August 24, 2017; September 10, 2019; May 23, 2024; October 29, 2024) 

1. For the trading in the KRX KTB, issues in the followings; 

    (a) Benchmark issues; 

    (b) Non-benchmark issues (excluding STRIP bonds) under [§78(1)1]; and 

    (c) In the case where a bond market-making member is a primary dealer, among the 
STRIP bonds, bond issues designated by the Exchange pursuant to Article 19-
2(1)1 of the Regulation on Operation of Treasury Bonds. In this case, the method 
of designating the relevant issue shall be as stipulated in [Annex 2-6], however, 
the Exchange may designate the relevant issue differently if necessary, taking 
into consideration market conditions, etc. (Amended on March 25, 2026) 

2. For the trading of LPBs, LPBs under subparagraph 2 of [§43] of the Regulation;   

2-2. For Repo trades, bonds under [§61] of the Regulation; and 

3. For the trading of in the KRX BondsAll, the debt securities excluding those stated 
in the following items: 

(a) Equity-related bonds; 

(b) Foreign currency denominated debt securities; 

(c) Corporate bonds with credit ratings that are below investment grades; 

(d) Floating rate debt securities; 

129 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(e) Option embedded debt securities (this provision shall not apply to the bonds for 
which the creditors have the right to claim the redemption before the maturity); and 

(f) Short-term bonds, etc. under subparagraph 4 of [§66]. 

4. For the negotiated trades, the listed debt securities. 

[July 16, 2015] 

§99-6. Spreads and Quantity of Market-making Quotations 

(1)  In  cases  where  a  bond  market-making  member  places  market-making  quotations 
pursuant to [§71-4(2)], the spreads of the quotations shall be as follows: (Amended on 
March 24, 2016; June 21, 2016; December 26, 2016; August 24, 2017; December 4, 2023; 
May 23, 2024) 

1.  For  the  trades  of  benchmark  issues  in  KRX  KTB,  the  prices  specified  in  each 
subparagraph of Article 31(3) of the Regulation on Operation of Treasury Bonds; 

2. For the trades of non-benchmark issues in KRX KTB, the prices equivalent to not 
more than eight (8) basis points based on yields. Provided that, for STRIPS, the prices 
specified in each item of Article 19-2(1)5 of the Regulation on Operation of Treasury 
Bonds; 

3. For the trades of LPBs, the prices corresponding to not more than quotation spread 
in  each  of  the  following  items  based  on  yields  that  fall  under  the  mark-to-market 
prices stated in [§65(2)] of the Regulation;   

(a) For National Housing Bonds Type I, ±0.1 percent points; and 

(b) For LPBs other than item (a), ±0.2 percent points. 

4. For the trades in KRX BondsAll, the prices  corresponding to not more than the 
quotation spread, based on yields, classified in each of the following items:   

(a) For government bonds, ten (10) basis points; 

(b) For corporate bonds with credit ratings of below “AA-”, twenty (20) basis points; 
and 

(c)  Debt  securities other than those noted in  items  (a)  and (b), fifteen  (15) basis 
points.   

(2)  In  cases  where  a  bond  market-making  member  places  market-making  quotations 
pursuant to [§71-4(3)], the quantity, etc. of the quotation shall be as follows: (Amended 
on March 24, 2016; June 21, 2016; May 23, 2024) 

130 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. For the trades of benchmark issues in KRX KTB, the number of quotations and the 
quantity  of  a  quotation  stipulated  in  Paragraphs  (1)  and  (2)  of  Article  31  of  the 
Regulation  on  Operation  of  Treasury  Bonds.  In  such  cases,  if  the  quantity  of  a 
quotation exceeds KRW 1 billion, it shall be deemed that as many of quotations as 
the number obtained by dividing the quantity by KRW 1 billion have been submitted; 

2. For the trading of the non-benchmark issues in KRX KTB, the quotation quantity 
shall be KRW 1 billion or higher based on face value. Provided that, for STRIPS, the 
number of quotations and the quantity of a quotation stipulated in subparagraphs 2 
and 4 of Article 19-2(1) of the Regulation on Operation of Treasury Bonds. In such 
cases, if the quantity of a quotation exceeds KRW 1 billion, it shall be deemed that as 
many of quotations as the number obtained by dividing the quantity by KRW 1 billion 
have been submitted; and 

3. For the trading of LPBs and trading in KRX BondsAll, the quotation quantity shall 
be KRW 100 million at minimum and KRW 10 billion at maximum based on face 
value. 

(3) Notwithstanding paragraphs (1) and (2), in cases where it is deemed necessary for the 
reasons such as a sudden change in quotation conditions or trading conditions and for the 
market  management,  the  Exchange  may  change  the  spread,  quantity,  etc.  of  market-
making quotations. (Amended on May 23, 2024) 

[July 16, 2015] 

§99-7. Special Cases Concerning Submission of Market-making Quotations, etc. 

(1) With respect to the trading in KRX KTB, a new market-making quotation shall be 
placed within  three (3)  minutes from  the cancellation of  an already submitted  market-
making quotation to be deemed that the quotation was placed continuously. 

(2) With respect to the trading in KRX KTB, [§79(6)], [§79-2(4)], and [§80] shall apply 
mutatis mutandis. (Amended on May 23, 2024; March 25, 2026) 

(3) With respect to the trading of LPBs and the trading in KRX BondsAll, if a part of 
market-making quotations were executed, it shall be deemed that the executed quantity 
of  the  market-making  quotations  of  the  relevant  issue  have  been  placed  continuously 
during the day. (Amended on March 24, 2016) 

(4)  In  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary  for  the  reasons  such  as  a  sudden 
change in quotation conditions or trading conditions and for the market management, the 
submission of market-making quotations may be exempted. 

[July 16, 2015] 

131 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§99-8. Cancellation and Modification of Market-making Quotations 

(1)  In  cases  where  a  bond  market-making  member  intends  to  cancel  market-making 
quotations  that  have  not  been  executed,  the  whole  quantity  shall  be  cancelled, 
notwithstanding [§17(1)]. (Amended on May 23, 2024) 

(2)  The  bond  market-making  members  may  change  the  price  of  a  market-making 
quotation  only  in  cases  where  the  requirements  on  spreads  stated  in  [§99-6(1)]  are 
fulfilled.  Provided  that,  in  the  case  where  the  number  of  spread  prices  of  two-sided 
market-making  quotations  is  multiple,  the  price  of  a  market-making  quotation  can  be 
changed only if the spread price of the two-sided market-making quotations satisfy the 
spread based on the maximum spread based on prices. (Amended on May 23, 2024) 

(3) The bond market-making members in the LPBs market may change the quantity of a 
market-making quotation only in cases where the requirements on quantity stated in [§99-
6(2)3] are fulfilled. (Amended on March 24, 2016; May 23, 2024) 

(Wholly amended on July 16, 2015) 

§99-9.  Designation  and Termination  of  Designation  of  Market-making  Dealers  or 
Market-making Accounts 
(Amended on May 23, 2024) 

(1)  The  Exchange  may  designate  a  person  of  a  bond  market-making  member  who  is 
eligible to submit market-making quotations (hereinafter referred to as the “bond market-
making dealer”) through the member debt securities terminal for each of the trades stated 
in [§71-3(2)1 & 4] of the Regulation, by the application from the relevant market-making 
member. (Amended on May 23, 2024) 

(2) The numbers of bond market-making dealers are as follows: (Amended on March 24, 
2016; May 23, 2024) 

1. For trading in KRX KTB, six (6); and 

2. For trading in KRX BondsAll, two (2).   

(3)  In  cases  where  a  bond  market-making  member  applies  for  the  designation  or  the 
termination  of  designation  of  a  bond  market-making  dealer,  it  shall  submit  to  the 
Exchange an application for designation or termination of designation of a bond market-
making dealer in accordance with [Annex: Form No. 7-4] for each of the trades stated in 
[§71-3(2)1 and 4] of the Regulation. (Amended on May 23, 2024) 

(4)  In  cases  where  a  bond  market-making  member  applies  for  designation  of  a  bond 
market-making  dealer  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1),  it  shall  appoint  a  staff-in-charge  and 
notify it to the Exchange, and the same shall apply to the case where the staff-in-charge 
is changed. (Amended on May 23, 2024) 

(5)  In  the  case  of  trades  in  the  KRX  KTB  or  SLBs,  the  Exchange  may  designate  an 

132 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
account  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “bond  market-making  account”)  through  which 
market-making quotations can be submitted. In this  case, the number of bond  market-
making accounts shall be a maximum of ten (10) by bond trade type per bond market-
making member. (Amended on May 23, 2024) 

(6) A member who intends to obtain the designation of a bond market-making account 
pursuant to paragraph (5) shall report the relevant account and the manager of the account 
to the Exchange using Appendix Form 7-6 by 18:00 on the day before the trading day. 
(Amended on May 23, 2024) 

(7) Paragraph (6) shall apply mutatis mutandis to the closure or change of a bond market-
making account or to a change in the manager of the relevant account. (Amended on May 
23, 2024) 

(Wholly amended on July 16, 2015)   

§99-10. Assessment of Bond Market-making Members 

(1) Pursuant to [§71-5] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall assess the market-making 
members on a quarterly basis by the trading type (excluding Repo trades) stated in [§71-
3(2)] of the Regulation with regard to each of following subparagraphs: (Amended on 
March 24, 2016; October 29, 2024)   

1.  The  performance  of  submission  of  market-making  quotations  (excluding  the 
performance of submission of market-making quotations for negotiated trades in KRX 
KTB and KRX BondsAll); (Amended on December 24, 2025) 

2.  The  performance  of  trading  by  market-making  quotations  (excluding  the 
performance of trading for the negotiated trades in KRX KTB and KRX BondsAll). 
Provided that, in cases where the counterparty quotation is a market-making quotation 
placed by the same member, such trading shall be excluded from the trading record: 
and (Amended on December 24, 2025) 

3. The validity of market-making quotations (limited to the market-making quotations 
in KRX KTB). 

(2) The assessment of a bond market-making member shall be conducted in accordance 
with the method specified in [Annex 4]. 

(3) The matters necessary for the assessment of bond market-making members, other than 
those stated in paragraphs (1) and (2), shall be determined by the Exchange. 

[July 16, 2015] 

§99-11. Payment for Bond Market-making Members 

(1) Pursuant to [§71-5(1)] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall make payment to bond 

133 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
market-making members according to the criteria that are determined separately. 

(2) The Exchange shall make payment within one (1) month from  the closing of each 
quarter. 

(3) In cases where a bond market-making member falls under any of the followings, the 
payment  to  the  relevant  member  may  be  restricted:  (Amended  on  March  24,  2016; 
December 26, 2016; October 29, 2024) 

1.  Where  the  performance  of  submitting  market-making  quotations  stated  in  [§99-
10(1)1] falls below the basic market-making score specified in subparagraph 1(d) of 
[Annex 4]; 

2.  Where  the  performance  of  trading  by  market-making  quotations  stated  in  [§99-
10(1)2] falls below the following ratios based on the trading performance by market-
making quotations submitted by the total bond market-making members for each of 
trading  types  (excluding  Repo  trades)  stated  in  [§71-3(2)]  of  the  Regulation;  and 
(Amended on December 24, 2025) 

    (a) For trading in KRX KTB: 0.5% [December 24, 2025] 

    (b) For trading of LPBs: 0.5% [December 24, 2025] 

    (c) For trading in KRX BondsAll: 1.0% [December 24, 2025] 

3.  Where  the  performance  of  validity  of  market-making  quotations  stated  in  [§99-
10(1)3] is less than 1 point; and 

4. Where the designation as a bond market-making member was revoked by falling 
under any of the subparagraphs of [§99-3(4)]. 

(4) The matters necessary with regard to the payment to bond market-making members 
and the restriction on such payment, other than those stated in paragraphs (1) through (3), 
shall be determined by the Exchange. 

[July 16, 2015]

CHAPTER VI. RECEIVING OF TRADE ENTRUSTMENT 

Section 1. Common Provisions 

§102. Definitions 

The  terms  used  in  this  Chapter  shall  have  the  meanings  given  to  them  in  each  of  the 
following  subparagraphs:  (Amended  on  February  8,  2006;  February  3,  2009;  June  24, 
2014; September 19, 2017) 

1. The term "KOSDAQ-listed securities" refers to the securities listed on the KOSDAQ 
Market established by the Exchange.   

2. The term "base date for calculation" refers to the base date used in calculating the 
substitute price for beneficiary certificates and stocks of unlisted investment companies 
(indicating the stocks which are not listed as those of investment companies; the same 
hereinafter.) and comes five (5) trading days prior to the first application date.   

(a) [Deleted on June 24, 2014] 
(b) [Deleted on June 24, 2014] 

3. The term "first application date" refers to the first trading day of each month, which 
is the first day to apply the substitute prices calculated for beneficiary certificates and 
unlisted stocks of investment companies.   

138 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(a) [Deleted on June 24, 2014] 
(b) [Deleted on June 24, 2014] 

Section 2. Methods and Conditions of Receiving Entrustment 

§103. Establishment of Joint Account for LPBs 

(1)  Each  member  shall,  when  executing  trades  by  opening  a  joint  account  under  the 
proviso to [§77(1)] of the Regulation, record, on the order slip, the details of agreement 
for the use of joint accounts, and the customer shall print its name and sign or put its seal 
thereon. (Amended February 28, 2014) 

(2) The joint account under the provisions of paragraph (1) shall make a clear distinction 
between the trade details of each customer.   

§104. Customer Information to be Confirmed When Opening Trading Account 

(1) “Matters stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§77(3)] of the Regulation shall refer 
to the details under each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on May 13, 2008; 
February 3, 2009; March 19, 2009; June 20, 2012; August 8, 2023; November 23, 2023) 

1.  Name  or  designation,  resident  registration  number,  business  registration  number, 
taxpayer number. in the case of foreigners, the number identifying the real name such 
as the number of foreigner identification means (in the case of a foreigner treated as a 
citizen, it refers the passport number, business registration number or taxpayer number); 

2. Address and telephone number;   

3. Password;   

4.  In  the  case  of  other  investment  traders  or  brokers,  the  type  of  account  (customer 
account or self-account);   

5. In the case of foreign investors, the matters specified in each of the following items: 

(a) The nationality or permanent resident; 

(b) [Deleted on November 23, 2023] 

(c) The availability of residence in Korea 

6. Investor classification code specified in each of the following items. Provided that, 
in the case of trading of stocks, etc. linked to the CFD, it is based on the investor who 
concluded the CFD: 

(a) In the case of financial investment companies: 1000; 

139 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(b) In the case of insurance companies: 2000; 

(c) In the case of collective investment vehicles:   

(i) Collective investment vehicle other than the one noted in (ii) below: 3000; and 

(ii) Privately placed funds: 3100. 

(d) Banks [the collective investment assets of collective investment business entities 
shall be classified into item (c)]: 4000;   

(e) Other financial institutions: 5000; 

(f) Pensions, funds, and cooperatives: 6000; 

(g)  The  Government,  local  governments,  international  organizations  and  public 
service institutions: 7000;   

(g-2) The corporation other than those specified in items (a) through (g): 7100;   

(h) Individuals: 8000. 

(i) [Deleted on March 19, 2009]   

7. In cases where an agent has been designated, the name or designation of agent, ID 
number of agent identifying the real name such as the resident registration number or 
business  registration  number,  the  relationship  with  the  customer,  address,  and  the 
power of such agent.   

(2) In cases where a customer falls under an investor classification code other than those 
mentioned in paragraph (1)6 at the time of opening a trading account, the member shall 
verify such fact immediately, and maintain a written record of such fact. (Amended on 
February 3, 2009) 

§104-2. Publication of Order Placing Methods, etc. 

(1) In cases where the member establishes the order placing method, etc. pursuant to [§77-
2(4)] of the Regulation, the matters noted in each of the following subparagraphs shall be 
stated: (February 28, 2014; December 22, 2022) 

1. With respect to the method of accepting entrustment of order, the matters noted in 
each of the following items:   

(a) Originator of order;   

(b) Location where the order originated; 

140 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
   
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(c) Order input device; 

(d) Order routing device; and 

(e) Order receipt device. 

2. With respect to order processing method, the matters under each of the following 
items:   

(a)  Verification  method  of  order  suitability,  etc.  according  to  [§11-2]  of  the 
Regulation and physical location of system used for verification; and   

(b) Session type specified in the Guideline on Connection, etc. to Member System. 

3. Conditions of use and user fees per method according to subparagraphs 1 and 2.   

4. In addition, matters that the member deems necessary to explain the differences 
between the ordering methods.   

(2) When establishing  or changing  the order placing  method,  etc., each member shall, 
pursuant to [§77-2(4)] of the Regulation, officially announce it through the medium such 
as the member’s internet website in advance and notify it to the Exchange immediately.   

[December 28, 2011] 

§104-3. Terms and Conditions for High-speed Algorithmic Trading 

Pursuant to [§78(1)8(b)] of the Regulation, in case where a customer of a member is a 
person who is required to registered as a high-speed algorithmic trader, the member shall 
include each of the following matters in the terms and conditions: 

    1. The customer shall identify and systemically manage risks that may arise from the 

high-speed algorithmic trading;   

2.  The  customer  shall  prepare  the  procedures  for  developing  and  changing  the 
electronic systems including an ordering system, etc. and the program related to the 
high-speed algorithmic trading, and shall comply with them when operating; 

    3. The customer shall cooperate in fulfilling the member’s obligation to manage high-
speed  algorithmic  traders,  including  checking  the  electronic  system  such  as  the 
ordering system, etc.; 

    4. The customer shall prepare an appropriate control and response system to effectively 
cope with accidents or system failures related to the high-speed algorithmic trading and 
to minimize damage therefrom; 

141 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
    5.  The  customer  shall  maintain  a  mutual  contact  system  with  members  to  respond 
promptly in the event of an emergency, such as errors in the electronic system such as 
the ordering system, etc.; and 

    6.  In  the  case  where  the  customer  who  has  conducted  the  high-speed  algorithmic 
trading  through multiple members pursuant  to  [§131(3)] is  suspended to  submit the 
orders for high-speed algorithmic trading pursuant to [§104-3(5)], he/she shall notify 
all other members of the relevant fact and reason. 

[December 22, 2022] 

§105. Notification Deadline of Agreement for Receiving Trade Entrustment 

The “period set forth in the Enforcement Rules” in [§78(3)] of the Regulation shall be 
five (5) trading days from the effective date of the relevant agreement.   

§106.  Methods  of  Receiving  Entrustment  of  Order  to  Trade  Treasury  Stocks  of 
Stock-listed Corporations 

(1) Each member shall, when receiving an entrustment of order for trading treasury stocks 
from  a  stock-listed  corporation  pursuant  to  [§79(3)]  of  the  Regulation,  receive  such 
entrustment in accordance with each of the following methods:   

1. Shall receive orders from the stock-listed corporation during the quotation receiving 
hours for the regular session of the day;   

2. Order price shall be the price pursuant to [§39(1)] of the Regulation. In such cases, 
when making corrections to such orders during the trading hours, the order prices shall 
be the ones mentioned [§39(2)] of the Regulation; and   

3. Order quantity shall be the quantity pursuant to [§57(1)3].   

(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), when receiving an entrustment of orders to purchase 
the treasury stocks from a stock-listed corporation pursuant to [§40(1)] of the Regulation, 
each member shall receive the orders in accordance with each of the following methods:   

1. Shall receive orders from the stock-listed corporation during the quotation receiving 
hours of the regular session of the day;   

2. Order price shall be the price mentioned in  each  subparagraph of [§40(2)] of the 
Regulation. In such cases, when making correction to such order, the order price shall 
be the one mentioned in [§40(2)2] of the Regulation; and   

3. The quantity of order shall be equal to or less than the number of shares intended to 
purchase.   

(3) The provisions of paragraphs (1) and (2) shall not apply to the cases where a member 

142 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
has received an entrustment of an order from a stock-listed corporation for the trading of 
treasury stocks by way of off-hours trading under [§39(4)] of the Regulation. [September 
8, 2006] 

§107. Methods of Receiving Entrustment for Trading of Treasury Stocks of Stock-
listed Corporations under Trust Contract 

In cases where a member receives an entrustment of order for trading the treasury stocks 
of listed companies from a trust company, etc. pursuant to [§80(4)] of the Regulation, 
[§106] shall apply mutatis mutandis. In such cases, “stock-listed corporations” shall be 
construed  as  “trust  companies”  and  “trading  treasury  stocks”  shall  be  construed  as 
“trading treasury stocks by trust company”, the order quantity mentioned in [§106(1)3] 
shall  be  less  than  1/100  of  the  total  number  of  shares  issued,  and  the  order  quantity 
mentioned  in  [§106(2)3]  shall  be  the  quantity,  for  which  the  amount  obtained  by 
multiplying the relevant order quantity by its price does not exceed the total amount of 
the relevant trust asset. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

§108. Details of Entrustment 

The “details specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§81] of the Regulation shall be the 
details under each of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on May 13, 2005; July 7, 
2006; February 3, 2009; March 19, 2009; July 16, 2009; July 29, 2010; January 27, 2011; 
September 2, 2014; December 10, 2014; July 11, 2019; December 22, 2022; August 8, 
2023; February 27, 2025) 

1. Classification of regular session, pre-hours session or after-hours session;   

1-2. In the case of quotations for after-hours session, classification of trade type noted 
in each subparagraph of [§33] of the Regulation;   

1-3.  In  the  case  of  quotations  for  regular  session  auction-based  block  trade,  regular 
session block trade or regular session basket trade, such classification; 

1-4. In the case of quotation for cancellation or correction, such classification; 

2. Issue or class;   

3. Quantity;   

4. Classification of bid or offer;   

5. Classification of order type pursuant to [§2(5)] of the Regulation;   

6. Price. Provided that this provision shall not apply to the market order, immediately 
executable  limit  order,  best  limit  order,  target  price  order,  mid-price  order,  auction-
based block trade order, off-hours closing price trade, or the quotation placed to correct 
or cancel the quotations already submitted; (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

143 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
    6-2. Stop price in the case of stop-limit order; [February 27, 2025] 

7.  In  the  case  of  an  order  related  to  arbitrage  trading,  each  of  the  following 
classifications:   

(a)Index arbitrage trading;   

(b)Sector index arbitrage trading; 

(c) Stock arbitrage trading;   

(d)  Arbitrage  trading  of  collective  investment  securities  of  ETF,  while  it  is  non-
arbitrage trading; 

(e) Arbitrage trading of collective investment securities of ETF, while it is not non-
arbitrage trading;   

(f) DR arbitrage trading;   

(g) DR of foreign stock arbitrage trading; 

(h) Arbitrage trading of ETNs while it is non-arbitrage trading; and 

(i) Arbitrage trading of ETNs while it is not non-arbitrage trading. 

8.  In  the  case  of  an  order  for  trading  a  basket  of  stocks,  each  of  the  following 
classifications: 

(a) Non-arbitrage trading;   

(b)  Trading  a  basket  of  stocks  for  the  purpose  of  creating  ETFs,  which  is  non-
arbitrage trading; and   

(c) Trading a basket of stocks for the purpose of creating ETFs, which is not non-
arbitrage trading.   

8-2. [Deleted on July 11, 2019] 

9. In the case of offer order, each of the following classifications:   

(a) Order for offer quotation falling under any subparagraph of [§17(1)] or [§44-2(1)] 
of the Regulation;   

(b) Order for covered short sale quotation pursuant to [§17(2)] or [§44-2(2)] of the 
Regulation; and 

144 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(c) Order for any other offer quotation.   

10. In  the  case of an order to  purchase or dispose the treasury stocks, classification 
according to each of the following items:   

(a) Following classifications according to the purposes 

(i) Trade for the purpose of distributing at the time when stock options is exercised; 

(ii) Trade according to the money trust contract; 

(iii) Trade for the purpose other than those noted in (i) and (ii).   

(b) Following classifications according to the trading method 

(i) Trade subject to [§35(4)] of the Regulation; 

(ii) Of the treasury stock purchases under [§39(4)1&2] of the Regulation, those 
subject to [§35(2)] of the Regulation; 

(iii) Trade other than those noted in (i) and (ii). 

11. Classification for cash transaction or margin transaction;   

11-2. In the case of trading of stocks, etc. linked to the CFD, such classification; 

12. In cases where the condition falling under any of the following items is affixed to 
the orders, such conditions;   

(a)  In  the  case  of  limit  order,  market  order,  immediately  executable  limit  order, 
auction-based  block  trade  order,  and  mid-price  order,  the  following  conditions: 
(Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(i)  Immediate  or  cancel  (IOC)  condition:  Condition  specifying  to  execute  the 
amount of quotation quantity of the order that can be executed at the time when 
the quotation is received, and to cancel any unexecuted quantity of the order; and   

(ii) Fill or kill (FOK) condition: Condition specifying to execute the order if its 
entirety can be executed at the time when the quotation is received, and to cancel 
the order if it cannot be executed in its entire quantity.   

(d) Following condition in the case of limit order, best limit order, and immediately 
executable limit order: Self-match prevention condition pursuant to [§13-2];     

(c) Quotation placing time for the order; and   

(d) In addition, other conditions concerning the order.   

145 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
13. Valid period of the order, if any;   

14. Time the order was received; and   

15. Identification codes  of order-inputting devices under the provisions of items  (c) 
through (e) of [§12(1)27].   

16. Specification of designated trading markets. Provided that, debt securities are an 
exception. [February 27, 2025] 

17. In cases where a customer receives the short selling registration number, the short 
selling registration number (limited to stocks). [March 26, 2025] 

§109. Methods for Receiving Orders   

(1) [Deleted on December 28, 2011] 

(2) When a member receives an entrustment of order in writing, it shall be done in the 
form of order slip in which the customer filled out the details of entrustment under [§81] 
of the Regulation and signed or imprinted his/her seal thereon. (Amended on February 3, 
2009) 

(3) When a member receives an entrustment of order by the telephone, etc., the person 
receiving  the  order  shall  fill  out  the  order  slip  in  such  manner  as  noted  in  any  of  the 
following  subparagraphs  after  verifying  that  such  order  is  placed  by  the  customer 
himself/herself, and such member shall keep a record that can prove the details of order 
by using such devices as a tape-recorder, etc. for a certain period of time: (Amended on 
February 3, 2009; December 28, 2011) 

1. The order receiving staff shall write down the order details specified in [§81] of the 
Regulation on the order slip and sign or imprint his personal seal thereon; and   

2.  The  order-receiving  staff  shall  input  the  order  details  specified  in  [§81]  of  the 
Regulation into the member computer system and sign or affix his personal seal on the 
printed copy of the order slip (hereinafter referred to as "computer order slip").   

(4) Each member shall, when intending to use the computer order slip, observe each of 
the following requirements:   

1. The order details shall be input into the member computer system without delay as 
the order is received;   

2. The member system shall be able to automatically record the time of input;   

3. The member system shall be able to record the identification of the person inputting 
the order details into the system;   

146 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
4.  In  cases  where  the  order  details  inputted  are  corrected  or  cancelled,  the  member 
system shall be able to keep the record of such cancellation or correction; and   

5. In cases where a customer or the Exchange requests for the details of an order, etc., 
the member shall be able to make available the requested information in a form that is 
easily understandable.   

(5) When a member receives an order via electronic communication means, such order 
shall be placed by a system meeting the following requirements, and such member shall 
have  entered  into  an  agreement  with  the  customer  for  the  entrustment  via  electronic 
communication means in advance: (Amended on February 3, 2009; June 21, 2016) 

1. The member shall be able to verify if the user is a legitimate user of the system;   

2. It shall be possible for a customer to confirm the details of order when placing an 
order;   

3. There shall be a system in place to record and maintain the details of the declined 
orders when a member refuses to receive an order because the details of the order do 
not meet the conditions of the entrustment agreement;   

4. It shall be possible for a customer to make inquiries about the order and its execution;   

4-2.  When  a  customer  request  for,  the  member  shall  be  able  to  submit  cancellation 
quotations at once without delay as requested; 

5. There shall be a system in place to prevent such practices as the unauthorized users 
from  submitting  orders,  withdrawing  or  transferring  cash  or  securities,  or  stealing 
information;   

6. The member shall maintain the record of data processing, including the details of the 
order handling and trade execution, and keep the details of orders, etc. by using the 
paper copies or electronic device; and   

7. The member shall be able to inform its customers any matter that the member or the 
Exchange deems it necessary to inform them.   

(6) In accordance with [§82(3)] of the Regulation, a member shall, when the trade has 
been executed according to the order submitted by a customer, promptly notify each of 
the following details to the relevant customer (including the notification by the telephone, 
etc. or via electronic communication means): (Amended on February 3, 2009; July 29, 
2010; December 28, 2011) 

1. Name of issue;   

2. Executed quantity and execution price. Provided that the member shall notify the 

147 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
execution  price  of  regular  session  auction-based  block  trade  and  off-hours  auction-
based  block  trade  to  the  customer  immediately  after  having  been  informed  by  the 
Exchange after the market closing;   

3. Classification for sale or purchase; and   

4. Other details that are deemed necessary by the member.   

(7) “Case specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§82(2)] of the Regulation 
shall mean a case where a member receives or process orders in the KRX KTB using the 
member debt securities terminals. [November 28, 2019] 

§110. Notification of Investment Risk, etc. 

Pursuant to [§83(1)] of the Regulation, in the case of falling under any of the following 
subparagraphs,  each  member  shall  post  a  notice  on  the  investment  risks  through  the 
electronic communication means, so that the customers can be aware of such risks, or 
urge the customers to take precaution regarding investment risks: (Amended on April 20, 
2012; July 23, 2020, September 22, 2020) 

1.  Where  posting  of  notice  is  deemed  necessary  for  the  protection  of  investors  or 
maintenance of trading order in the market as there is a sign of abnormal trading or 
abnormality in trading (referred to as "signs of abnormal trading, etc." hereinafter in 
this Article) of specific issues;   

2. Where the Exchange requests the members to send a notice of investment risk to the 
customers or urge the customer to take precaution because of the occurrence of signs 
of abnormal trading, etc. mentioned in paragraph (1); 

3. Where an issue is designated as an investment precaution issue; 

    4. Temporary overheated; and (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

    5. Where an issue is scheduled to be delisted. 

Section 3. Good Faith Deposits 

§111. Notification Deadline of Guidelines for Collection of Good Faith Deposits 

“Period stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§87(3)] of the Regulation shall refer to 
the period of five (5) trading days from the day when the relevant guidelines for collection 
of good faith deposits become effective.   

§111-2. Separate Management of Good Faith Deposits and Restrictions on Use as 
Member Margins 

148 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(1) With regard to “shall manage the good deposits separately from their own assets” in 
[§87(5)] of the Regulation, members shall state the cash good faith deposits separately 
from the customer deposits in accounting.   

(2) With regard to “shall not use the good faith deposits as member margins” in [§87(5)] 
of the Regulation, members shall maintain the current assets over the current liabilities 
under [Attached Table 10] and [Attachment 1] of the Detailed Regulations on Financial 
Investment Business. 

(3) [Deleted on February 27, 2025] 

[September 19, 2017] 

§111-3. Amount of Basic Deposits 

(1) “Cash amount stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§87-2(1)] of the Regulation 
shall be the amount that the member determines per customer within the amount specified 
in  any  of  following  subparagraphs,  by  taking  into  account  the  customer’s  object  of 
investment,  investment  experiences,  credit  status  and  other  matters  necessary  for 
understanding of customer. (Amended on July 23, 2020) 

1. ELWs: The amount stated in each of the following items. Provided that, in cases 

where a retail customer opens an account for ELW trades for the first time, the amount 

stated in item b) or c) shall apply; 

a) Phase 1: Equal to or more than KRW 5 million, but less than KRW 15 million; 

b) Phase 2: Equal to or more than KRW 15 million, but less than KRW 30 million;   

and 

c) Phase 3: Equal to or more than KRW 30 million. 

2. Securities noted in [§87-2(1)2] of the Regulation: The amount stated in each of the 
following items. Provided that, in cases where a retail customer opens an account for 
trades  of  securities  noted  in  [§87-2(1)2]  of  the  Regulation  for  the  first  time,  the 
amount stated in item b) or c) shall apply. 

a)  Phase 1: Less than KRW 10 million (including the exemption); 

b)  Phase 2: KRW 10 million; and 

c)  Phase 3: More than KRW 10 million, but less than KRW 30 million. 

3. [Deleted on July 23, 2020] 

(2)  Members  shall  establish  the  application  phase,  applicable  amount  per  phase, 
applicable period and other necessary matters under paragraph (1) (hereinafter referred to 

149 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
as the “standards for application of basic deposit”).   

(3)  In cases  where members establish or change  the standards for application of basic 
deposit,  they  shall  announce  it  in  advance  and  notify  the  Exchange  within  seven  (7) 
trading days from the application date. [July 23, 2020] 

(4) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), the Exchange may change the amount noted in each 
subparagraph of paragraph (1) if it is deemed necessary for the market management in 
view of the trading circumstances.   

[July 12, 2011] 

§112. Substitute Securities 

(1)  “Other  issues  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  item  (c)  of  [§88(2)2]  of  the

7,3(c)] of the KOSPI Market Listing Regulation. [February 28, 2017] (Amended on July 
23, 2020) 

(2) “Other issues specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§88(2)4] of the Regulation shall 
refer to the securities  falling under any of the following  subparagraphs:  (Amended on 
August 26, 2005; February 3, 2009; September 13, 2013; February 28, 2017; September 
7, 2017; September 19, 2017)   

1. KOSDAQ-listed securities that were designated as substitute securities pursuant to 
the KOSDAQ Market Business Regulation;   

1-2. KONEX-listed securities that were designated as substitute securities pursuant to 
the KONEX Market Business Regulation; 

2. Beneficiary certificates under Article189 of the Act and unlisted stocks of investment 
companies.  Provided  that  the  stocks  and  beneficiary  certificates  of  privately  placed 
funds under Article 9(19) of the Act shall be excluded; and   

3. Listed beneficiary certificates other than those under Article189 of the Act.
