§122. Special Cases concerning Collection of Good Faith Deposits 

“Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§89(2)2] of the Regulation shall refer to 
a case where the number of days when the payment for the securities sold has not been 
made by the settlement date is five (5) or more during the latest six (6) months and the 
aggregate amount of settlement shortage exceeds KRW 1 billion. [December 18, 2013]   

Section 4. Processing of Orders 

§123. Order Processing 

(1) Each member shall, when receiving orders in writing or by the telephone, etc. pursuant 
to [§91] of the Regulation, promptly and accurately input the details of orders into the 
input device of member computer systems (hereinafter referred to as "order input device") 
in the sequence of order receipt.   

(2) Each member shall, in cases where the order input devices of some business offices 
have broken down, the orders received shall be processed by using the order input devices 
in its headquarters or other business offices.   

151 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(3) Each member may, when the failure of the order input device prevents the processing 
of orders using the methods noted in paragraphs (1) and (2), process the orders by the 
methods otherwise specified by the Exchange.   

(4) [Deleted on December 28, 2011] 

§124. Orders according to Sales Agent Contracts, etc. 

(1) Each member shall, when entering into a sales agent contract for LPBs with a sales 
agent pursuant to [§95(2)] of the Regulation, specify each of the following matters.  In 
such cases, the relevant member shall notify the details thereof to the Exchange without 
delay.   

1. Matters relating to the methods of sales agent;   
2. Matters relating to order price;   
3. Matters relating to settlement of payment;   
4. Matters relating to agent commission; and   
5. Other matters necessary for sales agent.   

(2) The LPBs eligible for sales agent pursuant to paragraph (1) shall be limited to those 
bonds that have been sold by the relevant sales agent; in this case, the member shall place 
an ask quotation at a reported market price at the time of the market closing. (Amended 
on July 16, 2015) 

(3) Each member shall, when its sales agent has placed a quotation by aggregating orders 
submitted through a joint account, notify the Exchange the details of orders before the 
aggregation in person or by facsimile, in case the Exchange requests such details as they 
are deemed necessary for the market management.   

(4) Any other matters necessary for sales agent shall be determined through the agreement 
between the contracting parties.   

Section 5. Brokerage Commission 

§125. Deadline for Notification of Brokerage Commission Schedule 

“Period stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§100(2)] of the Regulation shall mean 
five  (5)  trading  days  from  the  date  when  the  relevant  brokerage  commission  schedule 
become effective.   

CHAPTER VII. MARKET MANAGEMENT 

152 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§126. Publication of Quotation Information, etc. 

(1) Pursuant to [§101(1)5] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall officially announce the 
details  of  quotation  information  specified  in  each  of  the  following  subparagraphs: 
(Amended  on  May  29,  2006;  February  3,  2009;  July  29,  2010;  September  2,  2014; 
February 27, 2025) 

1.  During  the  quotation  receiving  hours  for  call  auction,  the  prices  of  three  (3) 
successive  expected  best  quotations  and  the  quantities  at  such  prices,  including  the 
expected matching price, expected matching quantity and the prices of best expected 
bid and offer quotations. Provided that, during the quotation receiving hours for the 
determination  of  opening  price,  such  quotation  information  shall  be  published  after 
twenty (20) minutes have elapsed from the beginnings of the quotation receiving hour. 
(Amended on February 27, 2025) 

2. During the quotation receiving hours for continuous auction, ten (10) successive best 
quotation  prices  per  bid  and  offer  respectively,  including  the  best  expected  bid  and 
offer quotations, the quotation quantities at such prices and the total of such quotation 
quantities. Provided that, in cases where, for collective investment securities of ETFs, 
ETNs  or  ELWs,  a  liquidity  providing  quotation  submitted  is  among  the  ten  (10) 
successive  best  quotations,  such  information  may  be  kept  apart  and  published 
separately. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

    2-2. During the quotation receiving hours for continuous auction, mid-price and the 
quantity of mid-price quotation. In this case, such price and quantity shall be announced 
separately from the price and quantity announced in accordance with the main sentence 
of subparagraph 2, but if the input of mid-price quotation is restricted, it shall not be 
announced. [February 27, 2025] 

3.  During  the  quotation  receiving  hours  for  off-hours  closing  price  trading,  total 
quotation quantity per bid and offer quotations.   

4. During the quotation receiving hours for regular session auction-based block trade, 
among the ask quotation and bid quotation, the quotation with unexecuted quantity.   

(2) The expected matching prices, etc. that  are  made public pursuant  to  paragraph (1) 
shall be calculated according to each of the following methods: (Amended on February 
3, 2009; July 15, 2022) 

1. Expected matching price and expected matching quantity: Of the quotations received 
as  of  the  relevant  time,  the  price  and  quantity  of  quotation  that  are  expected  to  be 
matched by the methods under the provisions of paragraphs (3) through (6) of [§23] of 
the Regulation;     

2. Prices and quantities of three (3) successive expected best quotations, including the 
price  of  expected  best  quotation:  The  prices  of  three  (3)  successive  expected  best 
quotations, including the price of expected best quotation per bid and offer, and the 

153 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
quantities at such prices. In such cases, when it is possible to establish the expected 
matching price pursuant paragraph (1), it shall be based on the best quotation for the 
case where such trade has been executed; and 

3.Notwithstanding subparagraphs 1 and 2, the Exchange may determine the calculation 
method and cycle of the expected execution price, etc. differently in case of excessive 
quotations,  system  failure,  and  other  cases  that  it  deems  necessary  for  market 
management. 

(3) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), in case of debt securities, the quotation information 
specified in each of the following subparagraphs shall be published: (Amended on May 
29, 2006; May 18, 2007; February 3, 2009; February 28, 2014) 

1. During the quotation receiving hours for call auction, total quotation quantity by bid 
and  offer.  Provided  that,  after  the  market  opening,  it  shall  be  the  prices  of  five  (5) 
successive best quotations per bid and offer that include the best bid and offer quotation 
prices, the quotation quantities at such prices and the total of such quotation quantities; 
and   

2. During the quotation receiving hours for continuous auction, the five (5) successive 
best quotation prices per bid and offer respectively, including the best expected bid and 
offer quotations, the quotation quantities at such prices and the total of such quotation 
quantities.   

(4) [Deleted on February 28, 2014] 

§127. Public Announcement of Reference Information for Investors 

Pursuant to [§101(2)] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall officially announce any of 
the  followings  as  the  reference  information  for  inventors:  (Amended  on  July  7,  2006; 
August 28, 2007; May 13, 2008; July 29, 2010; June 21, 2016)   

1. The issues traded by way of the regular session block trading, regular session basket 
trading, off-hours block trading or off-hours basket trading;   

1-2. The issues traded by way of regular session auction-based block trade and off-
hours auction-based block trade;   

2.  The  issues  for  which  the  treasury  stocks  of  stock-listed  corporations  were  traded 
(including the trading of treasury stocks under trust contracts); 

3. [Deleted on August 28, 2007]   

4. The top twenty (20) issues in terms of daily turnover ratio; and   

5. The matters to be disclosed with respect to net holding balance prescribed in Article 
180-3 of the Act; 

154 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
6. Details of the net holding balance aggregated by issue, which was reported to the 
Exchange pursuant to Article 180-2 of the Act; and 

7.  Additionally,  the  matters  that  the  Exchange  deems  them  useful  for  making  the 
investment decisions. 

§128. Publication Methods of Market Prices, etc. 

The public announcement of market prices, etc. pursuant to [§101(3)] of the Regulation 
shall be made in accordance with any of the following methods:   

1. Posting on the securities information devices;   

2. Publication in the Daily Stock Market Review (available only in Korean); and   

3.  Posting  on  the  electronic  information  dissemination  medium  operated  by  the 
Exchange.   

§129. Notification to Members 

(1)  Pursuant  to  [§103]  of  the  Regulation,  the  Exchange  shall  notify  the  matter  falling 
under any of the following subparagraphs to its members: (Amended on August 28, 2007; 
October 22, 2012; February 28, 2017; July 23, 2020, November 26, 2020; April 12, 2023) 

1.  Amendments  to  the  Membership  Regulation,  the  KOSPI  Market  Business 
Regulation, the KOSPI Market Listing Regulation and the KOSPI Market Disclosure 
Regulation;   

2. Issues of initial listing, relisting, listing change and delisting; administrative issues; 
temporarily  overheated  issue,  investment  precaution  issues,  issues  of  investment 
caution  and  investment  risk;  issues  suspended  from  trading;  issues  scheduled  to  be 
delisted; low liquidity issues subject to call auction; different classes of stock issues 
subject  to  call  auction;  overheated  short  sale  issues;  and  call  auction  issues  with 
abnormally soaring prices; 

3. Temporary closing of the market, temporary suspension of the market, trading halt 
and changes in trading hours;   

4. Admission and withdrawal of members;   

5. Suspensions of membership and termination of such suspensions;   

6. Suspensions of members from trading and termination of such suspensions;   

7. Measures for payment prior to placing quotation or payment prior to settlement; and   

155 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
8. Additionally, other matters for which the disclosure is deemed necessary.   

(2) The notification to members pursuant to paragraph (1) shall be made by any of the 
following methods: (Amended on February 28, 2017) 

1. Posting on the electronic information delivery devices operated by the Exchange;   

2. Posting on the securities information devices;   

3. Publication in the Daily Stock Market Review (available only in Korean); and   

4. Notification in writing.   

§130. Method of Reporting Algorithmic Trading Account 

The reporting of algorithmic trading accounts by members pursuant to [§104-2(2)] of the 
Regulation shall be made by inputting a report prepared in accordance with [Annex: Form 
No. 1-2] into the Exchange system via the member system by 18:00 hours. 

[December 22, 2022] 

§130-2. Methods and Trades for Application for Quotation Processing by Account, 
etc. 

(1) The “case specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§104-2(3)] of the 
Regulation shall refer to regular the session auction-based block trade and the basket trade. 

(2) The request for quotation processing by account by members pursuant to [§104-2(3)] 
of the Regulation shall be conducted by the way of entering the matters noted in each of 
the following subparagraphs into the Exchange system via member system or member 
securities terminals: 

1. Algorithmic trading account number (limited to the account that was reported as an 

algorithmic trading account no later than the day before the date of request); 

2. Types and details of the quotation processing by account. In such cases, the details 

shall be classified as follows: 

(a) In the case of quotation processing by account pursuant to [§104-2(3)1] of the 
Regulation: Cancellation of all quotations received in the regular session; and 

(b) In the case of quotation processing by account pursuant to [§104-2(3)2] of the 
Regulation:  Blocking  the  receipt  of  additional  new  quotations,  correction 
quotations and cancellation quotations (excluding cancellation quotations in the off-
hours session). 

156 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
3. Other matters that the Exchange deems necessary. 

(3) Upon the request of members pursuant to paragraph (2), the Exchange shall perform 
the  quotation  processing  by  account  after  verifying  the  matters  noted  in  each  of  the 
subparagraphs. 

(4) The member who has requested for the quotation processing by account may request 
for the termination of such processing by the methods specified in paragraph (2) from the 
time  when  10  minutes  have  elapsed  since  the  request  for  the  quotation  processing  by 
account,  and,  in  cases  where  the  member  does  not  request  for  the  termination,  the 
Exchange may terminate the quotation processing by account at the closing time of off-
hours sessions after the market close of the day. 

(5)  Notwithstanding  paragraphs  (2)  and  (4),  the  Exchange  may,  in  the  case  of  system 
failures and other cases that are deemed necessary for the market management, refuse a 
member’s request for the quotation processing by account or request for the termination 
from such processing. 

(6) When a member has requested for the quotation processing by account, the member 
shall  keep  the  records  and  materials  related  to  the  quotation  processing  by  account, 
including the details of system failures, etc., for 10 years. 

[December 22, 2022] 

§131. Registration of High-speed Algorithmic Trader, etc. 

(1) Registration or reporting pursuant to [§104-3(1) and (2)] of the Regulation shall be 

made by a member’s inputting all matters in each of the following subparagraphs through 

member system. Provided that, in the case where a member reports itself as a high-speed 

algorithmic trader, matters in subparagraphs 1 and 4 shall be excluded: 

    1. Matters concerning the fulfilment of the requirement in each subparagraph of [§104-

3(1)] of the Regulation; 

    2. Information about a customer or member as information that can identify the subject 

of registration, such as mane or trade name; 

    3. Application for registration in accordance with [Annex Form 20]; 

    4.  Confirmation  on  inspection  of  registration  information,  etc.  in  accordance  with 

[Annex Form 21]; and 

157 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
    5. Other matters that the Exchange deems necessary. 

(2) In the case where there is a change in the matters registered or reported pursuant to 
paragraph (1), the member shall input the changed matter through the member securities 
terminal without delay.   

(3)  “The  requirements  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§104-3(1)3]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to all of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  The customer shall have a management system such as an internal control 

organization  and  two  (2)  or  more  of  professional  personnel  in  order  to  efficiently 
manage risks that may arise from high-speed algorithmic trading. Provided that, with 
regard to the risks that occurs from high-speed algorithmic trading, any of the following 
items shall be deemed to meet the relevant requirement: 

        (a) When a member directly conducts risk management; and   

        (b) Where a member judges that the customer can recognize, evaluate, monitor, and 

control risks in a timely manner.   

2. Other matters that the Exchange deems necessary for market management, etc. 

(4) When a member registers or reports itself as a high-speed algorithmic trader pursuant 
to paragraph (1), the Exchange shall process it without delay. In such case, the Exchange 
may ask the member to supplement if there is a defect in the registration or report. 

(5) The Exchange shall issue a trader registration number that can be commonly used in 
the KOSPI market, KOSDAQ market, KONEX market, and derivatives market for each 
high-speed algorithmic trader who has completed registration and reporting. In such case, 
the high-speed algorithmic trader can set the risk management number (referring to the 
two (2) digit number set by the high-speed algorithmic trader to distinguish the range for 
applying  the  self-match  prevention  condition  pursuant  to  [§13-2]  and  the  mass  order 
cancellation pursuant to [§17-2]; the same hereinafter) to the relevant registration number.   

(6)  Pursuant  to  [§104-3(3)]  of  the  Regulation,  a  member  shall  connect  a  high-speed 
algorithmic  trading  number  and  a  high-speed  algorithmic  trading  account  through  the 
member system and report it to the Exchange. 

(7) The “case specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§104-3(5)3] of the Regulation shall 
refer to each of the following subparagraphs: 

    1. Where a customer takes out the ordering system from the member computer center, 

etc.; or 

    2. Where the Exchange recognizes that it is necessary for investor protection or the 

158 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
stability of trading order in the market and notifies it to the member. 

(8) In case where all members that have received orders from a high-speed algorithmic 
trader cease to receive the orders pursuant to [§104-3(5)] of the Regulation, the Exchange 
may cancel the registration of the high-speed algorithmic trader of the relevant customer. 

[December 22, 2022] 

§131-2. Special Cases for Registration of High-speed Algorithmic Trader 

(1) In the case where the registration or reporting of a high-speed algorithmic trader is 
completed in accordance with any of the regulations of the KOSDAQ market, KONEX 
market, or derivatives market operated by the Exchange, the registration and reporting 
are also deemed to have been completed in the KOSPI market. 

(2)  In  the  case  where  multiple  customers  of  a  member  satisfy  all  of  the  following 
subparagraphs,  the  member  can  collectively  register  them  as  high-speed  algorithmic 
traders. In such case, the Exchange may issue a single trader registration number that can 
be jointly used by the relevant customers to a specific customer: 

    1.  The  customer  shall  be  an  affiliated  corporation  (including  a  foreign  corporation 

incorporated under foreign laws and regulations) of a specific customer; 

2. The customer and the affiliated corporation shall use the same trade ordering system; 
and 

3. The member shall verify whether the registration requirements stated in [§104-3(1)] 
of the Regulation are met for all of the multiple customers. 

[December 22, 2022] 

§131-3. High-speed Algorithmic Trading through Multiple Members 

In  case  where  a  member  intends  to  receiver  orders  for  high-speed  algorithmic  trading 
from a customer who has completed the registration as a high-speed algorithmic trader, 
the member shall apply for the right to use the trader registration number of the relevant 
customer to the Exchange. In such case, the latter part of [§104-3(1)] of the Regulation 
and [§131(1) (excluding subparagraph 3) through (4)] of these Enforcement Rules shall 
apply mutatis mutandis to the relevant application.   

[December 22, 2022] 

§131-4. Member’s Obligation to Manage High-speed Algorithmic Trading 

(1) Pursuant to [§104-4(1)] of the Regulation, a member shall inspect electronic system 
in order to verify whether the electronic systems including ordering system, etc. used by 
a  customer  has  sufficient  stability  and  adequacy  to  carry  out  high-speed  algorithmic 

159 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
trading as specified in each of the following subparagraphs: 

    1. Matters concerning inspection of electronic system, etc. related to the registration 
stated  in  [§104-3]  of  the  Regulation;  A  member  shall  prepare  the  standards  and 
procedures for electronic system inspection, conduct the inspection of the electronic 
system thoroughly through the linkage tests with trade ordering system by the customer 
before applying for the registration, and file the results with the Exchange; 

    2. Matters concerning regular inspection: A member shall inspect the connection with 
the customer’s electronic system on a regular basis every year. Provided that, if the 
member  conducted  the  inspection  on  a  timely  basis  due  to  the  change  of  electronic 
system, etc. during the relevant year, it shall be deemed that the inspection pursuant to 
the main clause is completed and   

    3.  Other  matters  that  the  Exchange  deems  necessary  for  the  stable  operation  of  the 

electronic system, etc. 

(2)  Pursuant  to  [§104-4(1)]  of  the  Regulation,  a  member  shall  establish  appropriate 
internal control mechanism for the management of risks and the prevention of financial 
accidents related to the high-speed algorithmic trading of customers as specified in each 
of following subparagraphs: 

    1. Matters concerning the granting of order limits: A member shall grant an appropriate 
order  limit  by  evaluating  the  financial  stability,  credit  rating,  etc.  and  check  the 
adequacy of the relevant limit on the regular basis; 

    2. Matters concerning the monitoring of trades: A member shall monitor and supervise 
whether a customer complies with relevant regulations and internal control standards 
through the monitoring of high-speed algorithmic trading; and 

    3. Matters concerning the response to accidents and failures: A member shall prepare 
appropriate  control and response system  including  manuals  to  effectively cope with 
accidents  or  failures  related  to  high-speed  algorithmic  trading  of  customers  and 
minimize damage.   

(3) With respect  to  the request  for submitting materials  pursuant  to  [§104-4(2)] of the 
Regulation, A member shall record and maintain the following materials for ten (10) years 
and submit them if the Exchange requests for the market management, etc. 

    1. Materials on the registration of high-speed algorithmic traders and their trades; and 

    2. Results of inspection and supervision conducted pursuant to paragraphs (1) and (2) 

and related materials. 

[December 22, 2022] 

160 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§132. Action Dates of Ex-dividends, etc. 

(1) The date of action for ex-dividends, ex-rights or ex-distribution under [§105] of the 
Regulation shall be each of the following dates:   

1. It shall be the day before the record date on which a person who is entitled to exercise 
the right is determined (hereinafter referred to as "the record date"). In cases where the 
record date is a market holiday or in the middle of the closing period of the shareholder 
register, the record date  shall be deemed one  (1) day before the first  day  of market 
holidays or the commencement date of closing of the shareholder register; and   

2. It shall be the day on which trading halt is called off, in cases where the record date 
falls in the middle of the trading halt (excluding the first day of trading halt).   

(2) The date of action for ex-interests under [§105] of the Regulation shall be the date 
noted  in  each  of  the  following  subparagraphs:  (Amended  on  December  30,  2011; 
September 10, 2019; October 29, 2024) 

1. Same day settlement trade: 

The  interest  payment  date  (referring  to  the  commencement  date  of  registration 
suspension  in  the  case  of  registered  bonds  under  the  State  Bond  Act;  the  same 
hereinafter). Provided that, if the relevant date is a market holiday under subparagraph 
4 of [§5] of the Regulation, it shall be the following day; and 

2. Next day settlement trade: 

It shall be the day immediately preceding the interest payment date. Provided that it 
shall  be  the  day  preceding  the  relevant  date,  if  the  relevant  date  is  the  due  date  for 
holding reserve set by the Bank of Korea. (Amended on December 30, 2011) 

(3)  The  provisions  of  paragraph  (1)  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis  to  the  case  of 
determining the date of actions for ex-conversion of convertible bonds, ex-warrants of 
bonds with warrants, or ex-exchange of exchangeable bonds. In such cases, the record 
date shall be deemed the closing date of request for conversion in the case of convertible 
bonds, the closing date of exercising subscription rights in the case of bonds with warrant, 
and the closing date of request for exchange in the case of exchangeable bonds.   

(4) The calculation of the date of actions specified pursuant to paragraphs (1) through (3) 
shall be based on trading day.   

(5)  The  date  of  action  where  the  provisions  of  paragraphs  (1)  through  (4)  are  not 
applicable shall be set by the Exchange for each case.   

§133. Designation of Temporary Overheated Issues 

(1) “Standards specified in the Enforcement Rules” in each subparagraph of [§106-2(1)] 

161 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  cases  of  falling  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs  (excluding  the  different  classes  of  stock  issue  subject  to  call  auction 
specified in [§56-4(1)]) within ten (10) trading days from the day when the fact that there 
is a possibility of being designated as temporary overheated issue pursuant to [§133-2(1)] 
has been forewarned. (Amended on April 25, 2013; April 1, 2016; September 22, 2020) 

1. In cases where all the requirements in [§133-2(3)1 through 3] are met (limited to 
cases where the closing price - of the day in which the decision on whether or not the 
requirements are met - is higher than the closing price of the trading day immediately 
preceding the date of decision, and is higher than the closing price of the trading day 
immediately preceding the date of forewarning of designation);   

2.  In  cases  where  the  different  classes  of  stocks  meet  the  requirements  in  [§133-
2(3)4].]; and 

3.  For  the  issues  other  than  subparagraphs  1  and  2  (excluding  the  issues  that  were 
forewarned to be designated as temporary overheated issues pursuant to [§133-2(1)1]): 
cases of satisfying all of the standards noted in each of the subparagraphs of [§133-
2(3)] 

(2) The Exchange may designate the issue falling under any subparagraph of [§106-2(1)] 
of the Regulation as temporary overheated issue on the next trading day. Provided that 
this provision shall not apply in cases where the designation of an issue as a temporary 
overheated issue is deemed manifestly inappropriate, such as for an issue ranked within 
the top 100 based on the value obtained by multiplying the closing price of the preceding 
trading day by the number of shares listed on the KOSPI or KOSDAQ Markets. 

[October 22, 2012] 

§133-2. Forewarning on Designation as Temporary Overheated Issue 

(1) In cases where an issue falls under any of the following subparagraphs (excluding the 
different classes of stock issues subject to call auction noted in [§56-4(1)]), the Exchange 
may forewarn the fact that there is a possibility for the relevant issue to be designated as 
a temporary overheated issue. (Amended April 25, 2013; April 1, 2016; September 22, 
2020) 

1. In cases where, within ten (10) trading days from the day - when all of the standards 
noted in subparagraph 1 through 3 of paragraph (3) were met and the closing price of 
the  same  day  was  higher  than  that  of  the  immediately  preceding  trading  day 
(hereinafter referred to as the “base day” in this Article) - all of the standards noted in 
subparagraph 1 through 3 of paragraph (3) are once again met (limited to the cases 
where the  closing price  -  of the day of  deciding  on whether the standards  are  once 
again met - is higher than the closing price of the immediately preceding day, and is 
higher than the closing price of the base day); and 

2.  In  cases  where  the  different  classes  of  stocks  once  again  meet  the  standards  in 

162 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
subparagraph 4 of paragraph (3) within ten (10) trading days from the next trading of 
the day when all of the standards noted in subparagraph 4 of paragraph (3) were met. 

(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), in case of issue that falls under any of the following 
subparagraphs, the Exchange may not forewarn the fact that there is a possibility of being 
designated as temporary overheated issue: (Amended on December 10, 2015) 

1. [Deleted on December 10, 2015] 

2. In addition, the issue for which forewarning of the fact that there is a possibility of 
being designated as temporary overheated issue is obviously inappropriate.   

(3)  The  Exchange  shall  calculate  the  standards  noted  in  each  of  the  following 
subparagraphs  for  each  issue.  In  such  cases,  numbers  shall  be  rounded  up  to  the  4th 
decimal place. (Amended on September 22, 2020) 

1. Rate of price increase: 

The closing price of the day shall be at least 130/100 higher than the average closing 
prices of recent forty (40) trading days. 

2. Turnover ratio: 

The average daily turnover ratio (to be calculated using the formula noted below) of 
recent two (2) days (based on the trading day of issue), including the  relevant day, 
shall be 600/100 higher than the average of daily turnover ratios of recent forty (40) 
trading days. 

Daily turnover ratio = Total value of the trades executed by continuous auction during 
the trading  hours of regular session of the day / (Closing  price of the day X Total 
number of listed shares)   

3. Stock price volatility: 

The average of stock price volatility for recent two (2) days (based on the trading day 
of issue), including the relevant day, shall be at least 150/100 higher than the average 
of daily price volatility of recent forty (40) trading days.   

Daily  stock  price  volatility  =  [Highest  price  (referring  to  the  price  established  by 
continuous auction during the trading hours of regular session of the day: the same 
hereinafter in this paragraph) – Lowest price]/ {[Highest price + Lowest price] / 2}   

4. Disparate ratio 

The  disparate  ratio  (calculated  by  the  below  formula)  between  the  price  of  the 
different classes of stock and the price of the relevant common stock based on the 
closing price of the day shall exceed zero point five (0.5). 

163 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
      Disparate ratio = (Price of different classes of stock – Price of relevant common stock) 

/ Price of relevant common stock 

(4)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (3),  for  the  issue  falling  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs,  the  criteria  noted  in  each  subparagraph  of  paragraph  (3)  shall  not  be 
calculated: (Amended on April 25, 2013; April 1, 2016; February 28, 2017; September 
22, 2020) 

1. A temporary overheated issue; 

2. An issue scheduled to be delisted;   

3. An issue suspended from trading; 

4. An issue for which the number of days with trades executed by continuous auction 
during the trading hours of regular sessions (including trading hours corresponding to 
the regular market of the Exchange among the trading hours of the multilateral trading 
company) during the latest forty (40) days is twenty (20) or less; and (Amended on 
February 27, 2025) 

5. An investment alert issue or an investment risk issue (including issues scheduled to 
be designated the next day as investment alert issues or investment risk issues) noted 
in [§5-3] of the Market Oversight Regulation. 

(5) For the issue that was released from the designation as temporary overheated issue 
pursuant to [§134], the base day (including the day when the issue under subparagraph 2 
of paragraph (1) first meets the standards in subparagraph 4 of paragraph (3)) may again 
be determined after the release date. (Amended on September 22, 2020) 

(6) “Average closing price” in paragraph (3)1, the “average of daily turnover ratio” in 
paragraph  (3)2  and  the  “average  of  daily  price  volatility”  in  paragraph  (3)3  shall  be 
calculated on the basis of trading day of the relevant issue.   

(7) The “total value of the trades executed by continuous auction during the trading hours 
of  regular  session  of  the  day”  in  paragraph  (3)2  shall  be  calculated  by  including  the 
trading value of the multilateral trading company (limited to the trading value during the 
trading hours corresponding to the regular market of the Exchange; the same hereinafter 
in  this  paragraph),  however,  in  the  case  where  the  Exchange  is  unable  to  receive 
information on trading value from a multilateral trading company, due to system failure, 
etc., such information may be excluded from the calculation. [February 27, 2025] 

[October 22, 2012] 

§134. Release from Designation as Temporary Overheated Issue, etc. 

(1) The Exchange shall release the issues designated as temporary overheated issues from 

164 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
such  designation  on  the  trading  day  after  the  three  (3)  trading  days  from  the  day  of 
designation. (Amended on April 25, 2013; December 10, 2015; April 1, 2016; September 
22, 2020) 

1 [Deleted on September 22, 2020].   

2. [Deleted on September 22, 2020] 

(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), in cases where the closing price of the day when the 
period specified in    paragraph (1) expires counting from the day of designation is higher 
than 120/100 of the closing price of the trading day immediately  preceding the day of 
designation  (excluding 
issues  designated  pursuant  only 
to[§133(1)2]),  the  issue  shall  be  released  from  the  designation  on  the  trading  day  that 
follows the day when the period specified in paragraph (1) expires counting from the next 
trading day immediately after.(Amended on April 15, 2013; December 10, 2015; April 1, 
2016; September 22, 2020) 

temporary  overheated 

(3)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1),  in  cases  where  the  closing  price  of  the  issues 
designated  as  temporary  overheated  issues  pursuant  to  [§133(1)2]  (including  the 
temporary overheated issues that fall under both [§133(1)1] and [§133(1)2]) meets the 
standard in [§133-2(3)4] on the day when the period specified in paragraph (1) ends, the 
designation shall be extended for the period specified in paragraph (1). In such cases, if 
the closing price meets the standard in [§133-2(3)4] on the day when the extended period 
ends, the designation shall be extended for the period specified in paragraph (1), and this 
provision shall apply repeatedly whenever the extended period ends. [September 22, 2020] 

(4) In cases where there has been ex-dividends, ex-rights, stock split-off or reserve stock 
split, etc., the “closing prices” noted in [§133(1)] and [§133-2(1)∙(3), (2) and (3)] shall be 
determined by taking such event into consideration. (Amended on September 22, 2020) 

[October 22, 2012] 

§134-2. Forewarning on Designation as Investment Precaution Bond Issue 

(1)  Pursuant  to  the  provisions  of  [§106-3(2)]  of  the  Regulation,  in  cases  where  a 
corporation falls under any of the following subparagraphs, the Exchange may issue a 
forewarning on the fact  that the listed debt security issued by the  relevant corporation 
may be designated as an investment precaution bond issue, by the trading day following 
the  day  on  which  the  relevant  ground  has  occurred:  (Amended  on  March  17,  2017; 
November 29, 2018; September 7, 2021) 

1. In cases where a bond-listed corporation has made a disclosure on the fact or 
decision about the matter that falls under any of the followings: 

(a) Filing of an application for corporate rehabilitation procedures;   

(b) Forfeiting of the benefits of time of listed debt securities; 

165 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(c) [Deleted on September 7, 2021] 

(d) Resolution at the meeting of bondholders. 

2. In cases where the closing price of an issue of corporate bonds falls under any of 
the followings. Provided that this provision shall not apply when the day’s trading 
volume is less than KRW 100 million. 

(a) Case of falling below 80/100 of the face value; and 

(b)  Case  of  rising  or  falling  by  15%  or  more  from  the  closing  price  of  the 
immediately preceding trading day. 

(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), in cases where it is deemed inappropriate to view that 
the matter disclosed is related to the rights, earnings or handling of listed debt securities, 
or where it falls under the issue scheduled to be delisted, the Exchange may not issue the 
forewarning  on  the  possible  designation  as  an  investment  precaution  bond  issue. 
(Amended on November 29, 2018) 

(3) In the case of falling under any of the following subparagraphs, the Exchange may 
release the relevant issue from the forewarning on designation. (Amended on March 17, 
2017; November 29, 2018; September 7, 2021) 

1. Case of having been forewarned on designation as an investment precaution bond 
issue pursuant to paragraph (1)1 and falling under any of the following items. Provided 
that,  when  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary  for  public  interests  and  protection  of 
investors,  or  maintaining  of  trading  order  in  the  market,  the  release  from  the 
forewarning on designation may not carried out. 

(a) For a case of having been forewarned on the ground noted in paragraph (1)1(a); 
when  the  relevant  bond-listed  corporation  has  made  a  disclosure  of  the  fact  or 
decision on the closing of the corporate rehabilitation procedures;   

(b) For a case of having been forewarned on the ground noted in paragraph (1)1(b); 
when  the  revocation  of  the  forfeiting  of  benefits  of  time  takes  effect  by  the 
resolution  of  the  bondholders’  meeting,  or  when  the  fact  of  revocation  of  the 
forfeiting of benefits of time is recognized by the Exchange; or   

(c) For a case of having been forewarned on the grounds noted in paragraph (1)1(d); 
when the resolution of the bondholders’ meeting takes effect. 

2.  In  cases  where  an  issue  that  was  forewarned  on  designation  as  an  investment 
precaution  bond  issue  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1)2  meets  all  of  the  following 
requirements: 

(a)The closing prices in the latest six (6) months shall remain above 80/100 of the 

166 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
face  value  (including  the  cases  with  no  trades;  the  same  hereinafter  in  this 
Subparagraph); and 

(b)The closing prices for the latest five (5) trading days shall not rise or fall by 8% 
or more from the closing price of the immediately preceding trading day. 

[November 23, 2016] 

§134-3. Designation as Investment Precaution Bond Issues 

“Requirements specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§106-3(1)] of the Regulation shall 
refer to the case when the closing price of an issue that was forewarned on the possible 
designation  as  an  investment  precaution  bond  issue  pursuant  to  [§134-2]  has  risen  or 
fallen  by  15%  or  more  from  the  closing  price  [it  shall  be  the  closing  price  of  the  day 
before  two  (2)  trading  days,  only  if  there  was  no  closing  price  on  the  immediately 
preceding  trading  day  as  the  trading  was  suspended  pursuant  to  [§49(1)2]  of  the 
Regulation] of the immediately preceding trading day (excluding a case where the day’s 
trading volume is less than KRW 100 million or an issue scheduled to be delisted). In 
such cases, the designation date shall be the following trading day. (Amended on March 
17, 2017; November 29, 2018; July 23, 2020) 

[November 23, 2016] 

§134-4. Release from Designation as Investment Precaution Bond Issues 

Pursuant to [§106-3(2)] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall release the issue designated 
as an investment precaution issue from such designation on the trading day following the 
date of designation. 

[November 23, 2016] 

§134-5. Forewarning on Designation as Investment Precaution Issue 

(1) Pursuant to [§106-4(2)] of the Regulation, in cases where an issue falls under all of 
the following subparagraphs, the Exchange may, on the next trading day, forewarn the 
fact that the concerned issue may be designated as an investment precaution issue : 

1. The immediate disparate ratio at the market closing is two (2) times or higher than 

the ratio specified in [§20-4(2) or (3)] of the Regulation; and 

2. Falls under the situation in subparagraph 1 again within ten (10) trading days after 

falling under the situation in subparagraph 1.   

(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), the Exchange may not forewarn the fact that there is 
a possibility of being  designated as an investment  precaution issue in  cases where the 
issue falls under any of the following subparagraphs: 

167 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. An issue designated as an investment precaution issue; 

2. An issue suspended from trading; 

3. In cases  where an error occurs in  calculating the  immediate disparate ratio at the                           
market closing due to the computer system failure of the Exchange or the institution 
that calculates the underlying index and the  immediate disparate ratio at  the market 
closing; and 

4. In cases where it is deemed inappropriate to forewarn the possible designation as                                                                     
an investment precaution issue. 

[July 23, 2020] 

§134-6. Designation as Investment Precaution Issue 

(1) “The criteria stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§106-4(1)] of the Regulation 
shall refer to cases falling under any of the following subparagraphs. In such cases, the 
following trading day shall be the designation day. 

1. In cases where the issue that has been forewarned to be designated as an investment 
precaution  issue  pursuant  to  [§134-5(1)]  falls  under  [§134-5(1)1]  within  ten  (10) 
trading days from the day of the forewarning; and 

2.  In  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  the  designation  as  an  investment  precaution 
issue is necessary for investor protection in consideration of the quotation situations and 
the trading conditions. 

(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), the Exchange may not designate the concerned issue 
as an investment precaution issue in cases where it falls under any of the subparagraphs 
in [§134-5(2)]. 

[July 23, 2020] 

§134-7. Release from Designation as Investment Precaution Issue 

(1) The issues designated as investment precaution issues pursuant to [§134-6(1)1] shall 
be released from such designation on the trading day after three (3) trading days from the 
date of designation (hereinafter referred to as the “designated unit period” in this Article). 
Provided that, in cases where the issue falls under any of the following subparagraphs, a 
new  designated  unit  period  shall  begin  from  the  date  specified  in  the  concerned 
subparagraph: 

1. In cases where the immediate disparate ratio at the market closing exceeds the ratio 

168 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
specified  in  [§20-4(2)  or  (3)]  of  the  Regulation  for  one  (1)  or  more  days  during  the 
designated unit period: The trading day after the day on which the designated unit period 
ends; and 

2. In cases where the trading of the issue is suspended pursuant to [§26(1)2-3] of the 

Regulation: The day on which the trading is resumed. 

(2) The issues designated as investment precaution issues pursuant to [§134-6(1)2] shall 
be  released  from  the  designation  considering  the  quotation  situation  and  the  trading 
situation. 

[July 23, 2020] 

§135. Suspension of Trading of Investment Risk Issues, etc. 

(1)  Pursuant  to  [§107(2)]  of  the  Regulation,  upon  receiving  the  request  for  trading 
suspension  pursuant  to  [§5-3]  of  the  Market  Oversight  Regulation,  the  Exchange  may 
suspend the trading of the relevant issue for the period requested. Provided that, in cases 
where  it  is  deemed  necessary  for  the  investor  protection  and  market  stability  due  to 
sudden changes in the market situation, etc., the Exchange may set the period of trading 
suspension differently or take the following additional measures from the date of release 
from the trading suspension:(Amended on January 30, 2008; March 8, 2012; February 28, 
2017) 

1. Change of the trade execution methods specified in paragraphs (1) through (4) of 
[§56-2]; 

2. Change of the price change limits specified in [§20(2)] of the Regulation; 

3. Change of the rates specified in paragraphs (1) and (2) of [§41-2]; and 

4. Other measures that are deemed necessary for the market management. 

(2) When taking the measure of trading suspension or any additional measures pursuant 
to paragraph (1), the Exchange shall officially announce such fact immediately. [February 
28, 2017] 

(Wholly amended on August 28, 2007) 

CHAPTER VIII. SUPPLEMENTARY PROVISIONS 

§136. Notification of Trade Details 

(1) Pursuant to [§110(1)] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall, when a trade has been 

169 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
executed,  notify  its  members  of  each  of  the  following  trade  details  without  delay: 
(Amended on February 3, 2009; July 29, 2010) 

1. Member’s ID number;   

2. Name of issue;   

3. Executed quantity and execution price. Provided that the Exchange shall notify the 
execution  price  of  regular  session  auction-based  block  trade  and  off-hours  auction-
based block trade to the member immediately after the market closing;   

4. Classification of purchase or sale;   

5. Classification of self-account transaction or customer-account transaction; and   

6. Any other details that the Exchange deems them necessary.   

(2)  Pursuant  to  [§110(2)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  Exchange  shall  notify  the  designated 
clearing members each of the following details of the trades executed under the names of 
non-clearing members after the market closing: (Amended on July 7, 2007; February 3, 
2009) 

1. ID number of non-clearing member;   

1-2. Name of issue;   

2. Quantities sold, and quantities purchased;   

3. Sale amount and purchase amount; and   

4. Any other details that the Exchange deems them necessary. Provided that it shall be 
limited to the details for which the prior consent of the non-clearing member has been 
obtained.   

(3) Notification of trade details pursuant to paragraphs (1) and (2) shall be accomplished 
by  transmitting  the  details  to  the  member  computer  systems.  In  such  cases,  when  the 
members received the notification of trade details, it shall be deemed that the members 
have confirmed the relevant trade details. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

§137. Request for Auction, etc. 

(1) The request for auction pursuant to [§112(1)] of the Regulation shall be restricted to 
those securities that are not listed on the KOSPI Market and KOSDAQ Market. Provided 
that,  when  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary,  listed  securities  may  also  be  auctioned. 
(Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(2) Any person who is not a securities member shall not be allowed to submit bids on an 

170 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
auction.  Provided  that,  if  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary,  anyone  who  wishes  to 
purchase may be allowed to participate. (Amended on February 3, 2009) 

(3) When the Exchange receives an entrustment of auction, the information necessary for 
such auction, including the name of issue, quantity, proposed price, time of auction and 
commission, shall be determined in writing in advance.   

(4) Any person who entrusts an auction shall deposit the security to be auctioned with the 
Exchange  after  taking  necessary  steps  for  the  transfer  of  rights.  Provided  that,  if  the 
security  to  be  auctioned  is  a  security  that  is  electronically  registered  pursuant  to  the 
Electronic  Securities  Act,  such  security  shall  be  electronically  registered  with  an 
electronic  registry  with  a  restriction  on  transfer  between  accounts,  instead  of  being 
deposited,  until  the  rights  are  transferred  subsequent  to  the  auction.  (Amended  on 
September 10, 2019) 

(5)  The  quantity  unit,  quotation  units  and  any  other  necessary  matters  relating  to 
auctioning of the securities shall be determined by the Exchange. (Amended on February 
3, 2009) 

(6)  In  cases  where  the  government  is  the  one  who  entrusted  the  auction  and  the 
entrustment conditions are different from this Article, the entrustment conditions of the 
government shall take precedence, except the conditions stipulated in [§141]. (Amended 
on February 3, 2009) 

§138. Methods for Determining Bidders, etc. 

(1) As a case of bidding method pursuant to [§112(4)] of the Regulation, when bidders 
with  the  same  unit  price  compete,  the  bidders  shall  be  determined  according  to 
proportional allocation in cases where there is insufficient remaining quantity.   

(2)  The  successful  bidders  shall  enter  into  a  bid  agreement  in  accordance  with  the 
agreement specially devised by the Exchange by the date determined by the Exchange.   

(3) Auction shall be carried out at the time and date determined by the Exchange, and the 
Exchange  shall  make  public  the  time,  date  and  place  of  auction  and  other  necessary 
matters  at  least  five  (5)  days  before  the  auction  date.  Provided  that  the  duration  of 
announcement may be shortened if the Exchange deems it necessary.   

(4) While making announcement pursuant to paragraph (1), the expenses for adverting in 
the  publications  such  as  newspaper  and  other  special  expenses  shall  be  borne  by  the 
person who entrusts the auction. Provided that an exception may be made in cases where 
the government is the consignor.   

(5) The Exchange shall prepare a register, record the details of each auction, and keep 
them.   

171 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§139. Bid Guarantee 

(1)  Anyone  who  intends  to  bid  on  auction  shall  deposit  with  the  Exchange  the  bid 
guarantee in cash or cashier’s check issued by the banks, which is equivalent to 10/100 
of bid price on auction by the date determined by the Exchange.   

(2) The bid guarantee deposited by the successful bidders shall be appropriated as a part 
of bid price. Provided that, in cases where a successful bidder does not enter into the bid 
agreement  pursuant  to  [§138(2)],  the  relevant  bid  shall  be  made  invalid,  and  the  bid 
guarantee deposited shall not be returned.   

(3) When the successful bidders at the lowest unit price according to the bidding method 
were determined according to the proportional allocation method, the amount exceeding 
the bid guarantee applicable to the successful bid quantity may be refunded.   

(4) The Exchange shall refund the bid guarantee deposited by the unsuccessful bidders 
without delay.   

§140. Successful Bidding Amount 

(1)  A  successful  bidder  shall  pay  the  successful  bidding  amount,  after  deducting  the 
amount of bid guarantee money deposited pursuant to [§139], within five (5) days from 
the successful biding and receive the relevant security (in the case of a security that is 
electronically  registered  pursuant  to  the  Electronic  Securities  Act,  it  shall  be 
accomplished by the electronic registration of transfer to the successful bidder’s customer 
account). (Amended on September 10, 2019) 

(2) In cases where the successful bidder fails to make the payment of remaining successful 
bidding amount by the date specified in paragraph (1), such bid shall be made invalid, 
and the bid guarantee money deposited shall not be returned.   

§141. Commission Fee for Auction Entrustment 

Any  person  who  entrusted  the  auction  shall  pay  the  commission  fee  for  auction 
entrustment to the Exchange, which is sum of the amounts calculated by applying each 
of successive rates to the successful bidding amount of each issue, at the time of receiving 
the  successful  bidding  amount.  Provided  that,  in  cases  where  the  consignor  is  the 
government or a corporation that is equivalent thereto and recognized by the Exchange 
as necessary, 1/2 of the respective rate shall apply. (Amended on September 10, 2019) 

- For a successful bidding amount equal to or less than KRW 100 million: 3/1,000; 
- For a successful bidding amount more than KRW 100 million, but equal to or less than 
KRW 500 million: 2/1,000; and 
- For a successful bidding amount more than KRW 500 million: 1/1,000 

§142. Public Opinion Gathering 

172 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Public opinion gathering pursuant to [§112-2] of the Regulation shall be governed by the 
provisions of [§5] of the Internal Regulations Management Regulation and [§6] of the 
Regulations Management Regulation. 

[May 7, 2020] 

ADDENDA 
(Regulation No. 17 / January 24, 2005)   

§1. Effective Date   

These  Enforcement  Rules  shall  become  effective  on  the  date  when  the  Exchange  is 
incorporated.  Provided  that  [§12(1)6,  (13),  (15)  &  (17)],  [§14(1)1&3],  [§23]  through 
[§25], [§27(1)3], [§28], [§48(1)2], [§49], [§50], [§52(2)], subparagraphs 6, 7(d) and 9 of 
[§108], [§127(1)] and [§131] shall become effective on March 28, 2005.   

§2. Abolition of Previous Enforcement Rules   

Beginning  with  the  date  when  these  Enforcement  Rules  became  effective,  the 
Enforcement  Rules  of  the  Business  Regulation  of  the  Korea  Stock  Exchange  shall  be 
abolished. Provided that the relevant provisions of the Enforcement Rules of the Business 
Regulation of the Korea Stock Exchange shall apply until the effective date of provisions 
specified in the proviso to [§1] of Addendum.   

§3. Interim Measures for Agreement for Correction of Transaction Error   

At the time when these Enforcement Rules become effective, the agreement for correction 
of transaction error that the members signed previously with the Korea Stock Exchange 
shall be construed as the agreement that was signed by the members and the Exchange 
pursuant to these Enforcement Rules.   

§4. Interim Measures for Application for Trading of Treasury Stocks   

At the time when these Enforcement Rules become effective, the application for trading 
of treasury stocks that was submitted under the Business Regulation of the Korea Stock 

173 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Exchange shall be construed as the application submitted pursuant to these Enforcement 
Rules.   

§5. Interim Measures for LPB Dealers 

At the time when these Enforcement Rules become effective, LPB dealers who have been 
designated pursuant to the Enforcement Rules of Business Regulation of the Korea Stock 
Exchange shall be construed as those designated pursuant to these Enforcement Rules.   

§6. Interim Measures for Surveillance Issues   

At the time when  these  Enforcement  Rules become effective, the issues  designated as 
surveillance issue pursuant to the Enforcement Rules of the Business Regulation of the 
Korea Stock Exchange shall be construed as the issues designated as abnormally rising 
issues pursuant to these Enforcement Rules.   

ADDENDUM 
(Regulation No. 88 / May 13, 2005)   

These  Enforcement  Rules  shall  become  effective  on  May  30,  2005.  Provided  that  the 
amended provisions of [§12 {except paragraph (1) 6} and §32] shall become effective on 
July 18, 2005.   

ADDENDA   
(Regulation No. 103 / August 26, 2005)   

§1. Effective Date   

These Enforcement Rules shall become effective on October 31, 2005. Provided that the 
amended provisions of [§76] shall become effective on August 29, 2005, and the amended 
provisions of [§30], [§55] and [§135], [Annex 1] and [Annex 2] shall become effective 
September 1, 2005.   

§2. Provision about the Effective Date of the Regulation   

“The date specified in the Enforcement Rules” mentioned in the proviso to Addendum 
(July 22, 2005) of the Regulation shall be September 26, 2005.   

§3. Interim Measure relating to the issues using the first trading price as the base price   

The issues that have not established the base price when these Enforcement Rules become 
effective shall be deemed that they are listed on the effective date of these Enforcement 
Rules. In such cases, the issues of which trading has been halted shall be deemed that they 
are listed on the day its trading is resumed.

(Regulation No. 259 / May 18, 2007) 

§1. Effective Date   

176 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
These Enforcement Rules shall become effective on the date that the Exchange 
determines by taking into account such factors as the time required for computer system 
development.   

§2. Effective Date of Stock Market Business Regulation   

“The  date  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  Addenda  of  the  Stock  Market 
Business Regulation (dated May 11, 2007) shall be the effective date pursuant to [§1] of 
this Addenda. 

§3. Special Cases concerning Designation of the First Retail Primary Dealer 

When designating a retail primary dealer for the first time, it shall be done on the basis of 
assessment of the submission records of market-making quotations and trading records 
for the three (3) months from the effective date pursuant to paragraph (1) of this Addenda 
and the designation period shall be from the designation date to December 31, 2008.   

§4.  Special  Cases  concerning  Composition  of  Retail  Primary  Dealer  Designation 
Committee 

In  cases  where  the  Retail  Primary  Dealer  Designation  Committee  is  established  to 
designate the retail primary dealers for the first time, the members noted in [§99-10/4] 
shall be excluded.   

§5. Interim Measures Relating to the Designation of Retail Primary Dealers for the First 
Time 

The  retail  dealers,  who  have  been  participating  in  trading  of  retail  bonds  before  the 
designation  of  retail  primary  dealers  for  the  first  time,  shall  be  deemed  to  have  been 
designated as retail primary dealer.

ADDENDA 
(Regulation No. 390 / November 27, 2008) 

§1. Effective Date 

These Enforcement Rules shall become effective on December 1, 2008. 

§2. Interim Measures   

In cases where, as of the effective date of these Enforcement Rules, after acquiring the 
shares through the liquidity providing quotation submitted by a member, the number of 
shares held by a member exceeds 2/100 of the total number of listed shares (on the basis 
of the settlement  date) of  the relevant issue, the  obligation for submission  of liquidity 
providing bid quotation may be exempted after specifying the details noted in [§31-4(1)6-
2] in the agreement for liquidity provision.   

ADDENDA

of the Regulation), §28 and §64-2(2)] shall become effective on March 23, 2009.

of the KOSPI Market Business Regulation (Amended on January 28, 2009) shall refer to 
March 23, 2009.

§1. Effective Date 

These Enforcement Rules shall become effective on December 14, 2015. 

§2. Effective Date etc. of the KOSPI Market Business Regulation 

“The date specified by the Enforcement Rules” in Addenda of KOSPI Market Business 
Regulation (No.1246, amended on November 4, 2015) refers to December 14, 2015 in 
case of [§26], [§106-2] and [§107] of the amended provision. 

§3. Applicable Example of Release from Designation as Temporary Overheated Issue 

(1)In cases where the Market Oversight Commission requests the trading suspension of 
an  issue  on  the  trading  day  before  the  effective  day  pursuant  to  [§2]  of  Addenda,  the 
relevant issue shall not be designated as a temporary overheated issue notwithstanding 
[§106-2(1)2]. 

(2)The amended provision of [§134] shall apply to the temporary overheated issue that is 
designated at the first since the effective date of the Enforcement Rules. 

196 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§4. Interim Measures related to the Trading Suspension of Investment Risk Issues, etc. 

In cases where an issue is designated as a temporary overheated issue as of the trading 
day before the effective day pursuant to [§2] of Addenda, the trading suspension may not 
be in effect pursuant to [§107(3)] of the previous Enforcement Rules of KOSPI Business 
Regulation.

member in the next quarter of the quarter that the effective date of  these Enforcement 
Rules falls under.

ADDENDA 
(Regulation No. 1303 / March 25, 2016) 

§1. Effective Date 

These Enforcement Rules shall become effective on March 28, 2016. Provided that the 
amended provisions of [§41-2], [§56-3] and [§3 of Annex 2-2] shall become effective on 
the  date  determined  by  the  Exchange  separately  by  taking  into  consideration  the  time 
required to develop the computer systems, etc. 

§2. Effective Date of the KOSPI Market Business Regulation, etc. 

The “date stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in Addenda of the Regulation (No.1246, 
amended on November 4, 2015) shall refer to the date specified in each of the followings: 

1. For the amended provisions of [§18] and [§20-9] through [§20-11] of the Regulation; 
March 28, 2016; and 

2.  For  the  amended  provisions  of  [§38-3]  of  the  Regulation,  the  effective  date  as 
stipulated in the proviso to [§1] of this Addenda. 

§3. Special Cases concerning the Term of Market-making Agreement 

Notwithstanding  the  amended  provisions  of  [§31-16(3)],  the  applicable  period  of  the 
market-making agreement that is entered into for the first time after the effective date of 

198 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
these Enforcement Rules shall be the period from the effective date noted in the main 
body of [§1] of this Addenda to the last trading day of the year to which the effective date 
belongs. 

§4. Interim Measures related to Market Makers 

Based on the effective date of these Enforcement Rules, selection of issues for market-
making,  reception  of  applications  for  market  makers,  conclusion  of  market-making 
agreements and other actions taken by the Exchange beforehand with respect to market 
makers for the purpose of implementation of the market maker system shall be deemed 
to have been conducted in accordance with the amended provisions. 

§5. Special Cases concerning Applicable Period of Low Liquidity Issue subject to Call 
auction 

Notwithstanding the amended provision of [§3 of Annex 2-2], the applicable period of 
the low liquidity issue subject to call auction that was selected for the first time after the 
effective date of this Enforcement shall be the period from the effective date noted in the 
proviso to [§1] of this Addenda to the last trading day of the year to which the effective 
date belongs. 

§6.  Interim  Measures  related  to  the  Selection  of  Low  Liquidity  Issue  subject  to  Call 
auction, etc. 

Notwithstanding  the  effective  dates  noted  in  the  proviso  to  [§1]  and  [§2(2)]  of  this 
Addenda, selection of low liquidity issues for call auction and other actions taken by the 
Exchange beforehand for the purpose of changing the trading method of the low liquidity 
issues into the call auction shall be deemed to have been conducted in accordance with 
the amended provisions. 

ADDENDA 
(Regulation No. 1306 / April 1, 2016) 

§1. Effective Date 

These Enforcement Rules shall become effective on April 4, 2016. 

§2. Special Cases concerning the Number of Circulating Stocks 

In  applying  the  amended  provisions  of  [§133(1)1],  until  the  stock-listed  corporation 
submits the ‘status of stock distribution’ as of the end of the business year to which the 
effective date of these Enforcement Rules belongs, the number of circulating stocks shall 
be  calculated  by  subtracting  the  number  of  circulating  stocks  held  by  the  largest 
shareholder,  etc.  from  the  number  of  circulating  stocks  stated  in  the  ‘status  of  stock 
distribution’ submitted before the effective date of these Enforcement Rules.

§2. Special Cases concerning the Timing for Calculating and Applying Assessment Rates 

Notwithstanding  the  amended  provisions  of  [§115(5)],  [§115-3(1)]  and  [§115-4(2)]  of 
these Enforcement Rules, the assessment rates of the quarter in which the effective date 
falls  shall  be  calculated  on  the  day  preceding  the  effective  date  and  applied  from  the 
effective date to the end of the quarter following the quarter in which the effective date 
falls. 

§3. Special Cases concerning Invalidation of Substitute Securities Ineligible for Member 
Margins 

Notwithstanding the amended provisions of [§99-20(1)] of these Enforcement Rules, the 
substitute  prices  for  the  substitute  securities  ineligible  for  member  margin  shall  be 
adjusted as follows:   

1. The adjustment rate shall be 25% from the effective date of these Enforcement Rules 
to September 24, 2018; and   

2. The adjustment rate shall be 50% from September 25, 2018 to September 24, 2019. 

§4. Special Cases concerning Deposit Limits per Issue of Substitute Securities 

Notwithstanding the amended provisions of [§99-21(1)] of these Enforcement Rules, the 
rates applied for calculation of deposit limits per issue or issuer of substitute securities 

203 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
shall be as follows:   

1.  In the case of subparagraph 1 of [§99-21(1)]: 100/100  from  the effective date of 
these Enforcement Rules to September 24, 2018; and 75/100 from September 25, 2018 
to  September  24,  2019.  Provided  that,  in  the  case  of  a  security  falling  under 
subparagraph 1(b) of [§112-2], it shall be 200/100 and 150/100, respectively; and   

2. In the case of subparagraphs 3 and 4 of [§99-21(1)]: 20/100 from the effective date 
of these Enforcement Rules to September 24, 2018; and 15/100 from September 25, 
2018 to September 24, 2019.

of trading securities pursuant to [§87-2(1)2] before these Enforcement Rules take effect) 
shall become effective on January 4, 2021.

provisions shall apply.
