276 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex: Form No. 2-6] Standard Agreement for Market-making in the Stock Market 
[March 25, 2016] (Amended on February 28, 2017; September 7, 2017; March 12, 2021; May 7, 2021;   
July 15, 2022; August 4, 2022; December 22, 2022) 

Standard Agreement for Market-making in the Stock Market 

The  Korea  Exchange  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  Exchange”)  and  xxx  Securities 
Company  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  market  maker”)  hereby  enter  into  a  market-
making  agreement  pursuant  to  [§20-9]  of  the  KOSPI  Market  Business  Regulation 
(hereinafter referred to as “the Regulation”) and [§31-16] of the Enforcement Rules of 
KOSPI Market Business Regulation (hereinafter referred to as “the Enforcement Rules”). 

Article 1. Purpose of agreement 
The market maker shall submit quotations or execute trades to improve the liquidity of 
stocks  or  DRs  that  were  designated  by  the  Exchange  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the 
“market-making”) and the Exchange shall make payments for the market-making of the 
market maker (hereinafter referred to as the “payments for market-making”). 

Article 2. Term of agreement 
(1) This agreement shall remain valid and in full effect during the period specified in the 
separate statement (hereinafter referred to as “the statement”) to mm/dd/yyyy. 
(2)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1),  in  cases  where  the  market-making  is  terminated 
pursuant  to  the  provisions  of  Article  9  hereof  for  each  market-making  issue  stated  in 
Article 3 hereof, the term shall end on the date of termination. 

Article 3. Market-making issue 
The market-making issue shall be a stock or DR for which the market maker shall make 
the market (hereinafter referred to as the “market-making issue”) and the starting date of 
market-making shall be as specified in the statement. 

Article 4. Obligations of market maker 
(1) The market maker shall report one (1) account that is exclusively for market-making 
to the Exchange (hereinafter referred to as the  “market-making account”) according to 
the method stipulated by the Regulation, etc., and the market-making shall be carried out 
through this account. In such case, when a market maker submits quotations through the 
relevant account, it shall not input anything other than matters in each of the following 
Subparagraphs: 

1. Type of account: [11] Market-making account 

2. Type of market-making quotation: 2 

(2) The market maker shall designate two (2) or more officers and employees who will 
be responsible for market-making and report to the Exchange. 
(3) The market maker shall continuously submit and maintain market-making quotations 
that satisfy the conditions specified in [§31-12] of the Enforcement Rules for the market-

277 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
making  issues  during  throughout  the  term  of  agreement.  In  such  cases,  the  method  of 
submission of quotations for the fulfillment of obligations - the obligatory spreads, the 
minimum quotation size, etc. - shall be as stipulated in the statement. 
(4)  The  market  maker  shall  have  an  internal  control  system  that  allows  to  submit 
quotations only in  the case when the relevant  listed stocks are borrowed if the market 
maker intends to submit the quotations for covered short sales noted in [§17(2)] of the 
Regulation. 
(5) The market maker shall report to the Exchange as a high-speed algorithmic trader in 
advance. In the case where the market maker submits the quotations for the fulfillment of 
obligations,  it  shall  affix  the  self-match  prevention  condition  under  [§13-2]  of  the 
Enforcement Rules to the quotations, except in unavoidable cases. 
(6) The market maker shall complete the training programs on the prevention of unfair 
trading provided by the Exchange after entering into the market-making agreement. 
(7) The market  maker may not  transfer or  entrust  the rights  and obligations under the 
market-making agreement to a third party without a prior written consent of the Exchange. 

Article 5. Assessment of market-making performance 
The  Exchange  shall  make  assessment  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “market-making 
assessment”)  of  whether  or  not  the  market  maker  has  fulfilled  the  market-making 
obligation stated in Article 4 hereof during the quarter for assessment (hereinafter referred 
to as the “assessment quarter”) on a quarterly basis and notify the market maker of the 
result in written form by the time for making the payments for market-making specified 
in Article 7hereof after the end of assessment quarter. Provided that, in cases where the 
number of market-making days during the assessment quarter (referring to the number of 
market-making days specified in the “guidelines for assessment of market makers and 
making payments for market-making” of [Annex 2-4] of the Enforcement Rules; the same 
shall apply hereinafter) is less than five (5) days, the market-making assessment may not 
take place. 

Article 6. Suspension of qualification of the market maker 
In cases where the market maker, according to the result of assessment of market-making 
performance conducted pursuant Article 5 hereof, has failed to perform its market-making 
obligations faithfully and consequently falls under the criteria specified in [§31-21] of the 
Enforcement Rules , the Exchange shall suspend the qualification of the market maker. 

Article 7. Payments for market-making 
(1) Based on the result of the assessment of market-making performance of the market 
maker conducted pursuant to Article 5 hereof, the Exchange may make  a payment for 
market-making  for  the  market-making  issue  for  which  market-making  obligation  was 
faithfully fulfilled. 
(2)The guidelines for payment, calculation of amount and time for making, etc. of the 
payments  for  market-making  mentioned  in  paragraph  (1)  shall  be  as  specified  in  the 
“guidelines for assessment of market makers and making payments for market-making” 
in [Annex 2-4] of the Enforcement Rules that are set by the Exchange, unless otherwise 
stipulated in this Agreement. 

278 

 
 
 
 
 
Article 8. Exception to making the payments for market-making   
(1) Notwithstanding Article 7 hereof, the Exchange may not pay all or a part of payments 
for market-making for the relevant quarter to the market maker in case of falling under 
any of the following subparagraphs: 

1. Case where the market-making assessment stipulated in Article 5 hereof has not been 
conducted; 
2.  Case  of  falling  under  any  of  subparagraphs  2  through  5  under  paragraph  (1)  of 
Article 11; and 
3.  Case  where  the  market  maker  who  intends  to  terminate  the  market-making 
agreement pursuant to paragraph (2) of Article 11 hereof has not fully performed the 
explanation obligations. 

(2) In cases when the Exchange has decided not to make the payments for market-making 
wholly or partially pursuant to paragraph (1) hereof, the Exchange shall notify the market 
maker in writing of the decision on and the reasons for the non-payment. 

Article 9. Termination of market-making   
(1) In cases where a market-making issue falls under any of the following subparagraphs, 
the market-making by the market maker for the relevant issue shall be terminated. 

1. Case where the average daily turnover ratio (excluding the last  seven (7) trading 
days  of  each  quarter)  is  assessed  every  quarter  pursuant  to  [§31-16(3)1]  of  the 
Enforcement Rules, and it exceeds 15% for two (2) consecutive quarters. In such cases, 
the market-making for the relevant issue shall terminate at the end of the concerned 
quarter; 
2. Case where the relevant issue is delisted; 
3. Case where the liquidity provision agreement pursuant to [20-3] of the Regulation 
was concluded and is in force; and 
4. Other cases that the Exchange deems necessary for market management. 

(2) In cases where any of the causes specified in each of followings has occurred to a 
market-making issue, the market maker may request the Exchange for the termination of 
market-making for the relevant issue: 

1. Case where a resolution on being merged into another corporation or delisting was 
made; 
2. Case where a resolution on spin-off was made; 
3. Case where a resolution on merger, stock swap, business takeover, asset takeover, 
investment-in-kind, etc. noted in [§32] of the KOSPI Market Listing Regulation was 
made; 
4. Case where the cause for review on listing maintenance eligibility has occurred; and 
5.  Other  reasons  equivalent  to  subparagraphs  1  through  4  hereof  that  may  cause  a 
significant change in the corporate entity of the market-making issue or a significant 
effect on the sustainability of listing have occurred. 

(3) When requesting for the termination of market-making pursuant to paragraph (2), the 
market  maker shall make a written notice which states the cause of termination to the 
Exchange, and the date of termination shall be the day  immediately following the day 
when the Exchange has made the decision on the termination of the market-making. 

Article 10. Suspension of market-making   

279 

 
 
 
In  cases  where  a  market-making  issue  falls  under  any  of  the  followings,  the  market-
making of the relevant issue by the market maker in charge shall be suspended during the 
periods specified in each of the followings: 

1.  The  period  from  the  time  when  the  cause  for  delisting  occurred  to  the  time  of 
delisting; 
2.  The  period  of  time  during  which  the  issue  shall  remain  designated  as  an 
administrative issue; and 
3. [Deleted on March 12, 2021] 

Article 11. Termination of agreement, etc. 
(1) The Exchange may terminate the market-making agreement with the market maker if 
any of the following subparagraphs occurs: 

1.  Case  where  it  becomes  impossible  to  perform  the  market-making  or  securities 
trading due to the bankruptcy, business suspension, revoked authorization, withdrawal 
from membership, etc. of the market maker; 
2. In cases where the market maker significantly undermines legal order by such acts 
as breaching the laws and regulations relating to the payment of securities transaction 
taxes by intention or gross negligence and commits the acts falling under any of the 
following cases: 

(a)  Case  where  the  market  maker  trades  non-market-making  issues  through  the 
market-making accounts; and 
(b)  Case  where  the  market  maker  has  been  subject  to  sanctions  from  the  tax 
authorities due to any untruthful reports on market-making. 

3. In cases where market maker has been subject to sanctions equivalent to or heavier 
than  penalty  surcharge  from  the  Financial  Services  Commission  or  member  fine 
(limited to a fine amounting to KRW 10 million or more) from the Exchange for unfair 
trading, etc. with respect to market-making tasks related to stocks (referring to market-
making tasks for stocks in the KOSPI and KOSDAQ markets and equity derivatives in 
the derivatives market); 
4. In cases where the market maker has violated the confidentiality obligation stipulated 
in Article 14 hereof. Provided that this provision shall not apply to the case when the 
market maker provides documents to the tax authorities to obtain the exemption from 
the  securities  transaction  tax  in  accordance  with  Paragraph(1)3of  Article  117of  the 
Restriction of Special Taxation Act; 
5. In cases where the market maker has refused or made a false, delayed or understated 
report with respect to the request or demand made by the Exchange pursuant to Article 
15 hereof or the matters to be reported, without any extraordinary circumstances; 
6.  In  cases  where  the  market  maker  falls  under  the  causes  for  the  suspension  of 
qualification noted in Article 6 hereof;   
7.  In  cases  where  the  market  maker  has  transferred  or  entrusted  the  rights  and 
obligations under the market-making agreement to a third party without an approval 
from the Exchange;   
8. In cases where the market maker has continuously failed to respond to or made a 
false or understated report with respect to any request, demand or report made by the 
Exchange in relation to the market maker’s violation of obligations under Paragraph 4 ; 
and 

280 

 
 
9.  Other  cases  where  it  is  deemed  inappropriate  to  maintain  the  market  marking 
agreement with the market maker. 

(2)  In  cases  where  it  is  deemed  difficult  to  perform  the  market-making  tasks  due  to  a 
significant change in the contents of the agreement, internal affairs, etc., the market maker 
may terminate this agreement in consultation with the Exchange. In such cases, the market 
maker shall explain faithfully the reasons why it is difficult to conduct the market-making 
to the Exchange. 
(3) When intending to terminate this agreement pursuant to paragraph (1), the Exchange 
shall notify the market maker of the cause of termination, termination date, etc. in writing 
no later than five (5) trading days before the termination date. 
(4)  When  intending  to  terminate  this  agreement  pursuant  to  paragraph(2),  the  market 
maker shall notify the Exchange of the cause of termination in writing no later than the 
last trading day of the first month of a quarter. In such cases, the termination of agreement 
shall  be  effective  from  the  first  day  of  the  quarter  following  the  quarter  to  which  the 
notification date belongs. 
(5) The market maker shall inform the Exchange without delay when any of the causes 
noted in subparagraphs 1 through 3 of paragraph (1) occurs. 

Article 12. Change in agreement etc. 
The  Exchange  and  the  market  maker  may  change  the  contents  of  the  market-making 
agreement by mutual consultation even during the term of agreement. 

Article 13. Disclosure of market-making details 
The Exchange may disclose all market makers’ trading volume, covered short sale size 
and performance of implementing obligations pursuant to Article 4 hereof on a quarterly 
basis on the website of the Exchange. 

Article 14. Confidentiality obligation, etc. 
The market maker shall not disclose the material contents of this agreement to any party 
or to the public without prior consent from the Exchange. 

Article 15. Request for change of market-making staff 
(1)  In  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  is  inappropriate  for  a  market-making  staff 
designated  by  the  market  maker,  taking  the  expertise,  morality,  etc.  into  account,  to 
perform the market-making tasks, the Exchange may request the market maker for the 
change of the  relevant  market-making staff  pursuant  to  the  regulation,  and the market 
maker shall faithfully comply with such request for the change of staff-in-charge unless 
there exist extraordinary circumstances otherwise.   
(2) The Exchange may request for documents or demand cooperation in business to the 
market  maker  in  case  when  it  is  necessary  for  the  effective  implementation  of  this 
agreement, and the market maker shall faithfully comply with such request or demand 
unless there exist extraordinary circumstances otherwise. 
(3) The market maker shall take necessary actions for the Exchange in making inquiries 
into details of trades through the market-making account in order to conduct businesses 
relating to the market-making or the exemption from securities transaction tax. 

281 

 
 
 
 
 
(4) In case of having been sanctioned by the tax authorities in relation with the payments 
of securities transaction  tax, the market  maker  shall  make a  report on such fact  to  the 
Exchange without delay. 

Article 16. Exemption from liability 
The  market  maker  has  no  right  to  make  an  objection  or  claim  damages  against  the 
Exchange in cases where the Exchange makes changes to the market-making system and 
takes other related actions in accordance with the Act, Enforcement Decree, Regulations 
and Enforcement Rules relating to the securities trade. 

Article 17. Application of Regulation 
Other  matters  which  are  not  stipulated  in  this  agreement  shall  comply  with  the 
Regulations and Enforcement Rules of the Exchange. 

We, the Exchange and the Company, hereby sign and affix our seals on two copies of the 
Agreement and keep one copy each as a proof of entering into the Agreement.

287 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex: Form No.4] Agreement for Correction of Transaction Errors 
(Amended on February 3, 2009) 

Agreement for Correction of Transaction Errors 

The  Korea  Exchange  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  "the  Exchange")  and  xx  Securities 

Company,  Ltd.,  who  is  a  member  of  the  Exchange  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  "the 

Company") agree on the following terms and conditions for the correction of error made 

by the Exchange in the course of executing the trade in the KOSPI Market and the errors 

occurred due to the failures of the Exchange computer system (hereinafter referred to as 

"the transaction errors").   

Article 1.In cases where a transaction error occurs during the course of execution of trades 

by the Exchange, the company shall take over such transaction error as an issue traded 

through the self-account upon receiving the request from the Exchange (see Attachment 

1: Request for correction of transaction error). 

Article 2.The Company shall trade the issue assumed upon receipt of the request from the 

Exchange  by  the  way  of  reverse  trading  of  which  the  quotation  participates  in  the 

determination of the opening price on the following day. Provided that, when, due to an 

unavoidable  reason  such  as  the  failure  of  the  Exchange  computer  system,  placing  a 

quotation  participating  in  determination  of  the  opening  price  was  not  possible,  the 

assumed securities shall be traded by way of reverse trading (except in the case of bonds) 

of which the quotation participates in the determination of the closing price. The results 

of such reverse trading (see Attachment 2. Notification of Results of Trading Transaction 

Errors)  shall  be  reported  to  the  Exchange  without  delay.  In  cases  where  the  assumed 
transaction errors are not cleared by the reverse trade on the following day, they shall be 

traded by the same method on the next trading day repeatedly.   

Article 3.The Exchange shall settle the profits and losses (includes the transaction tax, all 

expenses  incidental  to  such  transaction  and  the  dues  of  the  relevant  member)  resulted 

from the assuming and trading the transaction error as requested by the  Company (see 

Attachment  3.  Request  for  Settlement  for  Handling  Transaction  Error)  without  delay. 

Provided that any profits and losses resulted from the error made by the Company in the 

288 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
course of handling the assumed transaction error, shall be settled after the fact according 

to the request by the Exchange (see Attachment 4. Request for Settlement Adjustment for 

Handling Transaction Errors).   

Article 4.In cases where the issue assumed by the Company undergoes ex-rights or ex-

dividend, if there is any difference in the opinions on the methods of clearing the gains or 

losses incurred, including any other matters that are not stipulated in this agreement, such 

differences shall be resolved through the consultation and mutual agreement between the 

Exchange and the Company. 

Article  5.This  agreement  shall  be  valid  for  one  (1)  year  from  the  date  of  signing,  and 

unless any objection on the terms and conditions of this agreement is expressed at least 

thirty (30) days prior to the expiry date, it shall be deemed that an agreement with the 
same terms and conditions as the one expired has been signed on its expiry date.   

We,  the  Exchange  and  the  Company,  hereby  agree  the  above-mentioned  terms  and 

conditions, sign and affix our seals on two copies of the Agreement and keep one copy 

each as a proof of entering into the agreement. 

Date: mm/dd/yyyy 

For and on behalf of the Korea Exchange:    _________________________   

Chairperson& CEO of the Korea Exchange   

For and on behalf of the Company: _________________________   

Representative   

xxx Securities Company
